# Proxies | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FF9Z2v64CZtqcXa7GicfV%252F1%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3f4411d&sv=2)

[Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/zMKjd6kBzj)
 is a leading provider of high quality proxies tailored for botting retail products, web scraping and other online activities requiring anonymity and reliability. These proxies are designed to offer top notch performance and ensure seamless browsing experiences across various platforms. Whether you're a botter looking to cop the latest releases or a web scraper in need of reliable IP addresses, Stella Proxies has you covered.

[Stella Proxies Websitearrow-up-right](https://www.stellaproxies.com/)

[Stella Proxies Twitterarrow-up-right](https://twitter.com/StellaProxies)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#what-are-proxies)

**What Are Proxies?**

A proxy is an intermediary IP address that sits between you (or the bot) and a website. Instead of your real IP address connecting directly to a site like Walmart, Target, or Shopify, the proxy does it for you.

In botting and automation, proxies are used to:

*   Hide your real IP address
    
*   Prevent bans and rate limits
    
*   Run multiple tasks simultaneously
    
*   Appear as multiple unique users to a website
    
*   Bypass IP-based restrictions and throttling
    

Without proxies, most retail sites would instantly block or heavily limit automated activity.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#proxy-types-explained)

**Proxy Types Explained**

Stella Proxies offers multiple proxy types, each serving a different purpose. Choosing the right type for the right task is critical for success.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#isp-proxies-internet-service-provider-proxies)

**ISP Proxies (Internet Service Provider Proxies)**

**What they are:** ISP proxies are static IPs hosted in data centers but registered under real internet service providers. This gives them the speed of data center proxies with the trust level of residential IPs.

**Key characteristics:**

*   Extremely fast and stable
    
*   Static (IP does not change unless rotated manually)
    
*   Appear as real household internet connections
    
*   Very low ban rate compared to normal DC proxies
    

**Best used for:**

*   Monitoring tasks
    
*   Long-running tasks
    
*   Account-based sites (Target, Walmart, Amazon, Best Buy)
    
*   Situations where stability matters more than rotation
    

**Pros:**

*   Fast checkout speeds
    
*   Excellent reliability
    
*   Lower chance of bans than DCs
    

**Cons:**

*   More expensive than DC proxies
    
*   Limited IP rotation compared to residentials
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#residential-proxies-resi)

**Residential Proxies (Resi)**

**What they are:** Residential proxies use real IP addresses assigned to actual household devices through internet service providers.

**Key characteristics:**

*   Rotating IPs
    
*   Highest trust level
    
*   Appear exactly like real users
    
*   Hardest for sites to detect or ban
    

**Best used for:**

*   Checkout tasks
    
*   Queue-based sites
    
*   PX / Akamai protected sites
    
*   Aggressive actions like ATC spam or forced checkout
    

**Pros:**

*   Very hard to detect
    
*   Excellent for bypassing anti-bot systems
    
*   Ideal for checkout and queue passing
    

**Cons:**

*   Uses data (GB-based pricing)
    
*   Slower than ISP/DC proxies
    
*   Can be expensive if misused
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#datacenter-proxies-dc)

**Datacenter Proxies (DC)**

**What they are:** Datacenter proxies are IPs hosted entirely in data centers and not associated with residential ISPs.

**Key characteristics:**

*   Very fast
    
*   Cheap
    
*   Easily identifiable as datacenter traffic
    

**Best used for:**

*   Low-protection sites
    
*   Shopify monitoring
    
*   Speed-focused tasks where bans are less strict
    

**Pros:**

*   Fast
    
*   Affordable
    
*   Good for light monitoring
    

**Cons:**

*   High ban rate on major retailers
    
*   Not recommended for strict sites like Walmart, Target, or Amazon
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#which-proxy-type-should-i-use)

**Which Proxy Type Should I Use?**

A general rule of thumb for Stellar users:

*   **Monitoring → ISP Proxies**
    
*   **Checkout → Residential Proxies**
    
*   **Low-protection Shopify sites → DC or ISP Proxies**
    
*   **Queue-heavy or PX-protected sites → Residential Proxies**
    

Many successful setups use **a mix of ISP + Residential proxies** to balance speed, cost, and reliability.

* * *

Stella Proxies proxy network consists of both ISP and residential proxies, ensuring a diverse range of IP addresses to suit your specific needs. With Stella Proxies, you can enjoy fast and stable connections, bypass geo-restrictions and maintain anonymity while browsing online. Additionally, they regularly offer discounts and promotions to provide users with cost-effective solutions for their proxy needs.

circle-exclamation

 for more provider recommendations

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#proxy-to-task-ratio-how-many-proxies-do-i-need)

Proxy-to-Task Ratio (How Many Proxies Do I Need?)

One of the most common questions is: **“How many proxies do I need to run my tasks?”** The answer depends on the **type of proxy** you’re using and **how aggressive the site is**, but there’s a simple rule of thumb to start with.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#the-basic-rule-of-thumb)

The Basic Rule of Thumb

**1:1 proxy-to-task ratio (minimum)**

This means:

*   1 proxy per 1 task
    
*   Example:
    
    *   25 ISP proxies → safely run ~25 tasks
        
    *   50 ISP proxies → safely run ~50 tasks
        
    

This is the **bare minimum** and works best on:

*   Lower protection sites
    
*   Short restocks
    
*   Light monitoring
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#recommended-ratio-better-and-safer)

Recommended Ratio (Better & Safer)

**2:1 or higher proxy-to-task ratio (recommended)**

This means:

*   2 proxies per 1 task (or more)
    
*   Example:
    
    *   50 proxies → 25 tasks
        
    *   100 proxies → 50 tasks
        
    

Why this is better:

*   Allows proxy rotation if some IPs get flagged
    
*   Reduces bans, soft blocks, and captchas
    
*   Improves task stability during longer runs
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#how-proxy-type-changes-the-ratio)

How Proxy Type Changes the Ratio

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#isp-proxies)

ISP Proxies

ISP proxies are usually:

*   **Purchased in fixed quantities** (10, 25, 50, etc.)
    
*   **Static IPs** (they don’t rotate automatically)
    

Because of this:

*   You’re limited by how many you bought
    
*   You should be more conservative with task counts
    

**Recommended ISP usage**

*   Monitoring: 1:1 or 2:1
    
*   Checkout: 1:1 (or lower task count if site is strict)
    

Example:

*   25 ISPs →
    
    *   25 monitor tasks (max)
        
    *   Or ~15–20 checkout tasks for safer operation
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#residential-proxies-resis)

Residential Proxies (Resis)

Residential proxies are different:

*   They rotate automatically
    
*   You can generate **hundreds or thousands of unique IPs**
    
*   You’re limited by **data (GB)**, not IP count
    

Because of this:

*   You can safely run **far more tasks**
    
*   Perfect for:
    
    *   Checkout tasks
        
    *   Queue sites
        
    *   Aggressive ATC spam
        
    

**Recommended Residential usage**

*   Monitoring: 5–10 tasks per proxy pool is common
    
*   Checkout: scale based on data usage, not IP count
    

Example:

*   2–5 GB of residential data can support:
    
    *   Dozens of checkout tasks
        
    *   Hundreds of short-lived tasks if tuned properly
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#mixing-proxies-best-practice)

Mixing Proxies (Best Practice)

Most successful setups use **both**:

*   **ISP proxies**
    
    *   Monitoring
        
    *   Long-running tasks
        
    *   Account-based logins
        
    
*   **Residential proxies**
    
    *   Checkout
        
    *   Queue passing
        
    *   ATC spam
        
    

This lets you:

*   Save residential data
    
*   Keep costs down
    
*   Reduce bans
    
*   Scale safely
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#beginner-mistakes-to-avoid)

Beginner Mistakes to Avoid

*   Running more tasks than proxies (especially with ISPs)
    
*   Using the same proxy pool for everything
    
*   Ignoring proxy quality and only focusing on quantity
    
*   Forgetting that long-running tasks consume more resources
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#simple-starter-recommendations)

Simple Starter Recommendations

If you’re new, start here:

*   **ISPs**
    
    *   1 proxy per task (minimum)
        
    *   Don’t exceed what you purchased
        
    
*   **Residentials**
    
    *   Start small
        
    *   Increase tasks gradually
        
    *   Monitor data usage closely
        
    
*   **When in doubt**
    
    *   Fewer, cleaner tasks > more aggressive spam
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies#final-takeaway)

Final Takeaway

*   **1:1 proxy-to-task** is the minimum
    
*   **2:1 or higher** is safer and more stable
    
*   **ISPs = limited by quantity**
    
*   **Residentials = limited by data, not IPs**
    
*   Scaling smart beats scaling fast

# Getting Started with StellarAIO | Stellar

So you just got Stellar and don't know where to start? You're in the right place! We will let you know step by step on how to get started with StellarAIO

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar#what-is-stellar)

What is Stellar?

Stellar AIO is an all in one retail automation software built to help members purchase high demand products from major retailers at retail price. Our goal is to simplify the process of securing items like trading cards, collectibles, consoles, GPUs, toys and more so users can either keep or resell them

We support dozens of major retailers including Amazon, Walmart, Target, Best Buy, Pokémon Center, and many others with built in features like serverside monitoring, automatic checkout and real time Discord support

At Stellar, we focus on retail automation and restock monitoring, we are not a cook group. We do not offer product information, resale predictions or financial advice

Whether you’re just starting out or already experienced in the game, Stellar is built to be beginner friendly, powerful and always improving

If you're new here, the rest of this guide will walk you through how to install, set up and get the most out of Stellar

**We also have all the guides referenced in the step by step instructions below!**

*   Download Stellar [Windows](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_d523604013)
     or [Mac](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_6126dd8c70)
    
*   You're going to need to grab your license key from our [Stellar Whop pagearrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio/license-key-management-JVLVXWY5PXkmM2/app/)
     copy your key and paste it into Stellar
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCUznfLih39dDAx53Ze6S%252F3.0verifyinglicense.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0155f81e-92b7-498e-9a31-b2576b542b78&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5ebc7cea&sv=2)

*   Now it's time to start setting up your Stellar [settings](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab)
    ! It's very important to go through the settings tab and enter any information you can. For example, we highly recommend setting up your [Discord Webhook](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-to-set-up-discord-notifications)
     so you're notified when Stellar successfully checked out and other notifications
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FVPRhvTOatE81nHPvwfg3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db101810c-706a-4ab2-893c-0306977e0060&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1831069d&sv=2)

*   Setup your [Captcha Harvester/Solver](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
     so you'll be able to solve Captchas manually if needed. For example, some modules like Pokemon Center require you to solve some Captchas manually and you'll need Google Chrome installed on your PC
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fy2PshWqCiWvwXZ418U1e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38417c9e-c1da-4b4f-8dfa-86a1669aed7f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78aea589&sv=2)

*   Setup your [Sessions](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/how-do-i-add-a-session-or-mass-import-sessions)
     so you'll be able to stay logged into your accounts for a longer period of time and less errors going forward. Setup your Accounts so you'll have all of your emails and passwords to each account readily accessible. Some modules like Walmart have items that you'll need an account to purchase and is less likely for your orders to get canceled if you use an account
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FnESw9svIfTyqqsABGQlD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc284c5b0-982d-4e9e-841e-615e0a8c99ab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5a23f9f&sv=2)

*   Setup your [Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab/how-do-i-add-proxies)
     (proxies are required) so you're able to mask your local/server IP and you'll be able to monitor and checkout multiple items. Having multiple proxy groups (ISPs, DCs and Resis) is recommended so if you're having issues with one group then you can use another as your backup
    
    *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FZLmCd9Pk4BpEIncs4n34%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D099ab411-3ff9-41e9-ac6a-223a5ccbb2b3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a16027ef&sv=2)

*   Setup your [Profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
     so all of your personal information (billing, shipping and payment information) is saved in Stellar. Each checkout task is tied to a certain profile so make sure you're choosing wisely or you may receive shipping/payment issues
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FU10WD7wo5RyMgMZtvmwM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91614dd3-cf87-4331-bcdd-55cc36ba65f9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b29fbd9&sv=2)

*   Setup your [Tasks](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tasks-tab)
     there is where you will be able to monitor and checkout items! It's very important when creating tasks to know what all of the fields and checkboxes mean. If you're ever unsure what a field is then you can go to that actual modules guide where all of the fields are explained there. For example, if you're unsure what each mode does you can go to the [Target](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/targetgo)
     and there's a breakdown
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCMYro9LmZOAFwPKBEF2s%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De57c08cc-5880-4549-9283-4bcdcbc26488&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e10bdf97&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar#important-notes)

Important Notes:

*   We always recommend to be on the latest version of Stellar. There are always stability and antibot improvements on the later versions
    
*   Take full advantage of the StellarAIO Guide, it's constantly updated and has very general baseline setups for most major sites
    
*   Proxies are required to run Stellar
    
    *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    
*   You may find it beneficial to join a [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
    , this group will supply you with everything you need to know when botting. They provide product information, upcoming releases, early access links, passwords for sites and many other benefits
    

[NextProxieschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)

# How Do I Access and Manage My Account? | Stellar

**What is the StellarAIO Dashboard?** [https://whop.com/stellaraio/arrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio/)
 **How to Access and Manage My Account/Key?** Your key and all things renewal are all found on the StellarAIO Dashboard through Whop! 1. **Navigate to** [https://whop.com/stellaraio/arrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio/)
 into a browser of your choice and login with the respective Discord linked to your StellarAIO key (Click the blue "Continue with Discord" button)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FDWvjrVeJDBZwiBCZDcjX%252Fwhop.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1f79678-6498-4c6a-bb8f-c9cfbc32f5a4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ad60c18&sv=2)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FZwfCjVFmre2tj6VkslhQ%252Fsigninwhop.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De47f3ef3-abff-433d-b538-fd258ce84418&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95c7ad19&sv=2)

3\. Once you login with your Discord, you'll have access to:

*   View your Stellar key
    
*   The purchase price of the key
    
*   The monthly renewal price
    
*   The status of your key
    
*   The next renewal date
    
*   Your Discord username
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FnJgN0iRcirDLykWvYVJG%252Fwhopdashboard.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D714df6a0-f880-4da1-9433-ab19993eb716&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8bbd4f2e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/how-do-i-access-and-manage-my-account#h_efb0a10f16)

**How do I add a payment method for renewal fees?**

1\. **Navigate to** [**https://whop.com/stellaraio/**arrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio/)
 into a browser of your choice

2\. Click the **Update Payment Method** option

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FsP4AN5WzvzrumHeGs1uS%252Fupdatepayment.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47c0f668-bcf8-4824-9264-ed8f655bd04d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f9b81d14&sv=2)

4\. Update payment method

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/how-do-i-access-and-manage-my-account#h_916571401b)

**How do I reset my key?**

1\. **Navigate to** [**https://whop.com/stellaraio/**arrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio/)
 into a browser of your choice and sign in with your Discord account

2\. Go to Tools tab

3\. Click on Stellar AIO

4\. Now you can view your license key(s) and there'll be three dots button next to your key(s)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FRLDqRnWxIktiswypVP9L%252Fnewwhoplocatekey.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cfb7ceb-ea5b-4682-85e1-e5ea5d3287ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2f85d271&sv=2)

5\. Click on the three dots button and click Reset

# Support - Need Help? | Stellar

Whether you're just getting started or need help troubleshooting, **we’ve got multiple support options available to assist you every step of the way.** Here's how to get the help you need:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/support-need-help#discord-support-tickets)

💬 Discord Support Tickets

Our **Discord server** is the best place to receive fast, direct support from the Stellar team.

*   **Support Ticket** – For help with tasks, setup recommendations, errors or anything related to using the bot.
    
*   **Admin Ticket** – For billing, license key issues, or anything account related.
    

> To open a ticket, head to the [**#open-ticket**arrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417909247756468396)
>  channel in our Discord and select the ticket type that fits your need.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/support-need-help#weekly-group-voice-calls)

🎙️ Weekly Group Voice Calls

We host **free weekly group voice calls** in our Discord server where you can ask live questions, get setup advice and hear tips directly from the Stellar team and community.

> Check the recent messages in [**#weekly-support-calls**arrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1419803263179423844)
>  for the next scheduled session.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/support-need-help#id-1-on-1-call-w-stellar-expert)

👤 1-on-1 Call w/ Stellar Expert

Need personalized help?

*   **Free 1-on-1 calls** are available to paid members during special windows or promotions.
    
*   **Paid 1-on-1 calls** can be scheduled anytime with a Stellar expert to walk you through setup, troubleshooting, or advanced strategies.
    

> Visit our [Calendy websitearrow-up-right](https://calendly.com/d/crgd-hyb-ybx)
>  or the [**Whop dashboard**arrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio)
>  to book a session

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/support-need-help#ask-in-questions)

❓ Ask in #questions

For quick help, you can always post in the [**#questions**arrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417584359967428669)
 channel in our Discord. Both our support team and experienced users are active and ready to assist.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/support-need-help#were-here-to-help)

We're Here to Help

No matter your issue or experience level, Stellar’s support system is designed to make sure you're never stuck. If you're unsure where to start, **open a support ticket and we’ll point you in the right direction.**

# Cook Groups | Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups#whats-a-cookgroup)

What's a Cookgroup?

A cook group is a community, usually on Discord, that provides members with valuable resources for reselling and botting. This includes things like release info, restock alerts, early links, site monitors, bot setups, proxy recommendations and more. Essentially, it's a hub where people share knowledge and tools to increase success in buying limited items

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups#divine-x-stellaraio-partnership)

# Botting Terminology | Stellar

A reference for common terms in botting, reselling and automation.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/botting-terminology#core-botting-terms)

Core Botting Terms

*   **AIO (All-In-One Bot)** – A bot that supports multiple retailers (e.g., Stellar AIO supports Amazon, Best Buy, Walmart, Target, Shopify, Pokémon Center and more).
    
*   **Add to Cart (ATC)** – The step of getting an item into your cart. Success here is required before checkout.
    
*   **Task** – A single job your bot runs to monitor, ATC and checkout a product. Each task typically uses a profile, proxy and account.
    
*   **Delay** – The speed at which tasks check a site. Includes _Monitor Delay_ (checking for products) and _Retry Delay_ (how often it retries actions after errors).
    
*   **Token** – A digital pass/signature used on some sites (like Target) to confirm your session and allow checkout.
    
*   **Serverside Monitoring** – A method of detecting product changes directly from server data instead of local page refreshes, reducing proxy usage and increasing efficiency.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/botting-terminology#success-and-community)

Success & Community

*   **Cop** – Successfully purchasing an item (e.g., “Copped 3 pairs”).
    
*   **Brick** – An item with little to no resale value (resells at or below retail).
    
*   **Cook Group** – A Discord community providing resources, alerts, links and tools to help with botting/reselling.
    
*   **Slot** – A service where someone else runs their bot for you using your details, charging a Pay After Success (PAS) fee.
    
*   **Group Buy (GB)** – A special deal on bots, proxies, or tools offered within a community.
    
*   **WTB/WTS/WTT** – Marketplace abbreviations: Want to Buy / Want to Sell / Want to Trade.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/botting-terminology#anti-bot-and-protection)

Anti-Bot & Protection

*   **Captcha** – A challenge like “I’m not a robot” or image puzzles used to block bots. Some bots integrate captcha solvers.
    
*   **Bypass** – A method or module that skips queues, captchas, or other bot protection systems.
    
*   **Passthrough** – Allows tasks to bypass waiting rooms and directly access the product page.
    
*   **Spoofing** – Masking requests to look more human by faking browser/device details.
    
*   **Clipped** – When a method/module has been patched and no longer works.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/botting-terminology#proxies)

Proxies

*   **Proxies** – IP addresses used to mask activity and prevent bans. Categories include:
    
    *   **DC Proxies (Datacenter)** – Fast and cheap, but easily detected. Used on sites with lighter protection.
        
    *   **ISP Proxies** – Residential ISPs with static IPs, great for stability and high-protection sites like Best Buy or Target.
        
    *   **Residential Proxies (Resi)** – Rotate through real home IPs, more stealthy but data-based (sold in GBs). Ideal for Shopify, Pokémon Center, etc.
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/botting-terminology#retail-and-product-info)

Retail & Product Info

*   **Early Link (EL)** – A direct product link before public release/search visibility.
    
*   **Keywords (KWs)** – Search filters for bots (e.g., `+jordan,+4,-kids,-toddler`).
    
*   **OOS (Out of Stock)** – Item is no longer available.
    
*   **SKU** – Stock Keeping Unit, a code tied to a specific size or product variant.
    
*   **Sitelist** – A bot’s supported site list/modules.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/botting-terminology#servers-and-infrastructure)

Servers & Infrastructure

*   **Server (or RDP)** – A virtual machine hosted in a data center to run bots 24/7 with low latency.
    
*   **AWS (Amazon Web Services)** – Popular server provider.
    
*   **GCS (Google Cloud Services)** – Another server provider.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/botting-terminology#newer-modern-terms)

Newer/Modern Terms

*   **Queue-It** – A virtual waiting room system used by retailers to throttle traffic.
    
*   **Throttling** – When sites slow or block bot activity due to high requests.
    
*   **Checkpoint** – An extra verification challenge (common on Shopify) that tasks must solve before checkout.
    
*   **Rate Limit** – Error when too many requests are sent in a short time.
    
*   **FlareSolverr / Solver Services** – Tools/services integrated into bots to handle advanced anti-bot challenges.
    

[PreviousCook Groupschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
[NextSupport - Need Help?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/support-need-help)

# How do I update Stellar? (PC and Mac) | Stellar

Stellar will automatically attempt to update when StellarAIO is open. If there's any issues updating Stellar to the latest version you can download manually by visiting the [#change-logarrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417581765295472830)
 channel

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLnxOMU0jT3wTBkMmZtOp%252Fautoupdate3.0.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5c831f1-c851-4177-9367-cec2e9423546&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7744a48&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-update-stellar-pc-and-mac#manually-download-stellar-from-the-latest-change-log-post)

**Manually download Stellar from the latest** [**#change-log**arrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417581765295472830)
 **post**

If you cant see the channel above then you don't have the permissions to view it. You'll need to bind your Discord account to your Stellar key if you own it. If you don't own Stellar and are renting, you'll have to get latest download links from the person you're renting Stellar from

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLW2ZZDA1BWy1NqKydf6H%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2810096d-f2b4-4674-8c9b-9f5dcb45e776&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f307fd2&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

If you're on Mac, make sure you download the correct option. MacOS Intel or MacOS Silicon. You can check which one you can download in your Mac settings.

# Servers | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FHhHZb2SUJt7h4XhO7tmd%252Fcontainer_virtual-machine_530x330.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65ec6381-5d66-40c5-a141-3e93501bc289&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74065dcd&sv=2)

If you’re new to botting, you’ve probably heard about using a **server** but you might not know exactly what it is or if you need one. This guide will break it down in simple terms, explain the pros and cons and why Stellar recommends using servers from our trusted partner [**Stella Proxies**](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/servers#what-is-a-server)

**What is a Server?**

A **server** is essentially a powerful computer that you access remotely. Instead of running your bot from your home computer, you can rent a server to run your bot in a data center. These data centers are located in strategic locations with high speed internet connections and optimized hardware.

When you use a server, you can connect to it from anywhere using software like Remote Desktop Protocol (RDP). Once connected, it looks and works just like a normal computer desktop.

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FNBZbsiCHr5WBonwm9AdH%252Fstellaproxies.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcff647b9-5ebe-4791-a321-90d5224af80a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9335d6b&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/servers#why-use-a-server-for-botting)

**Why Use a Server for Botting?**

**Pros**

1.  **Faster Speeds** Servers are usually located near the regions of the websites you’re targeting. This proximity reduces latency, which can be crucial for successfully checking out items during drops or restocks.
    
2.  **24/7 Availability** You don’t need to leave your home computer on all the time. A server runs 24/7, so you can set up tasks and forget about them.
    
3.  **Better Performance** Servers are equipped with high end hardware that can handle multiple tasks and bots at once, ensuring smooth performance.
    
4.  **Reliability** With high speed internet and power backup systems, servers are far more reliable than home setups, especially in areas with inconsistent internet connections.
    
5.  **Portability** Access your server from any device, whether it’s a laptop, tablet, or phone, as long as you have an internet connection.
    
6.  **Privacy** Using a server helps separate your botting activities from your personal computer, which is ideal for security.
    

* * *

**Cons**

1.  **Cost** Servers are not free, and the monthly cost can range from $10 to $100+ depending on the specifications. However, this is often a worthwhile investment for serious botters.
    
2.  **Learning Curve** For beginners, setting up and using a server might seem a bit tricky at first. However, it’s relatively straightforward once you get the hang of it.
    
3.  **Dependent on Internet** While servers themselves have strong internet connections, your ability to access them depends on your local internet connection.
    

circle-exclamation

It's not recommend to use a server for some sites like Target and Pokemon Center. These sites can detect if you're on a server and will drastically decrease your chances to checkout products

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/servers#when-should-you-use-a-server)

**When Should You Use a Server?**

*   **High Traffic Drops:** If you’re going for limited items during a high demand release, a server’s low latency can make a big difference.
    
*   **Scaling Up:** If you want to run multiple bots or hundreds of tasks, a server is almost essential to avoid overloading your home computer.
    
*   **Inconsistent Internet or Power:** If your home internet is unreliable or you experience frequent power outages, a server provides a stable environment.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/servers#why-we-recommend-stella-proxies-for-servers)

**Why We Recommend Stella Proxies for Servers**

We are proudly partnered with [**Stella Proxies**](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
, a trusted provider of botting servers. Here’s why we recommend them:

1.  **Optimized for Botting** Stella Proxies servers are specifically designed for botting, ensuring low ping and fast speeds for your tasks.
    
2.  **Affordable Pricing** They offer competitive rates, so even beginners can afford to use high quality servers.
    
3.  **Excellent Support** If you run into any issues, their support team is knowledgeable and responsive, helping you get back on track quickly.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/servers#how-to-get-started-with-a-server)

**How to Get Started with a Server**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FNrqv54fsfMoRFbHMsjOb%252Fstellaproxies1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De71f605b-60f6-4cc0-90ea-145bf572bda0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df26e052&sv=2)

1.  **Choose a Server Plan** Visit [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/www.stellaproxies.com)
     website and select a server package that fits your needs. If you’re unsure, their support team can guide you. Join their Discord server, the invite link is located on their website
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCHbY6ParyILqESVytvyK%252Fstellaproxies2.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08eea0f6-d263-4225-b764-1b43d3ee5882&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49a4e946&sv=2)

1.  **Connect to the Server** Once you purchase a server, you’ll receive login credentials. Use Remote Desktop Protocol (RDP) to connect.
    
2.  **Install Your Bot** After logging in, download and install Stellar AIO or any other bot you’re using.
    
3.  **Set Up Your Tasks** Configure your tasks, just like you would on your home computer and start botting!
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/servers#final-tips)

**Final Tips**

*   **Test Your Server**: Always run a test task to ensure everything is set up correctly before a major drop.
    
*   **Monitor Latency**: Check your ping to the website you’re targeting and make adjustments if needed.
    
*   **Ask for Help**: If you run into issues, reach out to the Stella Proxies support team.
    

* * *

Using a server can greatly enhance your botting experience by improving speed, reliability, and convenience. If you’re serious about botting, it’s a worthwhile investment. For the best performance, check out Stella Proxies’ server options and let us know if you have any questions!

# How do I uninstall StellarAIO (Windows and Mac) | Stellar

[Windows Uninstall](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-uninstall-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_986547fada)

[Mac Uninstall](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-uninstall-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_7ec0576a7c)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-uninstall-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_986547fada)

**Windows Uninstall**

1.  Right-click the Windows icon on the bottom left of your screen
    
2.  Look for "**Control Panel**"
    
3.  Go to "**Programs**"
    
4.  Go to "**Programs and Features**"
    
5.  Look for "**StellarAIO X.X.XX**"
    
6.  Right-click on the program and click "**Uninstall**"
    
7.  You will be prompted with a confirmation screen to uninstall. Click on "**OK**" to confirm.
    
8.  StellarAIO is now uninstalled, restart your computer to make sure.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-uninstall-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_7ec0576a7c)

**Mac Uninstall**

1.  Click the **Apple** logo on the top left of your screen.
    
2.  Click on "**About This Mac**"
    
3.  You will get a pop-up with multiple tabs, look for the "**Storage**" tab and click on it.
    
4.  Once going to the "**Storage**" tab, click on the "**Manage...**" button
    
5.  Once all your applications and files have loaded, head to the "**Applications**" tab
    
6.  Once all your applications load, look for the "StellarAIO" app and `Control + Click`
    
7.  Click on "**Delete**" which will then give a confirmation pop-up that will ask you if you're sure you want to delete StellarAIO, click "**Delete**" again
    
8.  StellarAIO should now be deleted from your Mac computer, restart the computer to make sure.
    

[PreviousHow do I download StellarAIO? (Windows and Mac)chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac)
[NextHow do I move StellarAIO from PC/Mac to Mac/PC?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-move-stellaraio-from-pc-mac-to-mac-pc)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# How do I move StellarAIO to a new PC/Server? | Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-move-stellaraio-to-a-new-pc-server#how-do-i-move-stellar-to-a-new-pc-server)

**How do I move Stellar to a new PC/Server?**

1.  Go to the [Stellar Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio)
     and sign in
    
2.  Click on **Reset** button so you can attach your key to your new machine
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FTnknp8YVOunuomwEStdN%252Fresetkey.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7449f6f8-787c-4a69-9827-3e03f0995b0c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36a05818&sv=2)
    
3.  **Download** Stellar to your new machine and enter your key
    
    1.  [StellarAIO Windows Installation guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_d523604013)
        
    2.  [StellarAIO Mac Installation guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_6126dd8c70)
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-move-stellaraio-to-a-new-pc-server#h_f261e08d10)

**How do I locate and transfer my config.json/managed files?**

circle-info

_Note that in order to transfer all saved information, you must transfer the config.json file (steps provided further below)_

1.  Open **Stellar AIO**
    
2.  Go to **Settings**
    
3.  Go to **General**
    
4.  Scroll down and click **Export**
    
5.  This will save your config file to your desktop
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCJ5DIhQ3HuJqBJmwxvkh%252Fexportdata.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca000adb-25c3-4706-9360-048f74501a21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d526e0f2&sv=2)
    
6.  **Email** this file (located on your desktop) to yourself and download the file to your new machine
    
7.  **Import** this file
    
8.  Click the **Browse** button and click on the config you emailed yourself
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBCeiDzMf3BI9opYmIZph%252Fimportdata.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9819d757-cc36-4f2b-8c2c-22a744124ab4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cf12821&sv=2)
    
9.  Close and reopen Stellar AIO
    

[PreviousHow do I move StellarAIO from PC/Mac to Mac/PC?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-move-stellaraio-from-pc-mac-to-mac-pc)
[NextAbcMart JPchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/abcmart-jp)

# How do I download StellarAIO? (Windows and Mac) | Stellar

[Windows Download](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_d523604013)

[Mac Download](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_6126dd8c70)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_d523604013)

**Windows Download**

1.  Navigate towards the [#change-logarrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417581765295472830)
     channel
    
    1.  If you cant see the channel above then you don't have the permissions to view it. You'll need to bind your Discord account to you Stellar key if you own it. If you don't own Stellar and are renting, you'll have to get latest download links from the person you're renting Stellar from
        
    
2.  Look for the latest version of StellarAIO and download
    
3.  Click on the .exe once it is done installing.
    
4.  Agree to any terms to allow the installation of StellarAIO.
    
5.  Once the installation is finished, you will be prompted to enter your key before starting to use the bot. To get your key, head over to the [dashboardarrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio)
    .
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCUznfLih39dDAx53Ze6S%252F3.0verifyinglicense.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0155f81e-92b7-498e-9a31-b2576b542b78&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5ebc7cea&sv=2)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_6126dd8c70)

**Mac Download**

1.  Navigate towards the [StellarAIO discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/stellaraio)
     server
    
2.  Click on the [#change-logarrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417581765295472830)
     channel
    
3.  Look for the most recent Mac update
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FPevD0PvEQp7PVFk77mPr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De960e435-79f0-4181-a8c4-3a3e858c7ed4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bfdcf372&sv=2)

1.  Click on the link which will direct you to a WeTransfer download site
    
2.  Click on "**I agree**"
    
3.  Click on "**Download**"
    
4.  If Google Chrome asks to "**Keep**" or "**Discard**", click on "**Keep**"
    
5.  Once the dmg is done installing, click on it.
    
6.  Wait for it to verify the files and you will be prompted to **drag the StellarAIO icon into your Applications folder.** Proceed to drag the icon into the folder.
    
7.  Once done, it'll install StellarAIO on your computer
    
8.  Now navigate towards your "**Finder**" application
    
9.  Look for the "**Application**" section
    
10.  Scroll until you find the "**StellarAIO**" icon, double click to open.
    
11.  You will be prompted with a Security pop up asking if you want to open it. Click on "**Open**"
    
12.  Once clicking on "Open", you will be prompted to enter your key before starting to use the bot. To get your key, head over to the [dashboardarrow-up-right](https://account.stellara.io/)
    .
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCUznfLih39dDAx53Ze6S%252F3.0verifyinglicense.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0155f81e-92b7-498e-9a31-b2576b542b78&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5ebc7cea&sv=2)
    
    **How do I download an unidentified developer on Mac (Mac is blocking download)?** [Herearrow-up-right](https://support.apple.com/en-ph/guide/mac-help/mh40616/mac)
     is a simple to use guide on how to allow the download of StellarAIO!
    

[PreviousHow do I update Stellar? (PC and Mac)chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-update-stellar-pc-and-mac)
[NextHow do I uninstall StellarAIO (Windows and Mac)chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-uninstall-stellaraio-windows-and-mac)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Windows Download](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_d523604013)
    
*   [Mac Download](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-download-stellaraio-windows-and-mac#h_6126dd8c70)

# How do I move StellarAIO from PC/Mac to Mac/PC? | Stellar

**How do I move StellarAIO from PC/Mac to Mac/PC?**

circle-info

In order to transfer all saved information, you must transfer the config.json file (steps provided further below)

1.  Open **Stellar AIO**
    
2.  Go to **Settings**
    
3.  Go to **Data Management**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FsLAbbUPiRR29MaXUeYgR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6dc4e8f-55e5-4a2e-9987-99f8205be205&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6fddd7ad&sv=2)

1.  Scroll down and click **Export**
    
2.  This will save your config file to your desktop
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCJ5DIhQ3HuJqBJmwxvkh%252Fexportdata.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca000adb-25c3-4706-9360-048f74501a21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d526e0f2&sv=2)
    
3.  **Email** this file (located on your desktop) to yourself and download the file to your new machine
    
4.  **Import** this file
    
5.  Click the **Browse** button and click on the config you emailed yourself
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBCeiDzMf3BI9opYmIZph%252Fimportdata.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9819d757-cc36-4f2b-8c2c-22a744124ab4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cf12821&sv=2)
    
6.  Close and reopen Stellar AIO
    

**Download Stellar AIO**

1.  **Reset** your key in [Stellars Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio)
    
2.  Go to [#change-logarrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417581765295472830)
     in Stellars Discord server and download the latest version to your Mac or PC
    
    More information [here](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-update-stellar-pc-and-mac)
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBZJ5plOm3HPHbYbHSy9A%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8314e791-d2c2-452c-a8c4-a9e833f85fb1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aaf91296&sv=2)

[PreviousHow do I uninstall StellarAIO (Windows and Mac)chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-uninstall-stellaraio-windows-and-mac)
[NextHow do I move StellarAIO to a new PC/Server?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/installation-uninstallation/how-do-i-move-stellaraio-to-a-new-pc-server)

Last updated 3 months ago

# BaseJP | Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/basejp#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on BaseJP, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/basejp#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/basejp#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/basejp#base-jp-task-overview)

Base JP Task Overview

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYV7D6IhwPuE4zldEqmli%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80d70e42-f510-408e-8190-6ae9b20fa7f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a606f4b5&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   Normal mode allows you to use your profiles to purchase products fully automated
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Both ISPs and Resis work
        
    
*   What **Product** **URL** do I put in?
    
    *   The URL that should be entered is the URL of the product
        
        *   Ex. [https://marupei.shopselect.net/items/36946573arrow-up-right](https://marupei.shopselect.net/items/36946573)
            
        *   Lottery is supported, enter the product URL as normal and the bot will detect the Lottery
            
        
    
*   What **Site** do I put in?
    
    *   The sites homepage URL
        
        *   Ex. [https://marupei.shopselect.net/arrow-up-right](https://marupei.shopselect.net/)
            
            *   We support all Base JP sites
                
            
        
    
*   What **Size** do I put in?
    
    *   If sizes aren't loaded (OS product) we advise not to fill out sizes field
        
    *   If size are loaded, we support `Random` and direct size like `27` or `M` whichever the format is from the website
        
    
*   What's **Product Quantity**?
    
    *   Enter the quantity of the item you'd like to checkout
        
    
*   What's **Payment Methods**?
    
    *   Bank Transfer
        
    *   Credit Card (slowest payment method)
        
    *   Convenience Store
        
    

[PreviousBarnes & Noblechevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble)
[NextBestBuychevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/basejp#profiles)

# Argos UK | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXftG1NU9YsKRo7ZymskkIc-1ZSLzJagKgPu6i_ouB-Hq-hU7tvm1rRkRTAPqzBVGa0qvrw-lae1AORJ9khY5UMPXY-nY7DQxCyWIB1STDR_jOIOwctXj1s0BnbDHfjlgd4Q7gk8kQ%3Fkey%3DCy4ICRrbVLQ-mguc76QLCWHH&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0b46ea8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Argos UK, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#normal-shipping-mode)

Normal (Shipping mode)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FEs9TRQIeFm9Jyvo8j2yB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1dd8d8c-4b7b-4006-b1cf-2ca5e470a615&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e23fae4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#monitor-monitor-for-shipping)

Monitor (monitor for shipping)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXceJdBxZkukU-qjnKH_piSmy_cwrk3WCf2iUXC9a0WygRMypV2j_Qk2CuOMMpXOmylD0DuzQRdsWwwir5Q74YyJekR18zzIQUb5QKje-QSZAJ6gsFe_dcgG_MEtJZ0uNaLG2DvaZA%3Fkey%3DCy4ICRrbVLQ-mguc76QLCWHH&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f8b262b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#collection-mode)

Collection mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSL6NI3jDJXqMC3mtZKZr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D887db3eb-aec5-4f7b-b21a-8907ea9d84a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13c4f98b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#monitor-collection-monitor-for-collection)

Monitor-collection (monitor for collection)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FMLJTltN8YUW2kYLaiTEu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29d8aa0f-ac22-497e-8b40-6c1f82f8eef3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef64f420&sv=2)

*   Which Mode do I use?
    
    *   Normal mode (shipping) is your checkout task is to be used for normal shipping checkout flow
        
    *   Monitor mode (monitor for shipping) will only monitor and ping your watch tasks when they detect the item you're monitoring is in stock for shipping
        
    *   Collection mode is your checkout task is to be used for collection in store checkout flow
        
    *   Monitor-collection (monitor for collection) will only monitor and ping your watch tasks when they detect the item you're monitoring is in stock for collection
        
    
*   What does Profile mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of Proxies should I use?
    
    *   You need to use high quality proxies, usually ISPs but can also use resis
        
        If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    
*   What is Product SKU?
    
    *   For example https://www.argos.co.uk/product/7487499 so SKU will be 7487499
        
    
*   What is QTY?
    
    *   The number of items you want in one order
        
    
*   What is Delay?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error
        
        You can start your delays around 2000 and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is Postal Code?
    
    *   Your postcode for collection from stores, it will try to cart a stock nearby your postcode only
        
    
*   What is Pickup Radius?
    
    *   The max distance in miles of pickup from your postal code
        
    
*   What is Discount?
    
    *   The discount code or voucher
        
    
*   What is Store ID?
    
    *   The ID of the store use https://www.argos.co.uk/stores/ example: https://www.argos.co.uk/stores/6520-farringdon-sainsbury's-(argos-collection-point) so store ID will be 6520
        
    
*   What is Monitoring Delay?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product
        
        You can start your delays around 3000-5000 and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is Reset Delay?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product again after it has detected the item is in stock
        
        You can start your delays around 3000-5000 and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is Restart On Decline/Failure? Box?
    
    *   The task will auto restart if the card is declined or the item went out of stock
        
    
*   What is Watch task? Box?
    
    *   The task will monitor itself or rely on alert if the item will be back in a stock this mode is recommend it if you don't have enough proxies to run tasks to avoid proxy ban
        
    
*   What is Use TopCashBack? Box?
    
    *   Follow the [TopCashBack guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    

Important Notes:

Guest Checkouts Only: Argos does not support account logins. Ensure that your billing profiles are configured for guest checkout.

Proxies: Use ISP proxies for the best success rate. Ensure proxies are from the UK for optimal performance.

Product SKUs: The SKU is the unique identifier in the product URL (e.g., for https://www.argos.co.uk/product/7487499, the SKU is 7487499).

[PreviousArcteryxchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx)
[NextBarnes & Noblechevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#proxies)
    
*   [Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#task-overview)
    
*   [Normal (Shipping mode)](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk#normal-shipping-mode)

# Apple | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fl3MZIp3hhAvzOZcXGKJn%252FApple-Logo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2271d7f7-57da-48a0-9928-94ca7868e3a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aa4520f9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/apple#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Apple, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/apple#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/apple#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/apple#apple-task-overview)

Apple Task Overview

**Shipping Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F4yqEJHEUBmIG2PS5LrQP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0786bc15-9366-4309-a264-317d84ad2c2d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44d57f28&sv=2)

**Instore Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FsReHMs7k0HxJwzFc7HS7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2839da75-f18e-4f3e-83e7-546af896ba55&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d589fa4e&sv=2)

**In-Store Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FDX1LyGdZrVwMVAjdRyvI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b270b22-2806-48c2-9db4-91c64dc0f294&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39e7bdac&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Shipping mode** allows you to guest checkout products with shipping fulfillment
        
    *   **Instore mode** allows you to guest checkout products with pick up in store fulfillment
        
    *   **In-store monitor mode** allows you to monitor a product URL with just one monitor mode task and it'll notify all of your running Instore checkout mode tasks with the same product URL if they have Watch Task box checked
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Both ISPs and Resis work
        
    
*   What **URL** do I put in?
    
    *   The URL that should be entered is the URL of the product. You may have to go through the products options Apple offers on the website to get the correct url. The url will change depending on the options you select
        
        *   Ex. [https://www.apple.com/shop/buy-iphone/iphone-14-pro/6.7-inch-display-1tb-silver-unlockedarrow-up-right](https://www.apple.com/shop/buy-iphone/iphone-14-pro/6.7-inch-display-1tb-silver-unlocked)
            
        
    
*   How do I select a **Region**?
    
    *   You can select US, CA, JP or HK
        
    
*   What are **Delays**?
    
    *   The time in millisecond intervals the bot will monitor the product
        
        *   A good delay to use for Apple will be around `4500`
            
        
    
*   What is a good **Quantity** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://help.stellara.io/en/articles/5772208-cook-groups-and-proxies)
         since different items have different quantity limits but you can enter `1` or more
        
    
*   How do I use my **Giftcard(s)**?
    
    *   You can input up to 8 giftcards, the bot will add as much as needed but if the price on your giftcards is below order total, it'll continue with credit card otherwise it'll submit just order with giftcards if the price of giftcards is enough to pay their order
        
        *   Example of multiple gift card format `111111111111,222222222222,333333333333,444444444444`
            
        
    
*   What is **Instore Distance**?
    
    *   In miles, enter the distance you're willing to travel to pick up products in store
        
    
*   What is **Instore Pickup Name**?
    
    *   Enter the name of the person picking up your order
        
    
*   What is **Zipcode**?
    
    *   Enter the zipcode of the store you want to pickup from
        
    
*   What is **Business Name**?
    
    *   Enter the name of the business for Tax Exemption
        
    
*   What is **Monitor Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds when monitoring. `4500` is OK which would be 4.5 seconds
        
    
*   What is **Restart On Decline?** box?
    
    *   Check this box if you want your task to restart if it encounters a decline or OOS message
        
    
*   What is **Random Pickup Time?** box?
    
    *   Check this box if you want the task to pick a random pickup time
        
    *   Leave this box unchecked if you want the task to pick the earliest available pickup time
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the product, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousAmazon CAchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca)
[NextArcteryxchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx)
