# Arcteryx | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FTDyzrXgq1AEIZy0eO2V0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8ad090f-5774-48cb-af74-6860b5340aaf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=33d5bb62&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Arcteryx, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx#queueit-browser-extension)

Browser Extension

1.  **Download** Stellar-queue browser extension for Google Chrome: [Stellar AIO Chrome Extension V3arrow-up-right](https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/136nPcGwzFRLuLvtgaQyK1kVKf02QcQe9?usp=drive_link)
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAHRqmN8ivOO4vcejQx6C%252FSAIO%2520EXT%2520V3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee462893-1421-42c9-ab1e-b31c5e776cab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1764c6b4&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Extract All..."
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FU4ItmlMivPsAaw230rB8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df81ec76b-5f94-4d1e-b626-7e8f1bbab345&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cac4463d&sv=2)

1.  In Chrome, go to **Manage Extensions**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwmnhUm6l2azV30AUEHhH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39919511-46fa-40fe-a588-31df0675eec4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3b8f875&sv=2)

1.  On the top right corner of the Manage Extensions page turn on **Developer Mode** and click **Load Unpacked**. Now select the Stellar AIO Chrome Extension folder that you extracted, it'll be located in Downloads
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYh1VWAxvKbiCGcydttpw%252Fextensionfolder.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5464443f-2699-4242-a331-3e17f20f1143&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95661145&sv=2)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F82o0Ne5WzSNCZJRpllWT%252FSAIO%2520EXT%2520V3%2520Manage.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d4839ad-35ff-48f7-a4d0-def681f9a22b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64576229&sv=2)

1.  Go back to Chrome, click on the puzzle piece on the top right corner. You can now **pin** the **Stellar Extension** to your Chrome toolbar
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FEyuDqNyazdKsjlmpFEyR%252Fimageofextensionopen.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da28b28a7-236e-4955-91c0-a9508a5136c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c255a9f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx#offspring-task-overview)

Offspring Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FU4PSq0VprnkO1GfDPvDb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5417671d-28f9-4455-8629-ebe6ba6c236d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3107ffd4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FTlqgn538cEuCvZKqnBlx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f415923-fb27-47fc-afd1-027c063eb57d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9724312&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is used for normal guest checkout
        
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to monitor product availability, these tasks will notify/ping your Normal mode watch tasks
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **proxies** should I use?
    
    *   **DCs** and **ISPs** are the best due to speed but residentials also work but might have a large data usage
        
    
*   What is the **Product URL** and how do I get them?
    
    *   The product URL can be found from your cookgroup or by navigating the website to the correct product, then copy the entire url to the product and paste in this field in bot
        
    
*   What **Size** to use?
    
    *   Input the **Size** you'd like to run for. One size per task. For example `10.5`
        
        *   You can type `Random` for random sizing
            
        
    
*   What is **Payment Method**?
    
    *   You can select Credit Card or Gift Cards
        
    
*   What are **Gift Cards**?
    
    *   The Gift Cards option allows you to apply gift cards during checkout. To use gift cards:
        
        *   Go to the **Tags** tab in Stellar
            
            *   Create a new Tag Group (example: **Arcteryx Gift Cards**)
                
                *   Add your gift cards **one per line** using the format:
                    
                
            
            Copy
            
            Example:
            
            Copy
            
        
        Once saved, select this Tag Group in your tasks to apply gift cards at checkout.
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment anywhere between 3000 and 5000
        
    
*   What is **Force ATC?** checkbox?
    
    *   Only check this box if you want the bot to skip monitoring and forece add to cart
        
    
*   What is a **Watch Task** and should I select it?
    
    *   The **Watch Task** option allows your checkout task (e.g., Normal mode) to work together with a **Monitor mode task**. Here's how it works:
        
        *   If you check this box, your **checkout task** will not monitor for restocks directly. Instead, it will wait for a **Monitor mode task** (with the same SKU) to detect a restock
            
            *   Once the Monitor task detects the restock, it will "ping" your running checkout (with the same SKU) tasks to ATC and checkout
                
            
        
        When using the **Watch Task** option:
        
        1.  Start your checkout task. It will display the message: **"Waiting for Monitor Ping."** This means it's ready and set up correctly
            
        2.  When the Monitor task detects a restock, it will automatically trigger the checkout task (with the same SKU) to run
            
        
        If you leave the **Watch Task** checkbox **unchecked**, the checkout task will act independently. It will monitor the SKU itself, add the item to your cart, and checkout directly
        
    

[PreviousApplechevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/apple)
[NextArgos UKchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/argos-uk)

# Adafruit | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fnews.sophos.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2022%2F03%2Fadafruit-1200.png%3Fw%3D1200&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6b4bac4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/adafruit#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Adafruit make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/adafruit#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/adafruit#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/adafruit#adding-sessions)

**Adding Sessions**

To add your Adafruit sessions to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Sessions** tab then click on **Adafruit**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSjqYLmLBuVybxJHZRNam%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520162323.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97f77019-6a97-45cd-b577-3955ebae4f88&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9ddd482&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Session** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSxi7jWExkJvbs3evhkjZ%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520162343.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df444014f-ae56-4ff0-953e-9811a4f828c6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7b30c8c&sv=2)

1.  Enter your Adafruit account email and password and press save.
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgIJptCsbZ9iZsXwhwthG%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520162536.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc968899a-ef22-4c2c-8d50-6ea1d785d7ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf2b838e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/adafruit#adafruit-task-overview)

Adafruit Task Overview

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLLBjHXv2pr16tfnWj8ND%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4676c37d-1b1e-47cd-a106-45a053bc6ad2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ccf52ce&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is only mode available currently. This mode uses guest checkout to purchase items, unless a session is inputted
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Recommended to run a mix of ISPs and Resis
        
    
*   How do I find the **Product URL**?
    
    *   Go to the product page and copy the URL in task bar
        
        *   Example: [arrow-up-right](https://www.adafruit.com/product/50)
            [https://www.adafruit.com/product/50arrow-up-right](https://www.adafruit.com/product/50)
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   We recommend running around 5000 delays for restocks.
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   The best QTY to use is 1 but if the item you're running for allows for more QTY per cart, feel free to increase the QTY
        
    
*   What is a **Session**?
    
    *   This option allows you to select a specific session you'd like to use for this task. Each session has your account login saved making it faster to create tasks
        
    
*   What is **Cheapest Shipping?** box?
    
    *   Check this box if you'd like to purchase your product with the cheapest shipping option available

[NextAmazonV3chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on BillysJP, make sure you have everything below prepared:

###

Billys JP Accounts

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/billysjp#billys-jp-task-overview)

Billys JP Task Overview

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FOntKlnIF3QQvUWp9ODll%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99474281-215c-4458-bda8-a9b6dbc523b6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b800311&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   Normal mode allows you to use your profiles to purchase products fully automated
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Both ISPs and Resis work
        
    
*   What **Product** **URL** do I put in?
    
    *   The URL that should be entered is the URL of the product
        
        *   Ex. [https://www.billys-tokyo.net/shop/g/g6672930001044/arrow-up-right](https://www.billys-tokyo.net/shop/g/g6672930001044/)
            
        
    
*   How do I add **Sizing**?
    
    *   Sizing should be specific to the product and only one size per task. You must know the exact format in which it follows on BillysJP for each product.
        
        *   Some products are 22, 23, 24. Others might have 22cm, 23cm, 24cm etc. Same goes for clothing, hats, etc. **These must be entered in the same exact format for it to be picked up** such as sizes S, M, L, etc. If you are going after multiple sizes, you are going to need a task for each size you desire
            
            *   Ex. `22cm`
                
            
        
    
*   What's **Account**?
    
    *   This is required. To add accounts to Stellar, follow the steps [here](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/billysjp#billys-jp-accounts)
        
    
*   What are **Delays**?
    
    *   The time in millisecond intervals the bot will monitor the product
        
        *   A good delay to use for BillysJP will be around `4500`
            
        
    

[PreviousB&H Photochevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo)
[NextBooksAMillionchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion)

# BooksAMillion | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FkTEP4u1vyBhTozN6GFGM%252Fbam.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d6e437c-b653-4e7d-8a02-3a052e381b49&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0b9a4fc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion#accounts)

Accounts

All checkouts will be using Guest checkout so accounts are not needed. If accounts are required for purchases in the future, we'll look into adding account support

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on BooksAMillion, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fp51ozU3dLg3on1Wl8XwJ%252Fbammonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e98097d-b73b-4625-a569-a99c8072f820&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3295e1b5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fs9X6Ic1mojrT08E6CCnL%252Fbamnormal.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da647b8ba-6e48-47e6-84b9-7322611f2a00&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d84ab65&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor your desired items. When an item restocks, your monitor mode tasks will ping your running watch tasks (Normal mode) tasks to atc and checkout
        
    *   **Normal mode** is your normal checkout mode task
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and residentials will both work
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   Where do I find **URL**?
    
    *   Every product will have it's own unique Product URL. Ex. [https://www.booksamillion.com/p/Panini-Donruss-Optic-Football-Blaster/Panini/F746134146039arrow-up-right](https://www.booksamillion.com/p/Panini-Donruss-Optic-Football-Blaster/Panini/F746134146039)
        
    
*   What is **Max Price**?
    
    *   Input the max price of the product you're wanting to purchase (If retail cost for one qty is $29 you can put 35 here as a safe buffer)
        
        *   Max price field is only for one QTY regardless of how many you're wanting to purchase
            
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   A good default to use is 1, but if the listing on the site allows for multiple in one cart then feel free to increase the QTY. You can find out product Max Qty from your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment between 4000 - 6000
        
    
*   What is **Reset Delay** and what should I use?
    
    *   **Reset Delay** is the time in ms your monitor mode tasks will restart and monitor the product again after it catches a restock
        
        *   Around `5000` is OK
            
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   **Watch tasks** and **non-watch tasks** are different
        
        *   **Non-watch tasks** will be monitoring the site, which means that it will be using proxies. When a product restocks, this same task will atc and checkout
            
        *   **Watch tasks** are "watching" your **Monitor Mode** tasks waiting for a product you're running for to restock. Your **watch tasks** will add to cart and checkout when its pinged from a **Monitor Mode** task
            
        
    *   Your Monitor mode tasks will ping/notify your running Normal mode watch tasks when the product has restocked so they'll attempt to atc and checkout
        
    
*   What is **Use Rakuten?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [Rakuten guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-rakuten-cashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    
*   What is the **Task Limit**?
    
    *   Currently at 50 but may change at any time
        
    

[PreviousBillysJPchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/billysjp)
[NextBoxlunchchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch)

>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/abcmart-jp#adding-accounts)

Adding Accounts

To add your AbcMart accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to Sessions tab, click on Accounts then click on AbcMart
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAIVDiVlLhYpddFX3Jfub%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520161406.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De570feaa-e9da-4e81-8434-5e26309b7985&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30572e51&sv=2)

1.  Click on Add Account
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FFTrSA4qjgcwzdDdwlQ6u%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520161908.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5f6f477-b2af-4697-a10a-c5182f83ecae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2115cc9&sv=2)

1.  Add account details to bot and click Add to save
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FtrhKeoKhpw8YUC1wDcNA%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520161530.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9f3c6a6-05ab-4dbd-acc5-e080c2c00af9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76278b76&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/abcmart-jp#task-overview)

Task Overview

**FCFS Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FvicmAUk4iRahTTBptAnA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ce750b3-0405-4aa7-866c-2974e4872c39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8305e6aa&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   FCFS mode allows you to checkout first come first served products from AbcMart using an account
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Both ISPs and Resis work
        
    
*   What **URL** do I put in?
    
    *   The URL that should be entered is the URL of the product
        
        *   Ex. [https://www.abc-mart.net/shop/g/g6678930001043/arrow-up-right](https://www.abc-mart.net/shop/g/g6678930001043/)
            
        
    
*   How do I add **Size**?
    
    *   Sizing should be specific to the product and only one size per task. Size can be either `Random` or `23.5` etc.
        
    
*   What's **Account**?
    
    *   Use your accounts to purchase products. To add accounts to Stellar, follow the steps [here](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/abcmart-jp#adding-accounts)
        
    
*   What's **Payment Methods**?
    
    *   COD (Cash on Delivery, faster)
        
    *   Credit Card
        
    
*   What are **Delays**?
    
    *   The time in millisecond intervals the bot will monitor the product
        
        *   A good delay to use for AbcMart will be around `4500`

# B&H Photo | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYElvZEGnAevixqO1HqcF%252FB%2526H_Photo-Logo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45dd9081-968b-438d-8e99-496c93e3e784&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0ee94a&sv=2)

circle-info

The only support available at the time this guide was created was for guest checkout. When there is sufficient demand, we will think about implementing account support.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on B&H Photo, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Feitdhhw0bXMdCrZ2U86K%252Fbhphotomonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D517b090c-82f5-4c95-9c83-65fcb4a2c1ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3561ac1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FuCF24QedWKv5m4ENmsks%252Fbhphotonormal.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddedda155-d2c4-4a17-a185-3c9926286283&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5da49385&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** allows you to cart and checkout any products
        
    *   **Monitor mode** allows you to monitor any product. When the products you're monitoring come into stock, your monitor mode tasks will notify your running Normal mode tasks with the same product SKU
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   The best type of **proxies** to use for B&H Photo are ISPs
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **Product URL** and how do I get it?
    
    *   For example [https://www.bhphotovideo.com/c/product/1875718-REG/gigabyte\_gv\_n5090aorusm\_ice\_32gd\_geforce\_rtx\_5090\_master.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.bhphotovideo.com/c/product/1875718-REG/gigabyte_gv_n5090aorusm_ice_32gd_geforce_rtx_5090_master.html)
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   The safest QTY to use is 1, but some listings allow you to check out more than 1 QTY per order
        
    
*   What is **Delay**? (Normal mode only)
    
    *   This is the time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error
        
        *   Recommended `1000` or less
            
        
    
*   What is **Monitoring Delay**? (Monitor mode only)
    
    *   This is the time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product in intervals
        
        *   Recommended around `5000`
            
        
    
*   What is **Reset Delay**?
    
    *   This is the time in milliseconds the bot will restart the monitor task and monitor the product again after it has come in stock
        
        *   Recommended around `5000`
            
        
    
*   What is a **Watch Task** and should I select it?
    
    *   The **Watch Task** option allows your checkout task (e.g., Normal mode) to work together with a **Monitor mode task**. Here's how it works:
        
        *   If you check this box, your **checkout task** will not monitor for restocks directly. Instead, it will wait for a **Monitor mode task** (with the same SKU) to detect a restock
            
            *   Once the Monitor task detects the restock, it will "ping" your running checkout (with the same SKU) tasks to ATC and checkout
                
            
        
        When using the **Watch Task** option:
        
        1.  Start your checkout task. It will display the message: **"Waiting for Monitor Ping."** This means it's ready and set up correctly
            
        2.  When the Monitor task detects a restock, it will automatically trigger the checkout task (with the same SKU) to run
            
        
        If you leave the **Watch Task** checkbox **unchecked**, the checkout task will act independently. It will monitor the SKU itself, add the item to your cart, and checkout directly
        
    

circle-exclamation

Using Watch Task is highly recommended for restocks because it allows the Monitor task to do the heavy lifting. This improves performance and helps avoid overloading the site.

*   What is the **Task Limit**?
    
    *   Currently at 50 but may change at any time
        
    

[PreviousBestBuy CAchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca)
[NextBillysJPchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/billysjp)

*   [Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo#proxies)
    
*   [Monitor mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo#monitor-mode)
    
*   [Normal mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/b-and-h-photo#normal-mode)

# Amazon CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2Fa%2Fa9%2FAmazon_logo.svg%2F603px-Amazon_logo.svg.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97fd4a41&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Amazon, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca#h_50c8b20444)

**Amazon Accounts**

> This module requires an Amazon account. Before you start, double-check that your billing and shipping information lines up with the profile you’ll be using.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca#h_50c8b20444-1)

**Authenticator Application**

> Download and install an authenticator app (we recommend Google Authenticator). You’ll need it to properly set up and secure your tasks.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca#cook-group-access)

**Cook Group Access**

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **ISP** and **DC Proxies** are recommended for 24/7 Monitoring for Amazon.ca, you do not need Canadian ISP proxies for Amazon.ca. Residential proxies may also be used (if absolutely needed) but watch the amount of data usage.
    
*   Amount of proxies is still important for Amazon.ca, the quality of proxy will depend on the provider. You will see more of the "**Captcha Detected | Rotating Proxy**" status' if your proxies have been heavily abused. With clean proxies, you will see less of the captcha's.
    
*   Amazon Canada functions differently than Amazon US, so do not use Amazon US low delays and think it works for Canada.
    
*   You will need to create your own **Monitor** tasks to supplement Stellar's own checkout tasks, and having a few of your own monitor tasks is recommended.
    
*   **Sessions** are used for Amazon.ca, this will consist of your individual amazon accounts that you will need to create under the **Sessions** tab on the left hand side of Stellar. There are currently 2 options to add sessions
    
    *   Option #1 Mass Import Sessions - To begin Mass import, ensure you are on the Amazon sessions page, Click **Mass Import Sessions.**
        
        *   The format of your import needs to be **Format:**`Email;Password;LoginProxy;Region;AuthenticatorKey`
            
            **Example:** `[[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;Stellar9;;CA;XXXX`
            
        
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FtU2np5NXj2OTO7KRYgYx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db44ff602-1352-4f94-a3c6-c207087e4c83&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c4b3e8f&sv=2)
    
    *   Each Account you want to import will be in a separate line.
        
    *   Select **Save** once you are done
        
    *   Option #2 Manually Add Sessions - To begin adding individual sessions, ensure you are on the Amazon sessions page, Click **Add Sessions** and name your sessions followed by Save
        
        ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLI3yGexSNXR2mtSwdxZM%252FAMZ%2520Session.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4cfcdad3-9308-42de-9133-29c93c0521b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f911167&sv=2)
        
        ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSxi7jWExkJvbs3evhkjZ%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520162343.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df444014f-ae56-4ff0-953e-9811a4f828c6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7b30c8c&sv=2)
        
    *   A new row will appear under the session name you have just created. Open up the new session to edit **Region**, **Account Email, Account Password**, **Login Proxy**, your **2FA Authentication Key** and your **Login Method.** Hit Save when you are done.
        
        ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FFVk4xcQeSneHCtrZAgzc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf101ac1-f130-4561-9356-05ee23b26471&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fb87830&sv=2)
        
    

circle-exclamation

Proxies attatched to your amazon sessions are used for login as well as ATC

*   **Login Methods:** There are currently 2 methods Stellar uses to login to your Amazon Account
    
    *   Method #1 - **Request Login** - This method automatically handles the login process for you unless you have OTP confirmation popups, However if you have inputted a 2FA Authenicator Key, the login process will all be automatic
        
    *   Method #2 - **Browser Login** - Will pop up a browser when you start up a task with that account, will need to login to your Amazon account manually and will have to manually close the browse once complete.
        
    
*   **2FA Authenticator Key -** Please refer to [this guidearrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#h_50c8b20444)
     to create a 2FA Key
    
*   Do you think you are soft banned on Amazon.ca? Log into your account, and if you can click on "Your Account" after logging in and you do not see any "Amazon Dogs" you are not soft banned. It could be an error from the software.
    
*   Some accounts have been getting locked once they lose their Session. At this moment in time, there is no sure fire way to get around this. Amazon has been doing this to any account, with no rhyme or reason. This is happening for other bots as well.
    

**Important:** If your Amazon accounts are **re-logging in frequently**, it’s usually proxy-related.

Use **clean ISP proxies assigned directly to your sessions**. Residential proxies rotate IPs, which forces Amazon to re-login on every change. A single clean session IP can stay stable for **1–2 weeks** without issues.

Avoid running **multiple tasks on the same account at the same time**. Logging in or checking out from different IPs simultaneously will almost always trigger a re-login.

For best results:

*   Assign **one dedicated, clean ISP** per Amazon account
    
*   Do not rotate session IPs
    
*   Avoid sharing accounts across tasks
    

Amazon aggressively protects accounts and re-login is one of their most common safeguards.

* * *

**TAGS:**

You can also create **Custom** **TAGS**, you can do this by clicking on the **TAGS** tab, and then clicking on **Custom** and then **Add:**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FlwNDIvRimLg59XnBOy0W%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf7ea758-b585-4623-9821-7577d39808c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f18b14c4&sv=2)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FK1ZCwqg1Z0k2R4DHEgSe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94633fc6-a08d-4186-8f71-daa31c51cd39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e54a657&sv=2)

And then name that Tag whatever you like (for our example, let's call it **Lorcana**):

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FDbBC2iUcGxRX8pn35jnn%252FTags%2520name.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06ce6b85-80e8-4789-bae2-da100d598431&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=616dac66&sv=2)

Then click on **Manage SKUs** on the top right of Stellar and then enter your SKU's when the dialog box pops up.

**Amazon Max Price** **for Tags**

*   Max Price is used for checkout tasks. You can run a Fast Monitor with OID and if the item price exceeds your set limit, it will retry 5–10 times to check for a price adjustment. If the price remains too high, it will return to monitoring - eliminating the risk of checking out overpriced items.
    
*   This is optional and entirely based on user preference.
    
*   The price is **per unit, excluding shipping**.
    

**Example:**

*   Item Price: $50
    
    *   Quantity: 6
        
    *   Max Price in Tags: $50 (not $300)
        
    *   Shipping is not included.
        
    

Now you can point your **Watch Task/Checkout Task** to the **TAG** you have created.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca#task-overview)

Task Overview

You will be presented with different ways to create tasks: **Monitor or Special**. Cloud and Invite modes are not for Canada region at the time of updating this guide. The following will explain the different tasks that can be created:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F5tgc6H4p22d2uc2CCTHq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa9dc728-c7b3-4823-857c-96de0ef00970&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80bcf646&sv=2)

What to enter in **Monitor Task**:

*   This mode will only monitor and can't checkout. Use **Bulk CSV List** – This feature allows you to input multiple skus at once to monitor. you can monitor SKUs using the monitor mode task to ping any Watch Tasks. Special mode tasks are watch tasks by default
    
*   **Monitor Proxy:** Create a proxy group of your choice
    
*   **SKU:** Enter the SKU of the product you wish to monitor. Look at the Tags for AmazonCA in the TAGS tab that you would also like to create a manual monitor Task for. Otherwise, reach out to your cook group for the other SKU's.
    
*   **Offer ID:** Enter the OfferID of the product you wish to monitor. Reach out to your cook group for the Offer ID's.
    
*   **Max Price:** This isn't as necessary if you're using an OfferID as that will dictate the cost of the item you're monitoring. However, if you're using **Scrape** Mode (with no OfferID), it is recommended that you input a max price for the item you are looking at securing.
    
*   **Delay:** Enter a delay that will work for you (_**recommended 8500 and above, however lower at your own discretion**_), this is totally dependent on the proxies that you use, whether it be DC or ISP. The quality of proxy will dictate how quickly your monitoring tasks will see the "**Captcha Detected | Rotating Proxy**" status due to proxy abuse.
    
*   **Region:** **Select CA**
    
*   **Monitoring Method:** You will be presented with two different monitoring methods:
    
    *   **Scrape:** This method is used when you do not have an OfferID for the specific item. Input the SKU of the item you would like to monitor and **set a Max price** on the item just in case.
        
    *   **Fast:** This is an alternative monitoring method that uses a different endpoint and **requires an OID**. This will ignore the max price field and use the price within the OID. OIDs already have prices
        
        *   It is recommended to use both Fast and Scrape with your monitoring modes
            
        
    *   **Business**: Monitors the Amazon Business product page. Requires a valid Business Offer ID (OID) and an active Amazon Business account for checkout.
        
    
*   **Should Solve Captcha:** This will let Stellar know if you want it to solve the captcha's or not. Otherwise it will rotate your proxy.
    
*   **Reset Delay:** Test with 30000 to 60000, this is in milliseconds, so 30000 = 30 seconds, 60000 = 60s. Up to your discretion, too low of a reset delay will burn your proxies.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazon-ca#special-mode)

**Special Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FHdyW1fheAVTgh9vDoyaH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47a53514-a99d-4c96-b220-b196935f4365&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=389aefb9&sv=2)

What's the difference between these new modes?

*   **Special Mode** are checkout tasks and watch tasks by default. You can insert the OfferID in your monitor mode task if you'd like. This mode works better with Amazon Prime accounts but having a Prime account is not required to use this mode
    

What to enter for for these different modes:

*   **Monitor Proxy:** Choose from a group of proxies you have created under the Proxies Section in Stellar
    
*   **Checkout Proxy:** Choose from a group of proxies you have created under the Proxies Section in Stellar
    
*   **Input List -** There are 3 types of ways you can input the product you would like to checkout
    
    *   Input #1 - Tags
        
        *   Enter a **TAG** of the product you wish to monitor (You can use your custom **TAG** that you have created here or use the pre-populated tags by stellar which are being monitored by Serverside). With the custom **TAG** ensure it has all the **SKU's** that you intend on having for check out, You are not required to have your **Monitor Task** (using that **SKU and OfferID),** within the same task group! As long as your **TAG** has the **SKU's** being monitored, it will ping the **Watch** tasks! You can enter more than one **TAG** here. _For SKU's and OfferID's please refer to your Cook Group._
            
        
    *   Input #2 - SKU
        
        *   Another way to input the product you would like to checkout is to directly enter the SKU of that product into the Input List field, You can input more than one SKU here.
            
        
    *   Input #3 - SKU:OfferID
        
        *   **!!!!!!** **IF YOU WANT TO RUN THE OLD OFFERID/ATC SPAM !!!!!!:** Under the **Input List** when creating your **Special Task,** enter the SKU:OfferID. Note that you **cannot** have more thanone SKU:OID per task. Please see below for an example:
            
        
    
*   **Delay:** Set a delay of your choice, for example: 3500. You can lower if you have more proxies, and if you aren't seeing any account soft bans.
    
*   **Qty:** **RECOMMENDED** to set to 1 in most cases for GPU or Consoles. Otherwise, this will be up to you.
    
*   **Session:** This will allow you to select All Sessions or individual sessions that you have created.
    
*   **Enter Cart Attempts:** You can leave this blank, however some users have found success with 25.
    
*   **Checkout Attempts:** You can put in 25 as a baseline. Play around to see what works best for you.
    
*   **Start Time:** Choose the date and time you want to start the task, you do not need to do this if you're trying to run 24/7.
    
*   **End Time:** Choose the date and time you want to end the task, you do not need to do this if you're trying to run 24/7.
    
*   **Should Solve Captcha:** Tells Stellar to solve any captcha's (requires capmonster). If left unchecked, this will rotate to a different proxy if you have that set.
    
*   **Endless Mode:** It will checkout constantly with no limit. Not recommended for GPU or Consoles
    

* * *

# Canon UK | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FZkGtmyjM88EvVBZm92qH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc7dd303-9da5-46ab-9553-acef476a8979&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3779bed0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-uk#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Canon UK, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-uk#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-uk#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-uk#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwIWIY0Rob5HgWn6JzpZ0%252Fcanonmon.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D852e3f71-d38b-471c-a6bb-4eb91116bbb5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=baaddcd2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-uk#normal-mode)

Normal Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F9SCyCoyzceKBDxRIu2CQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17547045-416f-45bc-a182-417d4174704c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e756215&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor your desired items. When an item restocks, your monitor mode tasks will ping your running watch tasks (Normal mode) tasks to checkout
        
    *   **Normal mode** is your normal checkout mode task (guest checkout)
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and residentials will both work. Ideally you'd want to use ISPs for monitor mode and residentials for normal mode
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   Where do I find **Product URL**?
    
    *   Every product will have it's own unique Product URL
        
        *   You can find out any product information from your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Monitoring Delay: Experiment around 6000
        
    *   Delay: (normal mode) Expeirment around 3000
        
    *   Reset Delay: 10000 or less
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   A good default to use is 1, but if the listing on the site allows for multiple in one cart then feel free to increase the QTY. You can find out product Max Qty from your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   **Watch tasks** and **non-watch tasks** are different
        
        *   **Non-watch tasks** will be monitoring the site, which means that it will be using proxies. When a product restocks, this same task will atc and checkout
            
        *   **Watch tasks** are "watching" your **Monitor Mode** tasks waiting for a product you're running for to restock. Your **watch tasks** will add to cart and checkout when its pinged from a **Monitor Mode** task
            
        
    *   Your Monitor mode tasks will ping/notify your running Normal mode watch tasks when the product has restocked so they'll attempt to atc and checkout
        
    

[PreviousCanon US & CAchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca)
[NextCostco US/CAchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-uk#proxies)

# Crocs | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FQP3r6PeyZFYiBCF7s5Kw%252FCrocs-logo%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a896316-7453-4bb1-8a96-bcc3c1d22fde&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c692c48&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crocs#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Crocs, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crocs#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crocs#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crocs#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FXx2ZNloO2B7zM3z00zwe%252Fcrocsmonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf19cce6-51c2-4751-9371-cf171ee817b1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1824c38b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crocs#guest-mode)

Guest mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F6yYd5MgFAT2W8MV2Rw4i%252Fguestcrocs.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8495468c-480d-448a-b9b9-d559f3c10792&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bda30c44&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor your desired items. When an item restocks, your monitor mode tasks will ping your running watch tasks (Guest mode) tasks to atc and checkout
        
    *   **Guest mode** is your normal checkout mode and will use guest checkout
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and residentials will both work
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **Product** **URL** and how do I get them?
    
    *   The URL is a link that identifies the item you would like to run. Ex. [https://www.crocs.com/p/fortnite-x-crocs-classic-clog-battle-bus/210495.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.crocs.com/p/fortnite-x-crocs-classic-clog-battle-bus/210495.html)
        
    
*   What is **Size**?
    
    *   Select your desired size from the dropdown options
        
    
*   What is **QTY**?
    
    *   Enter the product quantity you wish to checkout. A safe QTY to use is 1 but you can increase this
        
    
*   What is **Color**?
    
    *   This is where you enter the color name. Ex. `Blue Multi` for the URL above
        
    
*   What is **Discount**?
    
    *   If you have a disocunt code, you can enter it here
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment between 4000 - 6000
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   **Watch tasks** and **non-watch tasks** are different
        
        *   **Non-watch tasks** will be monitoring the site, which means that it will be using proxies. When a product restocks, this same task will atc and checkout
            
        *   **Watch tasks** are "watching" your **Monitor Mode** tasks waiting for a product you're running for to restock. Your **watch tasks** will add to cart and checkout when its pinged from a **Monitor Mode** task
            
        
    
*   What is **Use Rakuten?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [Rakuten guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-rakuten-cashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    
*   What is **Use TopCashBack?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [TopCashBack guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    

[PreviousCostco US/CAchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca)
[NextCrunchyrollchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll)

Last updated 3 months ago

# BestBuy CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1000logos.net%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2016%2F10%2FBest-Buy-logo-2-500x281.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b36e3e2e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on BestBuy CA, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#best-buy-ca-task-setup)

Best Buy CA Task Setup


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#guest-mode)

Guest Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FxkYSVByXxQvks1Zo1tdG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D990e6abd-9e64-4c44-98b4-547f960c7b26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8c3fcf1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgQXzQ6LX2Aiadw6qV3vO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab169241-b2c1-44db-b18d-09bc397cc254&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f75736ba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#guest-mode-1)

Guest Mode

Guest mode is used for checkout tasks. It can be paired with monitor mode to only run when your monitor task detects that an item is in stock. Guest mode tasks will get a list of surrounding stores based on profiles before going into waiting for monitor ping. If a monitor task picks up a store that matches that list, it will ping and begin the checkout process.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#monitor-mode-1)

Monitor Mode

Currently, only in-store pickup monitor is supported. Monitor mode will monitor local stores around a set radius based on the user's profile. When using monitor tasks, it'll ping every task that shares the same store as the normal task.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#profile)

Profile

Select the appropriate profile you would like to use to checkout.

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#proxies-1)

Proxies


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

DCs and ISPs are the best proxies for Best Buy CA due to speed. Residentials also work but may have high usage. Best Buy CA is pretty strict in terms of IP Ranges, so only Canada-based proxies have been known to work on a consistent basis.

If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
 for high quality ISP and Residential proxies

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#sku)

SKU

A SKU is an item-specific identification ID that is unique to a single item. Best Buy CA SKUs tend to be near the end of the link. For example, in the link "[https://www.bestbuy.ca/en-ca/product/apple-airpods-max-over-ear-noise-cancelling-bluetooth-headphones-silver/15204589arrow-up-right](https://www.bestbuy.ca/en-ca/product/apple-airpods-max-over-ear-noise-cancelling-bluetooth-headphones-silver/15204589)
", the SKU is 15204589.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#delays)

Delays

For Best Buy CA, any delay between 3000 and 5000 is good for running 24/7.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#quantity)

Quantity

A good quantity to use is 1. Most hyped items have a 1-per-cart limit and possibly a 1-per-person or household limit. Most orders won't be able to place if there is more than 1 quantity in the cart.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#fulfillment-options)

Fulfillment Options

There are currently two fulfillment options you can utilize:

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#pickup)

Pickup

Will randomly select a store at your pre-defined pickup radius.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#shipping)

Shipping

Will deliver the item to your shipping address set out in your profile.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#pickup-radius)

Pickup Radius

Specify the distance from your profile postal code to have your item picked up in-store. If this value is left blank, the default value will be 25 miles. Note that the units are in miles and not kilometers.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#watch-task)

Watch Task

Select this checkbox if you want to utilize monitor mode.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#otp-number)

OTP Number

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#voipms)

VOIPMS

Select Use VOIPMS if you would like to use an auto-SMS service. Please ensure your API email and API password (different than your login password) are set up properly in settings as seen below. See below for a quick guide on how to set up and fund your VOIP MS account. Note that you can use a maximum of 1 VOIP.MS number per task. You will need to purchase additional numbers if you intend to run multiple profiles.

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCBEUfzFeHCRfvBqQp5rz%252FVOI%2520CA.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4150ad24-13cc-49ed-9bb2-4462cfd6ed0e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d130824e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#manual)

Manual

Please specify a phone number to send the OTP code to. If no number is set, the phone number attached to your profile will be used instead.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#otp-code)

OTP Code

If the item requested requires an OTP code, an automatic harvester should pop up. If this is not the case, manually open up a captcha harvester to input your OTP code followed by submit.

*   OTP Number - VOIPMS
    
    *   Select Use VOIPMS? If you would like to use an Auto SMS Service. Please ensure your API email and API Password (Different than your Login Password) are setup properly in settings as seen below. See below for a quick guide on how to setup and fund your VOIP MS account.
        
    *   NOTE: You can use a maximum of 1 VOIP.MS Number per Task. You will need to purchase additional Numbers if you intend to run multiple profiles
        
    
    *   You will also need to enable your Local IP Address to poll messages from VoipMS as well as Enable API
        
    
    Note: This configuration page can be found [herearrow-up-right](https://voip.ms/m/api.php)
    .
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgankyYYBofbyH6vIY1CM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f1b6950-e2fe-4b2f-bfac-faf7796d0289&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3271c22&sv=2)
    
*   OTP Number - Manual
    
    *   Please specify a phone number to send the OTP Code to, if no number is set, the phone number attached to your profile will be used instead.
        
    
*   What do I do if the item requested requires OTP Code?
    
    *   An automatic harvester should pop up, if this is not the case manually open up a Captcha harvester to input your OTP code followed by submit
        
        ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F430568463%2F6ec90f37f3859dc5eb51cf61%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10d7eba5&sv=2)
        
    
*   [hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy-ca#how-to-setup-voipms-if-you-need-a-canadian-did-number-with-sms-mms-support-you-can-purchase-it-easil)
    
    How to setup VOIPMS - if you need a Canadian DID number with SMS/MMS support, you can purchase it easily on VoIP.ms. Follow the steps below to get started:
    
    
    -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
*   **Step 1: Create and fund your account**
    
    *   If you don't already have an account, create one on the VoIP.ms website. Once you've created your account, make sure it is funded with sufficient credit to cover the cost of your DID number(s).
        
    
*   **Step 2: Go to the DID Numbers tab and Order DIDs**
    
    *   After logging in to your account, navigate to the DID Numbers tab and select "Order DIDs." This will bring up a search page where you can select the parameters for your DID number.
        
    
*   **Step 3: Search for Local Canadian Numbers with SMS/MMS Support**
    
    *   Search for Canadian numbers with SMS/MMS support by selecting the appropriate filters. Look for a green cellphone icon next to the number to ensure that it supports SMS/MMS.
        
    
*   **Step 4: Choose the Per Minute Plan**
    
    *   Select the per-minute plan, which costs 85 cents per number per month. You won't have to worry about the per-minute cost since you won't be using the number for phone calls.
        
    
*   **Step 5: Choose any POP server**
    
    *   You can choose any POP server. Select the one closest to you.
        
    
*   **Step 6: Manage your DIDs**
    
    *   After ordering your DID number, go to the Manage DIDs subtab under the DID Numbers main tab. Look for the number you just purchased and click the orange edit button.
        
    
*   **Step 7: Enable SMS/MMS Support**
    
    *   Scroll down to the "SMS" section and check the "Enable SMS/MMS" box. The fees for SMS are extremely cheap.
        
    
*   **Step 8: Enable API Acces**s
    
    *   Go to [https://voip.ms/m/api.phparrow-up-right](https://voip.ms/m/api.php)
         to enable API access. Set your API password as well as your local IP address that Stellar AIO will run on.
        
    

If you're receiving an error message you can look here in the [Status Codes article](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/status-codes-and-troubleshooting/how-do-i-run-stellaraio-with-logs)

# Canon US & CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FZkGtmyjM88EvVBZm92qH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc7dd303-9da5-46ab-9553-acef476a8979&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3779bed0&sv=2)

Our Canon US & CA module supports guest checkout and is designed for monitoring and purchasing high-demand Canon products that frequently restock in limited quantities. Because Canon drops often occur without notice and require captcha solving at checkout, Stellar uses a monitor-to-checkout workflow, watch task logic and flexible proxy support to help secure items efficiently. This module is best suited for cameras, lenses, accessories and limited-stock Canon products across both the United States and Canada.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Canon US, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Before you start, double-check that your billing and shipping information lines up with the profile you’ll be using.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwIWIY0Rob5HgWn6JzpZ0%252Fcanonmon.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D852e3f71-d38b-471c-a6bb-4eb91116bbb5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=baaddcd2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca#normal-mode)

Normal Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FuOWgwaS9pKgjUzaiBnxI%252Fcanonnormal.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b1e921d-fd74-40ed-85e4-614065fa813d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f75756aa&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor your desired items. When an item restocks, your monitor mode tasks will ping your running watch tasks (Normal mode) tasks to checkout
        
    *   **Normal mode** is your normal checkout mode task (guest checkout)
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and residentials will both work. Ideally you'd want to use ISPs for monitor mode and residentials for normal mode
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   Where do I find **Product URL**?
    
    *   Every product will have it's own unique Product URL. Ex. [https://www.usa.canon.com/shop/p/powershot-g7-x-mark-iii?color=Black&type=Newarrow-up-right](https://www.usa.canon.com/shop/p/powershot-g7-x-mark-iii?color=Black&type=New)
        
        *   You can find out any product information from your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Monitoring Delay: Experiment around 6000
        
    *   Delay: (normal mode) Expeirment around 3000
        
    *   Reset Delay: 10000 or less
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   A good default to use is 1, but if the listing on the site allows for multiple in one cart then feel free to increase the QTY. You can find out product Max Qty from your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
        
    
*   What is **Captcha Provider**?
    
    *   Captchas are required to be solved to checkout items from this site. Here you can select the method you want to use to solve captchas
        
        *   Bot will allow you to solve captchas using our [captcha harvester](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
             in bot
            
        *   AYCD will allow you to use this [AYCD toolbox](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
             to solve captchas
            
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   **Watch tasks** and **non-watch tasks** are different
        
        *   **Non-watch tasks** will be monitoring the site, which means that it will be using proxies. When a product restocks, this same task will atc and checkout
            
        *   **Watch tasks** are "watching" your **Monitor Mode** tasks waiting for a product you're running for to restock. Your **watch tasks** will add to cart and checkout when its pinged from a **Monitor Mode** task
            
        
    *   Your Monitor mode tasks will ping/notify your running Normal mode watch tasks when the product has restocked so they'll attempt to atc and checkout
        
    
*   What is the **Task Limit**?
    
    *   Currently at 50 but may change at any time
        
    

[PreviousChaos Cardschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards)
[NextCanon UKchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-uk)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca#profiles)
    
*   [Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca#proxies)
    
*   [Monitor Mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-us-and-ca#monitor-mode)
