# Frasers | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdSIF2kIkbV4YSYTHhVm2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8af5ee92-212b-4d68-a284-4245129914a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb256b59&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/frasers#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Frasers, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/frasers#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/frasers#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FfkfWqAOTcOORHayNlZog%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a2439a0-3df7-4fdc-93c5-7a41941d244c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7fd54545&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/frasers#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FifnCkmTYDnVIEt64XVBk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e797808-47af-4a4e-8dac-c3df5fcf3800&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6383dc41&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will check for product availability and ping your checkout tasks when the product comes into stock
        
    *   **Normal mode** will add to cart and checkout the product you input
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Both ISPs and Resis should work, try ISPs first on an in stock item with false payment information. If you receive any proxy related errors, switch to residentials
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is **Site**?
    
    *   Click the dropdown and select the site you're wanting to purchase products from
        
    
*   What is Product URL?
    
    *   For example, [`https://www.houseoffraser.co.uk/brand/pokemon/pokemon-tcg-charizard-ex-super-premium-collection-701234#colcode=70123499`arrow-up-right](https://www.houseoffraser.co.uk/brand/pokemon/pokemon-tcg-charizard-ex-super-premium-collection-701234#colcode=70123499)
        
    
*   What is **Size**?
    
    *   Select the size you'd like to purchase. You can select multiple sizes in your tasks so if one is OOS then it'll attempt the other sizes
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
         for quantity recommendations as different products have different quantity restrictions
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   **Monitoring Delay**: We recommend to use delays around 5000 depending on the quality of your proxies
        
        *   It's required to have at least one monitor task per product if you're choosing your checkout task to be a watch task
            
        
    *   **Reset Delay**: 10000 or less
        
    *   **Delay for checkout tasks**: 5000 or less
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousFootsiteschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/footsites)
[NextFunkoShopchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop)

# HobbyCraft | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fen%2Fthumb%2Fb%2Fb4%2FHobbycraft_logo_2011.svg%2F1280px-Hobbycraft_logo_2011.svg.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94a272cb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbycraft#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbycraft#shipping-home-delivery)

Shipping (Home delivery)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FfWUmlS2NE8tVBeZ1pFS8%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37940c78-7216-4b87-aa0b-0b3f3e4c7c6a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=992dfe83&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbycraft#collect-in-store-collection)

Collect (In-store collection)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fmr6CzR37cmT7luMO5bsS%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1893f958-83e0-485a-a50d-fd1f55de2a96&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=157a7e36&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbycraft#monitor-home-delivery-monitor)

Monitor (Home delivery monitor)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FnW2XrFgQnQT69iFkPGLI%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c57cde3-1126-4cf8-ac9d-1bae92f44c1a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f6377c9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbycraft#monitor-collect-in-store-collection-monitor)

Monitor-Collect (In-store collection monitor)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F1SWUrxZSiIwuuFA2BLIL%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1882ec85-6c16-4e1e-9891-3ed56cb4f3a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d34e965&sv=2)

*   Which mode do I use?
    
    *   Shipping mode - is your checkout task to be used for home delivery checkout flow, select watch task to pair with Monitor
        
    *   Collect - is your checkout task to be used for in-store collection checkout flow
        
    *   Monitor - is to be paired with shipping mode, for home delivery monitoring
        
    *   Monitor-collect - is to be paired with Collect mode, for in-store collection monitoring
        
    
*   What does profile mean?
    
    *   Select a profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of proxies should I use?
    
    *   For monitor instore and delivery, most ISP’s work. You can test and if you see proxy bans, you’ll have to switch to another provider or consider residentials (this however does consume data)
        
    *   For checkout tasks (in-store and delivery), use high quality residentials or ISP’s. Residentials preferred.
        
        *   Proxies
            
            ISP proxies - recommended for monitor mode (running longer periods of time). Can also run half checkout tasks with ISP
            
            Residential proxies - recommended for checkout mode when using watch task + monitor
            
        
    
*   What is the product SKU?
    
    *   For example [https://www.hobbycraft.co.uk/warhammer-age-of-sigmar-aggradon-lancers/6755271000.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.hobbycraft.co.uk/warhammer-age-of-sigmar-aggradon-lancers/6755271000.html)
        , the SKU is the numbers at the end - 6755271000
        
    
*   What is QTY?
    
    *   The number of items you want in one order
        
    
*   What is Delay?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error. If you’re running long periods of time on monitor modes, start between 5-10k delays, and adjust on proxy errors. I.e start on 5k, adjust to 6k if you observe errors.
        
        *   For checkout tasks, 1-2k
            
        
    
*   What is a Postal Code?
    
    *   Your postcode for collection from stores, it will try to cart a stock at the nearest store to your postcode
        
    
*   What is Pickup Radius?
    
    *   The max distance in miles that bot will search for stores based on your postcode
        
    
*   What is reset delay?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product again after it has detected stock. Recommend 3-5k
        
    
*   What is a watch task?
    
    *   Watch task is recommended when using monitor mode. The watch task will put the checkout task “to sleep”, and only when the monitor triggers stock, will the checkout task then attempt the checkout flow.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbycraft#important-notes)

Important Notes

Guest checkout only.

Ensure proxies are UK based, and ideally try and use ISP’s, especially for running over long periods of time - always recommended to test setup with an instock item.

Product SKUs: the numbers taken from the end of the URL, [https://www.hobbycraft.co.uk/warhammer-age-of-sigmar-aggradon-lancers/6755271000.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.hobbycraft.co.uk/warhammer-age-of-sigmar-aggradon-lancers/6755271000.html)
 i.e 6755271000

[NextHobbyLobbychevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Boxlunch | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.cookielaw.org%2Flogos%2F1da486d5-b07a-4ce9-9661-f95f7d55d0c9%2Fa2705db7-d975-4190-bc1a-b1fe47820c6f%2F0fc4eb6b-14ff-4a88-aec2-4e3f2be225bd%2Fbl-full.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b562a8af&sv=2)

Our BoxLunch module supports guest checkout only, making it one of the simpler and more straightforward modules in Stellar. BoxLunch typically releases products on a true first come first serve basis with no queue system, meaning speed and clean proxies are key. This module is ideal for collectibles, apparel and limited run exclusives that sell out quickly upon release or during small restocks.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Boxlunch, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch#test-task)

**Test Task**

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profile, account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch#adding-sessions)

**Adding Sessions**

To add your BoxLunch accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Sessions** tab > Click on **BoxLunch**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FcB653GF4peXRsFBDvXRd%252FBoxLunch%2520Session.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c09527d-5778-4052-8794-1b824e297050&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7104a517&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Session** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FVRlw3kTNCpVGEHDPkDDY%252FAdd%2520Session_.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd731ce7-e9a3-4f87-b2b3-d75d0e1e6d5f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=972807ff&sv=2)

1.  Enter your BoxLunch account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FIWS9BreZ3McifsSBlsRn%252FAcc%2520Setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f622e22-97ee-4b02-90d4-3a959bb191f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50245ba2&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch#task-strategy-and-timing)

Task Strategy & Timing

**How Many Monitor Tasks Should I Create?**

*   Run **1 Monitor task per SKU**.
    
*   You can run multiple Monitor tasks if you want redundancy, but it’s **not required** and usually unnecessary.
    
*   Monitor tasks are lightweight and can run 24/7.
    

**Recommended:** 1 Monitor task per SKU is sufficient for most users.

* * *

**How Many Checkout Tasks Per Account?**

*   **Strictly 1 checkout task for each SKU per Boxlunch account.**
    
*   Running more than one checkout task on the same account can cause:
    
    *   Account locks
        
    *   Checkout failures
        
    *   Login/session instability
        
    

**Rule:** 1 account = 1 checkout task (no exceptions).

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch#boxlunch-task-overview)

**BoxLunch Task Overview**

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fd51YwnshcAH7cRG5O9an%252Fbl%2520normal.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57d82d85-5beb-4749-aa1e-e362acfad370&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc63bea0&sv=2)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FB2MMz8YOBIbNanDlQaB7%252Fbl%2520monitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b9569ea-36a8-4cdb-9134-1327fa8e50d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=642b904e&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** uses guest checkout to purchase items, or has the ability to checkout via account checkout
        
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to monitor products on BoxLunch website for restocks. Your Watcher tasks will then notify your Normal tasks when your product restocked
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Recommended to run a mix of ISPs and Resis
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   How do I find the **PID**?
    
    *   Go to the product page and at the end of the URL you can find the PID
        
        *   Example: [arrow-up-right](https://www.adafruit.com/product/50)
            [https://www.boxlunch.com/product/stranger-things-hellfire-club-raglan-t-shirt/19995072.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.boxlunch.com/product/stranger-things-hellfire-club-raglan-t-shirt/19995072.html)
            
        *   The **PID** is 19995072
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   **Monitor Delays**: We recommend around 5000
        
    *   **Checkout Delays**: We recommend around 1000
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
         for quantity recommendations as different products may have different purchase limits set by the site
        
        *   Stellar does not automatically adjust the quantity if you set a number higher than what's allowed
            
        
    
*   What is **Session**?
    
    *   If you would like to use account checkout, select a [session](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/boxlunch#adding-accounts)
        
    
*   What is the **Watch Task?** checkbox?
    
    *   The **Watch Task** option allows your checkout task (e.g., Normal mode) to work together with a **Monitor mode task**. Here's how it works:
        
        *   If you check this box, your **checkout task** will not monitor for restocks directly. Instead, it will wait for a **Monitor mode task** (with the same SKU) to detect a restock
            
            *   Once the Monitor task detects the restock, it will "ping" the checkout (with the same SKU) task to run. The checkout task will then add the item to your cart and proceed to checkout
                
            
        
        When using the **Watch Task** option:
        
        1.  Start your checkout task. It will display the message: **"Waiting for Monitor Ping."** This means it's ready and set up correctly
            
        2.  When the Monitor task detects a restock, it will automatically trigger the checkout task (with the same SKU) to run
            
        
        If you leave the **Watch Task** checkbox **unchecked**, the checkout task will act independently. It will monitor the SKU itself, add the item to your cart, and checkout directly
        
    

circle-exclamation

Using Watch Task is highly recommended for restocks because it allows the Monitor task to do the heavy lifting. This improves performance and helps avoid overloading the site.

*   What is **Use Rakuten?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [Rakuten guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-rakuten-cashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    
*   What is **Use TopCashback?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [Topcashback Guidearrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    

[PreviousBooksAMillionchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/booksamillion)
[NextChaos Cardschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards)

# Fanatics | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flogowik.com%2Fcontent%2Fuploads%2Fimages%2Ffanatics-sports-retailer6202.jpg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3d4cbef&sv=2)

[_Adding Sessions_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fanatics#adding-sessions)

[_Task Overview_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fanatics#task-overview)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fanatics#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Fanatics, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.
> 
> **Important:** DSG does **not** support 3DS cards, use a payment method that does not require 3D Secure.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fanatics#adding-sessions)

Adding Sessions

To add your Fanatics accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Sessions** tab > **Sessions** > Click on **Fanatics >** Click on **Add Session**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fmb1rmAN6GbAnS4Rtg5vi%252Ffanaticssession.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e3f3f3f-a977-4e1f-a50e-9738b479864d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47e2f367&sv=2)

1.  Enter your account email and password and click **Save**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FfBthl8s1Kf1Va9FmVuK7%252Fsessioninfo.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87502b8a-5da3-4a87-b709-6227a677ae7d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb669be5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fanatics#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fanatics#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FrqxsoeFIAdqtJluoThJs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8db385e7-e0c2-49e0-9251-483530a4989a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e78cc065&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fanatics#checkout-mode)

**Checkout Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fv6OZt5ybni5B6T04zRCi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db556c453-7357-4478-bfac-2a9c8a3d637f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e913fd9&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to check for product availability. These monitor tasks will ping/notify your running Checkout mode watch tasks that the item is in stock
        
    *   **Checkout mode** is used to purchase products that you entered and selected for. Checkout mode will use the profile's to match it to an account in the account section of StellarAIO
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   For monitor and checkout proxy, ISPs/DCs should be used for speed. If they are getting banned we recommend using residential proxies to avoid them
        
    
*   What **Event URL** do I use?
    
    *   Use the raffle page URL in this section. For example: [https://www.fanatics.com/mlb/boston-red-sox/boston-red-sox-nike-2021-postseason-dugout-pullover-hoodie-navy/o-3498+t-25663097+p-71042959796+z-9-3767159932?\_ref=p-TLP:m-GRID:i-r0c0:po-0arrow-up-right](https://www.fanatics.com/mlb/boston-red-sox/boston-red-sox-nike-2021-postseason-dugout-pullover-hoodie-navy/o-3498+t-25663097+p-71042959796+z-9-3767159932?_ref=p-TLP:m-GRID:i-r0c0:po-0)
        
    
*   What **Password** do I use?
    
    *   This section allows you to set the password of the accounts you are making, this can be anything as long as it satisfies the Fanatics password requirement (Must be 8 - 20 characters)
        
    
*   What **Quantity** do I use?
    
    *   Fanatics may have quantity limits for certain hyped products (if so, set it to those). Overall it is recommended to use 1
        
    
*   What is **Size**?
    
    *   From the dropdown options you can select one size per task or select `Random`
        
    
*   What is **Monitoring Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds before retrying when an item is back in stock. `4500` is OK which would be 4.5 seconds
        
    
*   What is **Discount**?
    
    *   If you have a discount code, you can enter it in this field
        
    
*   What is **Cheapest Shipping?** box?
    
    *   Check this box if you'd like to purchase your product with the cheapest shipping option available

[NextFiveBelowchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fivebelow)

# Barnes & Noble | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSP1F0CK5W1T4ahzOsglS%252FBarnes-Noble-Logo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72e80990-becd-40ea-bfba-cddedb507af4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=242df25c&sv=2)

Our Barnes & Noble module supports both guest checkout and account based checkout that follows a true first come first serve release structure with no queue system. Because products frequently sell out within seconds during popular drops, speed and stable proxies are essential for success. This module is best suited for books, exclusives, collectibles and limited edition items that release or restock without warning.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#quick-start-recommended-setup)

**Quick Start (Recommended Setup)**

_(For members who want a fast setup without reading everything)_

*   Create a checkout **Profile** with billing, shipping and payment info
    
*   (Optional) Add Barnes & Noble accounts under **Identities → Accounts**
    
*   Create **Monitor Mode** tasks for each product URL you want
    
*   Run matching **Normal Mode** checkout tasks with **Watch Task enabled**
    
*   Use **ISP or Residential proxies** (both work well)
    
*   Set delays around **4000 ms**
    
*   Use **guest checkout** if you don’t select an account
    
*   Enable **Endless Mode** only if you want repeated checkouts
    
*   Before major drops, run a **test task** on an in stock item
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Barnes & Noble, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#barnes-and-noble-accounts-optional)

Barnes & Noble Accounts (Optional)

> Store your accounts in Stellar -> Identities

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#test-task)

Test Task

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profile, account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#adding-accounts)

Adding Accounts

To add your Barnes & Noble accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Identities** > Accounts > Click on **BarnesAndNoble**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FeXFmjYAyfMOjbTsOqlcD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf90371a-aede-4820-a3aa-1f087f9083c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=504c65d9&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Account** button
    
2.  Enter your account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYVMZWJvHRBc4KhxCPHgZ%252FAcc%2520Setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45cb5378-4a49-4c51-af28-14e011e3d62c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb0ec3fa&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#mass-import-accounts)

Mass Import Accounts

Have a lot of accounts and want to import them into Stellar fast and easy? No problem!

1.  In bot, navigate to **Sessions** > Accounts > Click **BarnesAndNoble**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FY4KAGhNBa7gwvsrpA35A%252FBarnes%2520_Acc.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bdbc83e-36bd-4687-b437-1ba28339302e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f094f46a&sv=2)

1.  Click **Mass Import Accounts** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FB02LeuBlnB8cpmtNOTn1%252FMass%2520Import.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2966528-4b9b-4692-b580-a0af9b970984&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0dddc46&sv=2)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FOXCflF7EY3KamYxzaZwN%252FMass%2520Import%2520Setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43f4ccd4-877a-4f0f-a87d-f10399538f3e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d3f1b38&sv=2)

1.  Enter your accounts emails and passwords in the format `email:password`
    
    *   For example `[[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) :stellar123 [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) :stellar123$ [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) :stellar1234 [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) :stellar1237 [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) :stellar1230`
        
    
2.  Click **Save**
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/barnes-and-noble#barnes-and-noble-task-overview)

**Barnes & Noble Task Overview**

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F9zIF7dNVdHWpB0U6Zz57%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8116b4c-9a63-47cf-a6ca-0cbd508716f5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d4da777&sv=2)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F2JecFhqudh4enktamMK6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30808b92-f3ac-490f-ac39-d76585c933c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65fd4aca&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal Mode** will use your profile to guest checkout products if you don't select an account
        
    *   **Monitor Mode** will check for product availability regularly. Once stock is detected, it will ping/notify your running normal mode tasks with the same URL (watch task must be enabled)
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   Which **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and Resis are both OK
        
    
*   How do I find the **URL**?
    
    *   **URL** is the product URL of the item you want to checkout
        
        *   For example, [https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/pokemon-trading-card-game-sword-shield-ultra-premium-collection-charizard-panini/1142777799?ean=0097712558134arrow-up-right](https://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/pokemon-trading-card-game-sword-shield-ultra-premium-collection-charizard-panini/1142777799?ean=0097712558134)
            
        
    
*   What's **Product Quantity**?
    
    *   Enter the quantity of the item you'd like to checkout
        
    
*   What's **Account**?
    
    *   Select an account you want to use when purchasing products
        
        *   If you don't select an account, it'll be guest checkout
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Delays around 4000 are OK
        
    
*   What is **Endless Mode**?
    
    *   If you have this box checked the task will restart after a successful checkout. Ideally you would want to use this if you want to continue purchasing the product until it goes out of stock
        
    *   If you have this box unchecked the task will stop completely after a successful checkout
        
    
*   What is **Endless Limit**?
    
    *   Enter the max number of checkouts with Endless Mode enabled
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task**?
    
    *   Checkout task waits for Monitor task to ping
        
    *   Easier on proxies
        
    *   Faster response time

# HobbyLobby | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdOHyOvi0zWS4ptgjlzB8%252FHobby-Lobby.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8d2bec3-a598-4206-b19e-cdcf10316fc3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edf31f30&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on HobbyLobby, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fvrmwd5Bnat2XGmBdrYqk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3a161de-eddd-4de1-a652-fc6dcca37436&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eed6f193&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby#guest-mode)

Guest Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FchOFvl89flP6Na2J8ME0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e3e369c-b132-47b4-9af9-73c8862445c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=82a704a3&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor** mode allows you monitor product stock and will automatically notify your running Guest mode watch tasks to start the checkout process
        
    *   **Guest** mode allows you to automatically checkout product via guest checkout
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   All types of proxies from DCs to ISPs to Resis. Must be US proxies
        
    
*   What's **URL**?
    
    *   Paste the product URL here. For example [`https://www.hobbylobby.com/Christmas/Home-Decor-Pillows/Advent-Countdown-Calendars/Light-Up-Rotating-Advent-Calendar/p/81151405`arrow-up-right](https://www.hobbylobby.com/Christmas/Home-Decor-Pillows/Advent-Countdown-Calendars/Light-Up-Rotating-Advent-Calendar/p/81151405?queryId=34bdae59086759c1db24ac75bc6eecca)
        
    
*   What **Delay** should I use?
    
    *   Between 4000-6000 is OK
        
    
*   What **Quantity** do I use?
    
    *   There may have quantity limits for certain hyped products (if so, set it to those) Overall it is recommended to use 1
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the product, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousHobbyCraftchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbycraft)
[NextHome Depotchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Preliminary Checklist](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby#preliminary-checklist)
    
*   [Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby#task-overview)
    
*   [Monitor Mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby#monitor-mode)
    
*   [Guest Mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby#guest-mode)
    

Was this helpful?

# GameStop CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1000logos.net%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2022%2F10%2FGameStop-logo-500x281.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f530b09&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop-ca#gamestop-ca)

GameStop CA

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop-ca#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on GameStop CA, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

GameStop CA can utilize any ISP Proxy, or Resi.

*   Keep delays above 6000 if you want to run 24/7. Ideally higher. This is heavily dependant on the amount of proxies you decide to dedicate to the website. You can lower at your discretion.
    

The following explains how to create a task under the GameStop CA module:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop-ca#guest-mode)

Guest Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FB8sCRlL5ok1tVdSgKfWp%252FGME%2520CA%2520Guest.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e133121-c825-41fe-a78f-57fdb217cf9b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45a92a2f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop-ca#account-mode)

Account Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F0bCn9fXEMHTg3OdjK2Zr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D819aed71-17be-4a46-ae13-e5ddba0f06ae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f4e0994&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop-ca#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FeyqFSw3qpHBjVrDmEP6w%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D760c34c2-f931-430c-bed8-1b0a29fda5bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37ff535c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop-ca#account-gen-mode)

Account Gen Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F6h9go139nha8GTFAvOt9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbcd0b735-3f66-4ac9-9517-f8c454299de3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50313504&sv=2)

Uses profile email to create account

There are several drop down lists that you will be presented with.

**Mode:** Normal **Profile:** Choose the profile you have created in Stellar

**Monitor Proxy:** Use an ISP or Resi proxy, preferably Canadian

**Checkout Proxy:** Use a ISP or Resi Proxy**,** preferably Canadian

**SKU**: Located on the product page, see example below `https://www.gamestop.ca/Toys-Collectibles/Games/919040/the-nightmare-before-christmas-best-of-action-figures-series-4-easter-bunny-with-igor` the product code for this product is not ~919040~, its actually `786841`

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F8HwapLBmfMpWPSpVUu5E%252Fgmeca%2520product1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b4e1c0d-775b-4e6f-b1af-cbb9558ceea4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27451140&sv=2)

**Qty:** This is the item quantity, most hype items will only allow you to check out 1, however this is dependent on the item you are hoping to purchase, check the website for the limits.

**Qty Per SKU:** Enter the quantity you'd like to purchase for each SKU using comma seperation without spaces. Ex. `1,2,3`

**Delay:** This is highly dependent on how many proxies you own, if running 24/7 on gamestop.ca, it is recommended to go no less than 6000 delay, unless you have a lot of proxies to work with.

**Minimum Cart Quantity:** Set the minimum number of items that must be added to the cart before checkout is attempted. If the cart contains fewer items than the number you specify, the task will not proceed to checkout.

**Account:** If you would like to use an account to check out, you can select it here. If you want to use guest checkout, leave this blank.

**Start Time:** Select the date and time you would like to start the task.

**End Time:** Select the date and time you would like to end the task.

**Tasks:** On the bottom right of the **New Task** creation menu, you can choose how many Tasks to create at one time.

[PreviousGameStopchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop)
[NextHobbyCraftchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbycraft)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Currys | Stellar

**Index** [Task Modes](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#task-modes)
 [Normal Mode Setup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#normal-mode-setup)
 [Monitor Mode Setup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#monitor-mode-setup)
 [Important Notes](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#important-notes)
 [Tips for Success](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#tips-for-success)

This guide will help you create tasks for Currys UK using Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Currys, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

circle-info

Currys UK supports **guest checkouts only**—accounts are not supported.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#task-modes)

**Task Modes**

*   **Normal Mode**: Use this for standard product checkout.
    
*   **Monitor Mode**: Use this to monitor product availability and it'll notify/ping your running Normal mode watch tasks to checkout when the product restocks.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#normal-mode-setup)

**Normal Mode Setup**

1.  **Navigate to the Task Creation Screen**
    
    *   Open Stellar
        
    *   Go to Tasks Tab
        
    *   Click on the green `+` symbol to create a new task group
        
    *   Search "Currys" or scroll down to it
        
    *   Enter a group name (Usually best to organize task groups by using the product name you want to run for as the group name)
        
    *   Click on the Create Task button towards the top
        
    *   Select Normal mode
        
    
2.  **Fill in Task Details**:
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F392svn7WYHiaINN4Jtx5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68fb4cdf-d843-4a59-a628-0800d5ac3755&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c24d42c6&sv=2)

*   **Mode**: Select **Normal** mode.
    
*   **Profile**: Choose the [profile](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/profile-overview)
     you want to use.
    
*   **Checkout Proxy**: Assign a [proxy](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
     to use during checkout.
    
*   **Product SKU**: Enter the product’s SKU (found on the product page URL).
    
*   **Product Quantity**: Enter the number of units you want to purchase.
    
*   **Delay**: Set a delay in milliseconds (e.g., 2000 ms for 2 seconds).
    
*   **Optional Features**:
    
    *   Enable [TopCashback](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         if you want to earn cashback on your purchase.
        
    *   Enable **Watch Task?** if you want your task to watch/wait for a Monitor mode task to ping/notify it. This is recommended to use for restocks and your Normal mode task must be started and say "Waiting for Monitor Ping"
        
    

1.  **Set Task Quantity**: Ensure the quantity at the bottom is accurate (defaults to 1).
    
2.  Click **Create** to save your task.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#monitor-mode-setup)

**Monitor Mode Setup**

1.  **Navigate to the Task Creation Screen**
    
    *   Click on the green `+` symbol to create a new task group
        
    *   Search "Currys" or scroll down to it
        
    *   Enter a group name (Usually best to organize task groups by using the product name you want to run for as the group name)
        
    *   Click on the Create Task button towards the top
        
    *   Select Monitor mode
        
    
2.  **Fill in Task Details**:
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F62Ht0zPxEFED4aP83dvH%252Fcurrys%2520monitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ec32b19-5ac1-4506-a1dd-89314e0b614e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e2f548a&sv=2)

*   **Mode**: Select **Monitor** mode.
    
*   **Profile**: [Profile](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/profile-overview)
     isnt used for Monitor mode so you can just select any profile here, doesnt matter
    
*   **Checkout Proxy**: Assign a [proxy](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
     for monitoring and checkout.
    
*   **Product SKU**: Enter the product’s SKU.
    
*   **Monitoring Delay**: Set a monitoring delay (e.g., 3000 ms for 3 seconds).
    
    *   For restocks around 8000 delay is recommended
        
    *   For releases around 3000 delay is recommended
        
    
*   **Reset Delay**: Set a reset delay so your task can monitor continuously even after the product comes in stock
    
    *   Around 5000 is recommended
        
    

1.  **Set Task Quantity**: Ensure the quantity at the bottom matches the desired number of units (defaults to 1).
    
2.  Click **Create** to save your task.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#important-notes)

**Important Notes**

*   **Guest Checkouts Only**: Currys does not support account logins. Ensure that your billing profiles are configured for guest checkout.
    
*   **Proxies**: Use [ISP proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
     for the best success rate. Ensure proxies are from the UK for optimal performance.
    
*   **Product SKUs**: The SKU is the unique identifier in the product URL (e.g., for `https://www.currys.co.uk/gbuk/product/12345678`, the SKU is `12345678`).
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#tips-for-success)

**Tips for Success**

*   **Timing**: Start tasks 1-2 minutes before the expected product drop/release time.
    
*   **Monitor Settings**: Fine-tune your monitoring delay based on how frequently the product restocks.
    

[PreviousCrunchyrollchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll)
[NextDicks Sporting Goodschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#proxies)
    
*   [Task Modes](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#task-modes)

*   [Monitor Mode Setup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#monitor-mode-setup)
    
*   [Important Notes](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#important-notes)
    
*   [Tips for Success](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys#tips-for-success)
    

Was this helpful?

# John Lewis | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FJjn5nhyO79ggYvUjQ6XL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D36eea770-5dfd-4c95-ad41-cc91619f1e56&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c47df2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/john-lewis#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on John Lewis, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/john-lewis#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/john-lewis#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FjDdvXG4KaZ1hGee4UhYA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f5a48c8-88cb-4208-99b9-203994a81057&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9bfd4b15&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/john-lewis#guest-mode)

Guest mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FWD8k8D3MUlhutUBN8Lpc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6860a043-ad6c-482a-bcfd-d524d13e09c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c481a5b2&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will check for product availability and ping your guest mode tasks when the product comes into stock
        
    *   **Guest mode** will add to cart and checkout the product you input
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Both ISPs and Resis should work, try ISPs first on an in stock item with false payment information. If you receive any errors, switch to residentials
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **SKU** and how do I get them?
    
    *   Look for the item you want to run for. An example link would be [https://www.johnlewis.com/american-tourister-take2cabin-casual-backpack-24l-raspberry-sorbet/p112529276arrow-up-right](https://www.johnlewis.com/american-tourister-take2cabin-casual-backpack-24l-raspberry-sorbet/p112529276)
         the SKU is `p112529276`
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   **Monitoring Delay**: We recommend to use delays around 5000 depending on the quality of your proxies
        
        *   It's required to have at least one monitor task per product if you're choosing your checkout task to be a watch task
            
        
    *   **Reset Delay**: 10000 or less
        
    *   **Delay for checkout tasks**: 5000 or less
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
         for quantity recommendations as different products have different quantity restrictions
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    
*   What is **Use TopCashback?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [Topcashback guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    

[PreviousIndigoCAchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/indigoca)
[NextKohlschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/kohls)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Preliminary Checklist](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/john-lewis#preliminary-checklist)
    
*   [Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/john-lewis#task-overview)
    
*   [Monitor mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/john-lewis#monitor-mode)

# Lids | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FF5bEfSClu9GCn71bcged%252F1200px-Lids_%28store%29_logo.svg.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98b65772-1113-4483-ae1a-7b20e3dda2e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9dc3b9dd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lids#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Lids, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lids#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lids#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F7zDk8wgabgappSxRsRoY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92c2ccca-78b6-4892-9712-be20f510c0f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13af3f00&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lids#checkout-mode)

Checkout Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FGFrTNZobXUh50BHqUNO8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea4519de-1471-4658-83fa-a8e8fc2a15cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8da094f7&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   Monitor mode is used to check for product availability
        
    *   Checkout mode uses guest checkout
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   All types of proxies from DCs to ISPs to Resis
        
    
*   What's **Event URL**?
    
    *   Paste the product/event URL here
        
    
*   What is **Size**?
    
    *   From the dropdown options you can select one size per task or select `Random`
        
    
*   What **Quantity** do I use?
    
    *   There may have quantity limits for certain hyped products (if so, set it to those) Overall it is recommended to use 1
        
    
*   What **Delay** should I use?
    
    *   Between 4000-6000 is OK
        
    
*   What is **Monitoring Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds before retrying when an item is back in stock. `4500` is OK which would be 4.5 seconds
        
    
*   What is **Discount**?
    
    *   If you have a discount code, you can enter it in this field
        
    
*   What is **Cheapest Shipping?** box?
    
    *   Check this box if you'd like to purchase your product with the cheapest shipping option available
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout

[NextLoweschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lowes)

# Chaos Cards | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FKffjCGzuH4Lvxw7oWE84%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb01cf5d-0749-4e86-a9b5-56846b6fc3aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a73b0cda&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Chaos cards make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – recommended for monitor, checkout, acc-generation
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Issues with checkout task, switch to residentials. Same if you’re generating large amounts of accounts at scale
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#accounts)

**Accounts**

> *   Accounts are required. Thankfully Stellar has an account-generation module.
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#task-overview)

Task Overview

To add your Chaos Cards sessions to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

*   In bot, navigate to **Identities** tab then click on **Chaos Cards**
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBl9Q9mAkKKL4KvSnhTUr%252FScreenshot%25202026-02-20%2520at%25209.12.38%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2565163f-4894-4efa-b753-a4fe3616b50a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed7844c&sv=2)
    
*   Click the green plus button next to the site name (pictured above) and create an account group. ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F3IGuqUkffFSdYfFSIjX0%252FScreenshot%25202026-02-20%2520at%25209.15.18%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D858bd79a-6d0d-4d05-8c5d-5fc1a4fbf198&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55592c6&sv=2)
    
*   Click **Add Session** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSxi7jWExkJvbs3evhkjZ%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520162343.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df444014f-ae56-4ff0-953e-9811a4f828c6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7b30c8c&sv=2)

*   Enter your Chaos Cards account email and password and press save.
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgIJptCsbZ9iZsXwhwthG%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520162536.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc968899a-ef22-4c2c-8d50-6ea1d785d7ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf2b838e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#chaos-cards-task-overview)

Chaos Cards Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fg2D0dyO5mvOuubJUzIth%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0dac4b91-709c-48f8-8186-69b266d5fffa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9584e2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#invite-mode)

**Invite Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FxuRpuGcRZvWWVrx0aZM6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D392cbc68-f601-449e-9f08-9f9bac181c89&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3962a869&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fc6Kp7rQZ2GTG1MJIIhsY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68ef2995-fc35-4e6d-ac4e-758c65391186&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fec56c0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#account-gen)

**Account-Gen**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FnUW2Gnca59jSalGXFTkp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D904b6f97-323d-4a00-b8b0-9e7767b93566&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2bda7b2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#reset-password-mode)

Reset password mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FlypAr5aYZEBvvEKnoE8S%252FScreenshot%25202026-02-28%2520at%25204.24.18%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba511ae3-47ec-4810-8445-ea924a8c4a3e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18d43347&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal** \- is your checkout task to be used for shipping.
        
    *   **Monitor** - used for monitoring stock changes, will ‘wake up’ your normal tasks as long as they’re set to watch tasks.
        
    *   **Invite** - Used to request **Invite-Only** product access.
        
    *   **Reset Password Mode** - Used to reset the password to the account, the new password is automatically updated within the account session.
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   You need high quality proxies, ideally ISP. You can use most good ISP’s for monitoring and checkout. If you notice proxy errors, in the first instance try different ISP’s, and if you have to switch checkout (normal) to residential first. Always test on an instock item.
        
    
*   How do I find the **Product URL**?
    
    *   Full URL, taken directly from the website. I.e [https://www.chaoscards.co.uk/prod/elite-trainer-boxes-pokemon/pokemon-mega-evolution-ascended-heroes-elite-trainer-boxarrow-up-right](https://www.chaoscards.co.uk/prod/elite-trainer-boxes-pokemon/pokemon-mega-evolution-ascended-heroes-elite-trainer-box)
        
    
*   What is **QTY**?
    
    *   The number of items you want in one order.
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   The best QTY to use is 1 but if the item you're running for allows for more QTY per cart, feel free to increase the QTY
        
    
*   What is **delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error. The time also in milliseconds the bot will refresh on monitor and check again for stock.
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   We recommend running around 5000 delays for restocks.
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   **Normal task** - Recommend 3000 delay.
        
    *   **Monitor** - Recommend 5-10k (especially if running longer periods of time).
        
        \*With all delays, it’s about trial and error. If you notice tasks leading to errors, adjust delays i.e +1k on top.
        
    
*   What is a **Session**?
    
    *   This is your account, you can either match yourself i.e if the profile for this task is [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
         then the session needs to be that same email. You can also leave the session blank and bot will auto match.
        
    
*   What is **watch task**?
    
    *   Select this on your normal task, the task will ‘sleep’ and start attempting checkout once your monitor task finds stock.
        
    
*   What is **max price**?
    
    *   Chaos cards are known to hike prices up after release, use max price to monitor for stock at RRP. Ask your cookgroup for more information on prices if you’re not aware.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#important-notes)

Important notes:

*   You don’t have to run monitor mode if you’re aware of when a drop is or should be happening.
    
*   Use monitor mode to reduce proxy usage and stress and run for longer periods of time 24/7
    
    **Monitor** - used for monitoring stock changes, will ‘wake up’ your normal tasks as long as they’re set to watch tasks.
    
*   Do run with max price - this is important to prevent over RRP checkouts.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/chaos-cards#undefined)
