# Hot Topic | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2F2%2F2f%2FHot_Topic_logo.svg%2F412px-Hot_Topic_logo.svg.png%3F20141003231757&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ab5d8e5&sv=2)

[_Adding Sessions_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#adding-sessions)

[_HotTopic Task Overview_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#hot-topic-task-overview)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Hot Topic, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#adding-sessions)

Adding Sessions

To add your HotTopic accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Sessions** tab then click on **HotTopic**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F93hELCmULbhR4Eqh1u1e%252FHT%2520Session.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8cc869d5-5aa0-4eca-9b9b-6b7eca6cf23b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fdfcaa1&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Session** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FrePQWG9iLEi241NwjRrD%252FAdd%2520Session_.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da13c4ef4-1f84-43b3-88c6-00f11a2089a4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffe0593f&sv=2)

1.  Enter your account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FkBHZVZ3UTJFzYnh7n7Bi%252FSession%2520Setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D299b4af4-9cbf-4648-97b9-24e36ee723f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67b85c14&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#hot-topic-task-overview)

Hot Topic Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fu0kdmRE9SD7MYk3Sbjak%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dffaef2e3-b5d5-4c8a-b0f1-92faeb1dda98&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=479b960c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLmGyn8KCe0vVnQG978gP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deee9c370-0b4d-4a5f-88ab-df04d7ff82f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ceb0c7c&sv=2)

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** uses guest checkout or account checkout. Works for all products that are loaded on the site
        
    *   **Monitor mode** will allow you to monitor any product on HT and will alert your Normal mode watch tasks as long as the SKU is the same
        
        *   Monitor mode is optional, you can run Normal mode alone if you'd like
            
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs for monitoring and residentials for checkout tasks
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   Where do I find **SKU**?
    
    *   SKU can be found in the product URL. It will be towards the end of the URL
        
        *   Ex. [https://www.hottopic.com/product/invader-zim-gir-duo-crew-socks/16751950.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.hottopic.com/product/invader-zim-gir-duo-crew-socks/16751950.html)
             the SKU is **1675190**
            
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
         for quantity recommendations as different products may have different purchase limits set by the site
        
        *   Stellar does not automatically adjust the quantity if you set a number higher than what's allowed
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   **Monitor Delay** of **0** is recommended. HT doesn't ratelimit
        
    *   **Retry Delays** around 500 is recommended. This delay would allow you a chance to catch restocks as soon as they drop and not completely expose your proxies
        
    
*   What is **Session**?
    
    *   This option will allow you to select which [sessions](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#adding-sessions)
         you want to use
        
    
*   What is a **Watch Task** and should I select it?
    
    *   **Watch Tasks** waits until another source to ping it to trigger to attempt to add to cart. In this case with Hot Topic, your Monitor mode tasks will notify your Normal mode watch tasks when that specific product has restocked. The monitor task product needs to be identical to the normal mode product.
        
        *   The benefits of using watch tasks are 1) You'll use less proxy data as watch tasks do not use proxies while in Waiting status and 2) You'll be using less proxies overall which will reduce proxies being detected from the site.
            
        
    

[PreviousHome Depot CAchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca)
[NextIndigoCAchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/indigoca)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Preliminary Checklist](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#preliminary-checklist)
    
*   [Adding Sessions](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#adding-sessions)
    
*   [Hot Topic Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#hot-topic-task-overview)
    
*   [Normal Mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hot-topic#normal-mode)

# IndigoCA | Stellar

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/indigoca#undefined)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgLNVOOYFWAaVaPWyaRXN%252F640px-Indigo_logo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57ae1a43-26c2-4647-9ea5-65ba78e6b14c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee884dd9&sv=2)

Add Account

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FRJfo5RMTyD5rQnQrkClC%252FIndigo%2520Acc.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D668b718f-f633-43e2-9595-0a3b235c31ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3cd3ad5b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/indigoca#indigoca-task-overview)

IndigoCA Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/indigoca#shipping-mode)

**Shipping Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FqS5z9rylc7D9lg4OJCdZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91ea414c-d92c-4e05-9227-c96d9d98cf58&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3acfc900&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/indigoca#instore-mode)

Instore Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F0y9Xs3vPAwoarC87DYus%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbcc0b65c-9063-42ea-b409-e6e34dec5ad0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd0bfba2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/indigoca#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fup8HbhkGPoVXWQNI1xeO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc51def45-d194-4e20-9a3e-7346e12fbba4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41bd48ca&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Shipping mode** will allow you checkout shipping products from IndigoCA
        
    *   **Instore mode** will allow you checkout in store pick up products from IndigoCA
        
    *   **Monitor mode** will allow you to monitor products from IndigoCA and will ping/notify your shipping or instore mode watch tasks
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   Which **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and Resis are both OK
        
    
*   How do I find **SKU**?
    
    *   The product SKU is located at the end of the product URL
        
        *   For example [https://www.indigo.ca/en-ca/disney-lorcana-the-first-chapter-illumineers-trove/4050368981745.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.indigo.ca/en-ca/disney-lorcana-the-first-chapter-illumineers-trove/4050368981745.html)
             the SKU is `40500368981745`
            
        
    *   You can enter multiple SKUs in normal mode and monitor mode. SKUs are separated using a comma, no spaces
        
        *   Format is `SKU,SKU,SKU,SKU`
            
        
    
*   What **Quantity** should I use?
    
    *   At least 1 and could increase it depending on products max quantity
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Delays around 4000 are OK
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Running **Watch Tasks** will wait until monitor mode tasks ping/notify them. Watch tasks essentially wait to be notified/pinged to attempt to cart and checkout

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Gamestop, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop#h_08b1548129)

**Accounts**

1.  Go to **Sessions** tab, **Accounts** section and select **GameStop**
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fs3YQQHWo6OY7PQNLPKQJ%252FGME%2520Account.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e0df0e2-b71b-437c-b2c1-ea15701d8f6a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0ad0612&sv=2)
    
2.  Click **Add Account**
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAmGlG1s1DRCvZeIXCkaS%252FAdd%2520Account.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7bbb9ed-e0a8-49e1-a0a4-ec198e13937a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93503c1b&sv=2)
    
3.  **Email :** Enter your account email
    
    **Password :** Enter your account password
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FxbSTOWtFD3e8H2xZjf8j%252FAcc%2520Setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D36ee1bd9-80b9-44de-860c-507f27013668&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa605ffb&sv=2)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop#h_f30e70f32e)

**GameStop**

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop#checkout-mode)

**Checkout Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdXR6hIx1VoIGlCDd4hK2%252Fgamestop%2520checkout.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11afaea8-633b-446c-80c8-5b0f508bba77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7ac9f01&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fr1qu6zFHWbWBC78H4F3n%252Fgsmonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff0800ef-ec33-45ca-8853-a638318600fc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf55a295&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Checkout mode** allows you to cart and checkout any products from GameStop.com
        
    *   **Monitor mode** allows you to monitor any product from GameStop.com. When the products you're monitoring come into stock, your monitor mode tasks will notify your running checkout mode tasks with the same product SKU
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items. Profile email has to match your GameStop account email from the sessions tab
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs for monitoring and residentials for checkout tasks
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **SKU** and how do I get it?
    
    1.  Open the the product page, for example [https://www.gamestop.com/consoles-hardware/playstation-5/products/sony-playstation-5-pro/20015604.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.gamestop.com/consoles-hardware/playstation-5/products/sony-playstation-5-pro/20015604.html)
        
    2.  `CTRL+SHIFT+i` to open Developer Tools
        
    3.  Go to Elements tab on the top bar
        
    4.  `CTRL+F` and search `SKU`
        
    5.  The actual product SKU will appear to the right of the search result. In the example image below, the SKU is `C200246`
        
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FbJWPaWR7JpekRzlOKFNG%252Fgamestop%2520sku.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43694804-37b0-4632-8681-24082f1e93ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2687593&sv=2)

*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
         for quantity recommendations as different products may have different purchase limits set by the site
        
        *   Stellar does not automatically adjust the quantity if you set a number higher than what's allowed
            
        
    
*   What is **Account**?
    
    *   Select your [account](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop#h_08b1548129)
         to use for you task
        
        *   This is optional, it'll use guest checkout if you don't select an account
            
        
    
*   Which **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Monitor Delay: Around 5000
        
    *   Reset Delay: Around 5000
        
    *   Checkout task Delay: Around 1000
        
    
*   What is a **Watch Task** and should I select it?
    
    *   **Watch Tasks** waits until another source to ping it to trigger to attempt to add to cart. In this case with GameStop, your Monitor mode tasks will notify your running Checkout watch tasks when that specific product has restocked. The monitor task and checkout task need have the same product URL
        
        *   The benefits of using watch tasks are 1) You'll use less proxy data as watch tasks do not use proxies while in Waiting status and 2) You'll be using less proxies overall which will reduce proxies being detected from the site
            
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop#common-errors-and-fixes)

**Common Errors and Fixes**

*   **Moving To Cart:** `**Status 410**`
    
    *   _Cause:_ Error during add-to-cart flow; item is out of stock (OOS)
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Stop tasks **or**
            
        *   Let tasks run a bit longer in case of a restock
            
        
    
*   **Loading Product:** `**Status 403**`
    
    *   _Cause:_ Most likely proxy-related
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Try different proxies
            
        *   Test different proxy types
            
        *   Use a different proxy provider
            
        
    

[PreviousFunkoShopchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop)
[NextGameStop CAchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/gamestop-ca)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Home Depot CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FrWhZhwIAPnLbkmdxWYGq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe0eaba5-2e98-4ce5-baa3-9073c014d611&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e46994e9&sv=2)

Home Depot CA supports **guest checkout only**, making it a straightforward and reliable module for retail restocks and in-stock pickups. It’s primarily used for tools, hardware, seasonal items, and high-demand restocks that often appear without warning.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Home Depot CA, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for monitoring tasks.
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for checkout tasks. Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profiles, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#supported-modes)

Supported Modes

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fpjw43DNipCvkN6lnZ5OT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0846e6a-0fa9-4818-9fe4-ae6fa765996c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44c08918&sv=2)

Monitors restocks separately from your checkout tasks. When the monitored SKU restocks, the monitor task **pings** any checkout tasks with the same SKU.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#shipping-mode)

Shipping Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F3m5gLh4on4pVt8ddBh7H%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69662ef4-6b12-4fae-831d-6cf99f281eea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca9dcd&sv=2)

Used for **shipping fulfillment** (guest checkout only). If your default store has no stock, adjust your **Zip Code** or **Store ID**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#when-to-use-each-mode)

When to Use Each Mode

*   **Monitor Mode** → Detects restocks and pings your checkout tasks
    
*   **Shipping Mode** → Use for regular shipping checkout flow
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#profile-selection)

**Profile Selection**

Select the profile to be used for checkout. Home Depot CA does **not** support accounts; all checkouts are guest.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#proxy-setup)

**Proxy Setup**

Both **ISP** and **Residential** proxies are supported. Higher-quality proxies result in fewer errors. If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
 for high quality ISP and Residential proxies

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#product-sku)

**Product SKU**

An item’s unique identifier. Found near the end of most product URLs.

**Example:** `https://www.homedepot.ca/product/.../1001814680` SKU = **1001814680**

It's recommended to get product SKUs from your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#quantity-qty)

**Quantity (QTY)**

Check your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
 for product-specific purchase limits. Stellar does **not** auto-adjust quantities.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#zip-code)

**ZIP Code**

*   Determines your default store selection
    
*   Different ZIP codes may affect pricing or availability
    
*   Only use if you want to override your Profile’s ZIP
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#store-id)

**Store ID**

Overrides ZIP code. Sets a specific store as your default location.

Store IDs can be found here: `https://stores.homedepot.ca/`

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#maximum-price)

**Maximum Price**

Sets a price ceiling to prevent purchasing items above your desired max spend.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#delays)

**Delays**

*   **Shipping Delay:** 3000ms
    
*   **Monitor Delay:** 5000ms
    
*   **Reset Delay:** 9000ms
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#watch-task-how-it-works)

**Watch Task – How It Works**

The **Watch Task** option connects your Shipping task to your Monitor task.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#if-watch-task-is-enabled)

**If Watch Task is enabled:**

*   The checkout task does **not** monitor
    
*   It waits for a Monitor task with the **same SKU**
    
*   When the item restocks, the Monitor task **pings** the checkout
    
*   Checkout task adds to cart → proceeds to checkout
    

Your checkout task will show: **“Waiting for Monitor Ping”** This is correct.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#if-watch-task-is-disabled)

**If Watch Task is disabled:**

The checkout task monitors the SKU itself, adds to cart, and checks out directly.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#why-watch-task-is-recommended)

**Why Watch Task is recommended**

*   Reduces proxy bans
    
*   Improves task performance
    
*   Keeps monitoring centralized and efficient
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca#errors-and-fixes)

**Errors & Fixes**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Error Message**

**Possible Fixes**

# Lowes | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FXakEdvwlDzWozbHEP6hl%252Flowes.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0948b65-9ff8-4bd2-a7d5-8945c77cb172&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5337bc60&sv=2)

Our Lowe’s module supports both guest and account based checkout and operates on a true first come first serve system with no queue, making fast monitoring and efficient task setup essential. Because Lowe’s restocks can appear without warning and sell out quickly, Stellar automates account login, carting and checkout flows to help secure high demand items consistently. This module is ideal for tools, appliances, seasonal items and limited retail products that drop or restock abruptly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lowes#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Lowes, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profile, account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lowes#lowes-task-overview)

Lowes Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lowes#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwUjpt7bw7G6dahAAyVZM%252Flowesmonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ed35015-9439-4e66-8be6-494844b69911&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50ec6367&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lowes#account-mode)

Account Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FO68qSV2DPyBofZHUGc6m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7cee5435-1a0d-465b-a16d-cfb43c6a989a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6bf567bf&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lowes#guest-mode)

Guest mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FFfp5XkEOb3C1JN96Crfv%252Flowesguest.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ebc4067-e41c-481c-a9e5-0ce64b98b6a6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbdf2833&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor your desired products and ping your watch tasks when they detect the item you're monitoring is in stock
        
    *   **Guest mode** is to be used for guest checkout flow
        
    *   **Account mode** is to be used for account based checkout flow
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and resis will both work great
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is **Fulfillment Type**?
    
    *   Select Shipping or Pickup
        
    
*   What is a **Product SKU**?
    
    *   The **Product SKU** is a set of numbers and/or letters that identifies the item you would like to run. For example for this product URL [https://www.lowes.com/pd/Tide-Refreshing-Breeze-HE-Laundry-Detergent-46-fl-oz/5015041951arrow-up-right](https://www.lowes.com/pd/Tide-Refreshing-Breeze-HE-Laundry-Detergent-46-fl-oz/5015041951)
         the SKU is `5015041951`
        
    
*   What do I enter for **Zipcode**?
    
    *   Enter your **Zip Code** into this field
        
    
*   What is **Radius**?
    
    *   **Radius** is necessary to put in the tasks for **Pickup** fulfillment type. This is how far you're willing to pickup the item in miles. Make sure you have a zip code setup in your monitor mode task
        
    
*   What do I select for **IMAP** **Session**?
    
    *   Select an [IMAP session](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/imap-overview)
         that you named from the sessions tab in bot you'd like to use for your task
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   **Delay** to run is anywhere around 2000
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://help.stellara.io/en/articles/5772208-cook-groups-and-proxies)
         since different items have different quantity limits
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousLidschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lids)
[NextMacy'schevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys)

# Footsites | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FB5JaUHPhD6nLOHgXQBmO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc9a26cf-c90b-4dc0-8c7d-821272105189&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c33c912a&sv=2)

Our Footsites module supports account based checkout across major Footsite retailers and is designed to handle Akamai protection, captcha challenges and fast first come first serve releases. Because Footsites rely heavily on queue less speed, proxy quality and captcha solving, Stellar integrates flexible proxy support, multiple captcha providers and streamlined checkout logic to improve success rates. This module is best suited for sneakers and footwear releases on Footlocker, Champs Sports, Eastbay, and Kids Foot Locker that sell out quickly without warning.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/footsites#quick-start-recommended-setup)

**Quick Start (Recommended Setup)**

_(For members who want a fast setup without reading everything)_

*   Create a checkout **Profile** with billing, shipping and a **non 3DS payment method**
    
*   Use **high quality ISP or Residential proxies** (avoid flagged pools)
    
*   Select the correct **Footsite** (Footlocker, Champs, Eastbay, Kids Footlocker, etc.)
    
*   Enter the correct **SKU** and choose a **Size** (or Random)
    
*   Run **Normal Mode** tasks only
    
*   Set delays around **4000 ms**
    
*   Configure a **Captcha Provider** (Bot Harvester, AYCD or Capmonster)
    
*   Before major drops, run a **test task** on an in stock item
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/footsites#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Footsites, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Sessions (Accounts)**
    

> Footsites are **account-based**. You’ll need accounts added in Stellar before running tasks.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profile, account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/footsites#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/footsites#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FiMRwBVb6sY2upeEBrXKp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ea6417f-9859-4481-8b71-b8cc96fd382d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d9e2c3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/footsites#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F1I4P5thQstvDJEQGBZIL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da5060b27-9775-4157-9fbc-b466ec2fa3b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d85dc226&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to check for product availability
        
    *   **Normal mode** uses normal checkout flow
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Both ISPs and Residentials will perform great
        
    
*   Which **Site** do I select?
    
    *   You can choose from Footlocker, Footlocker CA, EastBay, Champs Sports, Champs Sports CA, Kids Footlocker
        
    
*   How do I enter a **SKU**?
    
    *   SKU can typically can be found in the product page
        
        *   For example [https://www.footlocker.com/en/product/~/C8013057.html?f=1arrow-up-right](https://www.footlocker.com/en/product/~/C8013057.html?f=1)
             the SKU is `C8013057`
            
        
    
*   How do I select a **Size**?
    
    *   From the dropdown options you can select one size per task or select `Random`
        
    
*   What is **Payment Method**?
    
    *   Select **Credit Card** or **Gift Cards**
        
    
*   What are **Gift Cards**?
    
    *   The Gift Cards option allows you to apply Footsites gift cards during checkout. To use gift cards:
        
        *   Go to the **Tags** tab in Stellar
            
            *   Create a new Tag Group (example: **Footsites Gift Cards**)
                
                *   Add your gift cards **one per line** using the format:
                    
                
            
            Example:
            
        
        Once saved, select this Tag Group in your Footsites tasks to apply gift cards at checkout.
        
    
*   What's **Queue Captcha Provider**?
    
    *   **Bot** will use the [Captcha Harvester](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
         in bot so you can manually solve captchas
        
    *   **AYCD** will use the [AutoSolve feature from AYCD](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
         to solve captchas for you
        
    *   **Capmonster** will use your [Capmonster](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
         account to solve captchas for you
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Monitoring Delay: Between `5000 - 9000`
        
    *   Reset Delay: Around `5000`
        
    *   Normal mode: Around `4000`
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    
*   What is the **Task Limit**?
    
    *   Currently at 500 but may change at any time
        
    

[PreviousFLX US & CAchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca)
[NextFraserschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/frasers)

# Dicks Sporting Goods | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgWr5e0B2uozz4GzLylDe%252F620516064e162f000480eda3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d182bdc-5907-4504-81ce-ae29514f7e18&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bde3b708&sv=2)

Our DSG module is designed for fast, reliable retail checkouts across scheduled launches and random restocks. With multiple task modes, strong monitoring options and support for both ISPs and residential proxies, it excels on high demand products that frequently restock without warning.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on DSG, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.
> 
> **Important:** DSG does **not** support 3DS cards, use a payment method that does not require 3D Secure.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops and restocks, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profiles, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#supported-modes)

Supported Modes

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F9ykEYdvuDwlmvURV9g1Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30f03686-210e-4ab4-a369-3591f8afa128&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b55adc9c&sv=2)

Used only for monitoring. This task will detect restocks and **ping your Watch Tasks** (Normal or Launch Mode) when the product becomes available.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Ftfl6u89fYfx2QFHMFazv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcbbb77a6-ca54-45cc-a510-9115e610847e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec09720c&sv=2)

Standard checkout flow for general restocks and everyday releases.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#launch-mode)

Launch mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FcRP2ij8vnRCVWmJcSdnW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d4e7c5b-f8c1-4a38-9de1-ab6b548bfc55&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=176a5fa6&sv=2)

Used for **scheduled releases** or **timed drops**, typically announced in advance. Best for products that go live at a specific time.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#when-to-use-each-mode)

When to Use Each Mode

*   **Monitor Mode** → Detects restocks and pings your checkout tasks
    
*   **Normal Mode** → Use for regular restocks or non-scheduled items
    
*   **Launch Mode** → Use for **scheduled drops** (e.g., 10 AM releases)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#profile-selection)

Profile Selection

Select a profile from the **Profiles tab**. That information will be used at checkout.

**Note:** DSG does **not** support 3DS cards. Use a card that **does not require 3D Secure authentication**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#proxy-setup)

Proxy Setup

DSG is extremely strict with bot protection, so proxy quality is crucial.

Use:

*   **High-quality ISPs** (best performance)
    
*   **Residential proxies** (work well too)
    
    *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    

Avoid:

*   Public, cheap, or low-quality proxies
    
*   These will trigger **Akamai errors** and cause your tasks to fail
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#product-url)

Product URL

The **Product URL** identifies the exact item you're attempting to run.

Example: `https://www.dickssportinggoods.com/p/-/24PAAUNBLG2324SLCXFLA`

Paste the full URL into your task.

You should be receiving product URLs from your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#monitor-types)

Monitor Types

You can choose between three monitor types:

*   **Normal (Default):** Standard monitoring endpoint
    
*   **API:** Alternative monitoring endpoint
    
*   **API2:** Alternative monitoring endpoint
    

For best performance: Create **three monitor tasks per product. O**ne using **Normal**, one using **API** and one using **API2**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#color-selector)

Color Selector

Optional field. If the product has multiple colors, type the color name you want (e.g., “White”).

If blank, a **random color** will be selected.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#size-selector)

Size Selector

*   Choose a size from the dropdown, or
    
*   Select **Random** for “One Size” products
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#delay-recommendations)

Delay Recommendations

Task Type

Delay Range

Notes

Monitoring Tasks

4000–7000 ms

Adjust based on proxy quality and site activity

Reset Delay

≤ 5000 ms

Controls retry frequency

Checkout Tasks

≤ 2000 ms

Faster delay for better speed at checkout

Tip: Always run at least **one Monitor Task per product** to catch restocks quickly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#quantity-qty)

Quantity (QTY)

Check with your cookgroup for QTY recommendations. DSG often has strict limits.

**Stellar will NOT automatically correct QTY** if you enter a number higher than site limits.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#watch-task-recommended)

**Watch Task (Recommended)**

**Enabling Watch Task:**

*   Your checkout task waits for a **Monitor Mode** task to detect the restock
    
*   Reduces proxy bans and errors
    
*   Improves overall performance
    

**If unchecked:**

*   Your checkout task will monitor on its own
    
*   Higher proxy consumption
    
*   Higher chance of bans or instability
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#cashback-options)

Cashback Options

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#use-rakuten)

**Use Rakuten**

Check this box to earn cashback. Follow the [Rakuten setup guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-rakuten-cashback)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#use-topcashback)

**Use TopCashBack**

Check this box to earn cashback. Follow the [TCB setup guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dicks-sporting-goods#error-messages-and-fixes)

Error Messages & Fixes

*   **Akamai Error / Access Denied**
    
    *   _Potential fix:_ Switch to higher-quality proxies (ISP proxies preferred)
        
    
*   **Product Not Found**
    
    *   _Potential fix:_ Verify the product URL or size availability
        
    
*   **Cart Error**
    
    *   _Potential fix:_ Reduce quantity (QTY) or use random size/color
        
    
*   **Monitoring Loop / No Pings**
    
    *   _Potential fix:_ Ensure a Monitor Mode task is running for the same URL
        
    
*   **Payment Declined**
    
    *   _Potential fix:_
        
        *   Use a non-3DS card
            
        *   Confirm billing information is accurate

[NextDroppchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp)

# Magic Madhouse | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FKAdlZnjGUlicEyR8Auv5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c400c59-b308-40a4-86e7-c980eb71966d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca277843&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Magic Madhouse make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – recommended for monitor and checkout.
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – IIssues with checkout task, switch to residentials.
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FVztJLPU2cHN54Maan3ei%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59999ce8-12df-4679-8832-d2d1f4f1ea54&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=295cca88&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fg4q0ox2RzM8M2eemP7K6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D956d28c3-67f1-472b-a645-7c3a33b055b5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4545a9ef&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal** \- is your checkout task to be used for shipping.
        
        **Monitor** - used for monitoring stock changes, will ‘wake up’ your normal tasks as long as they’re set to watch tasks.
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   You need high quality proxies, ideally ISP. You can use most good ISP’s for monitoring and checkout. If you notice proxy errors, in the first instance try different ISP’s, and if you have to switch checkout (normal) to residential first. Always test on an instock item.
        
    
*   How do I find the **Product URL**?
    
    *   Full URL, taken directly from the website. I.e https://magicmadhouse.co.uk/yu-gi-oh-yu-gi-oh-2021-tin-of-ancient-battles
        
    
*   What is **QTY**?
    
    *   The number of items you want in one order.
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   The best QTY to use is 1 but if the item you're running for allows for more QTY per cart, feel free to increase the QTY
        
    
*   What is **Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error. The time also in milliseconds the bot will refresh on monitor and check again for stock.
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   We recommend running around 5000 delays for restocks.
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   **Normal task** - Recommend 2000-3000 delay.
        
    *   **Monitor** - Recommend 5-10k (especially if running longer periods of time).
        
        \*With all delays, it’s about trial and error. If you notice tasks leading to errors, adjust delays i.e +1k on top.
        
    
*   What is a **Session**?
    
    *   This is your account, you can either match yourself i.e if the profile for this task is [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
         then the session needs to be that same email. You can also leave the session blank and bot will auto match.
        
    
*   What is W**atch Task**?
    
    *   Select this on your normal task, the task will ‘sleep’ and start attempting checkout once your monitor task finds stock.
        
    
*   What is **Captcha Provider**?
    
    *   The automated or in house solver. We **recommend** capsolver or capmonster (you will need a balance on these services, and you’ll also need to make sure the **API keys** are added to Bot settings - Captcha.
        
        You don’t need both.
        
    *   You can opt for bot solver, if you have an aged and high scoring gmail account, however currently it’s **recommended** to opt for capsolver or capmonster first. Trial and error.
        
    
*   What is M**ax Price**?
    
    *   Magic Madhouse are known to hike prices up after release, use max price to monitor for stock at RRP. Ask your cookgroup for more information on prices if you’re not aware.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse#important-notes)

Important notes:

*   You don’t have to run monitor mode if you’re aware of when a drop is or should be happening.
    
*   Use monitor mode to reduce proxy usage and stress and run for longer periods of time 24/7
    
    **Monitor** - used for monitoring stock changes, will ‘wake up’ your normal tasks as long as they’re set to watch tasks.
    
*   Do run with max price - this is important to prevent over RRP checkouts.
    
*   Magic Madhouse is optimised for speed, and if the product is already in stock, watch task is ignored and it will go straight to checkout for fastest speeds.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse#undefined)

[PreviousMacy'schevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys)
[NextMenardschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Kohls | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ftheretailconnection.net%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2FClientLogos%2FKohls-4c.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4323c27&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/kohls#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Kohls, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/kohls#task-overview)

Task Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/kohls#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F9P5Bw100Aa7afbHoAWH4%252Fkohlsmonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80adba90-6f17-4d01-a9de-76e08a4c6856&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6697ee26&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/kohls#guest-mode)

Guest mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FWoHmvm7LEwNoGQltTo53%252Fkohlsguest.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14280b7a-d848-4803-8dfd-161df2ec7259&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91dd63b7&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will allow you to monitor products on [https://www.kohls.com/arrow-up-right](https://www.kohls.com/)
         your monitor tasks will ping your guest mode tasks that have the Watch Task checkbox checked
        
    *   **Guest mode** will allow you to guest checkout products from [https://www.kohls.com/arrow-up-right](https://www.kohls.com/)
         using your profile information
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs are recommended but Resis will work as well
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What do I enter for **URL**?
    
    *   Copy and paste the **Product Page URL**. Make sure you're not pasting any unwanted characters or spaces
        
        *   For example [https://www.kohls.com/product/prd-5154798/mens-under-armour-wordmark-tech-20-tee.jsp?isClearance=true&prdPV=18arrow-up-right](https://www.kohls.com/product/prd-5154798/mens-under-armour-wordmark-tech-20-tee.jsp?isClearance=true&prdPV=18)
            
        
    
*   What is a **SKU** and how do I get it?
    
    *   A SKU is an item-specific identification ID that is special only to a single item. Kohls SKUs tend to be near the beginning of the link. ( ex. [https://www.kohls.com/product/prd-5154798/mens-under-armour-wordmark-tech-20-tee.jsp?isClearance=true&prdPV=18arrow-up-right](https://www.kohls.com/product/prd-5154798/mens-under-armour-wordmark-tech-20-tee.jsp?isClearance=true&prdPV=18)
         , SKU would be **5154798** )
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
         for quantity recommendations as different products may have different purchase limits set by the site
        
        *   Stellar does not automatically adjust the quantity if you set a number higher than what's allowed
            
        
    
*   What **Monitoring** **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   The best delay to use is 4000. If your proxies are getting flagged/banned, increase delays
        
    
*   What **Reset Delays** should I use?
    
    *   We recommend delays around 5000
        
    
*   What is **Discount**?
    
    *   If you have a discount code, you can paste it here
        
    
*   What is a **Watch Task** and should I select it?
    
    *   **Watch Tasks** waits until another source to ping it to trigger to attempt to add to cart. In this case with Kohls, your Monitor mode tasks will notify your Guest watch tasks when that specific product has restocked. The watch task product needs to be identical to the normal mode product.
        
        *   The benefits of using watch tasks are 1) You'll use less proxy data as watch tasks do not use proxies while in Waiting status and 2) You'll be using less proxies overall which will reduce proxies being detected from the site
            
        
    
*   What is **Use Rakuten?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [Rakuten guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-rakuten-cashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    
*   What is **Use TopCashBack?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [TopCashBack guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases

[NextLegochevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lego)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Crunchyroll | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F2P0xTAmZhjWsrRNi5DDQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0a41ddf-1d9c-46cf-b661-13036b98d23f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ebb5259&sv=2)

The Crunchyroll module is designed for purchasing anime figures, collectibles, exclusives, and limited merchandise directly from the Crunchyroll Store. It supports both monitoring and checkout workflows, allowing you to run 24/7 for restocks or prepare ahead of known drops. The site is generally stable but can slow down significantly during high-traffic releases, so proper setup is important for success.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#module-summary)

Module Summary

Crunchyroll uses relatively light bot protection compared to major retailers, making it beginner-friendly while still benefiting from clean proxies and optimized task structure. The module supports:

*   Guest checkout or logged-in checkout via sessions
    
*   Monitor → Checkout (Watch Task) workflows
    
*   Manual or automated captcha solving
    
*   Fast checkout during drops with built-in optimizations
    

This module is ideal for figures, anime merch, re-runs, and surprise restocks that sell out quickly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#quick-start-recommended-setup)

Quick Start (Recommended Setup)

For members who want the fastest setup without reading everything:

1.  Create at least one checkout profile in the Profiles tab
    
2.  Load Residential proxies into the Proxies tab
    
3.  Find the Crunchyroll product SKU (PID) from the product URL
    
4.  Create:
    
    *   1–2 **Monitor** tasks per SKU
        
    *   1 **Normal** task per SKU with **Watch Task enabled**
        
    
5.  Set delays around 3500 ms
    
6.  Choose your preferred captcha provider
    
7.  Start Monitor tasks first, then start Normal (Watch) tasks
    

For in-stock items, the module will skip the watch step and proceed directly to checkout automatically.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Crunchyroll, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Anti-bot related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#task-strategy-and-timing)

Task Strategy & Timing

**How Many Monitor Tasks Should I Create?**

*   Run **1 Monitor task per SKU**.
    
*   You can run multiple Monitor tasks if you want redundancy, but it’s **not required** and usually unnecessary.
    
*   Monitor tasks are lightweight and can run 24/7.
    

**Recommended:** 1 Monitor task per SKU is sufficient for most users.

* * *

**How Many Checkout Tasks Per Account?**

*   **Strictly 1 checkout task for each SKU per Crunchyroll account.**
    
*   Running more than one checkout task on the same account can cause:
    
    *   Account locks
        
    *   Checkout failures
        
    *   Login/session instability
        
    

**Rule:** 1 account = 1 checkout task (no exceptions).

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#task-overview)

Task Overview

**Normal mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FTWCvlRSL3rNg26PsFGN1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D897aa563-95ef-49dd-8b6a-53b677bf52a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c42196ef&sv=2)

**Monitor mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwZ2kJguGdowmob9KqH0Y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f562e2d-c949-4f0b-ab96-f717976d5d3c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0e61fa1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#task-field-explanations)

Task Field Explanations

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#mode)

Mode

*   **Monitor**: Monitors stock and pings Watch Tasks
    
*   **Normal**: Handles add-to-cart and checkout
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#profile)

Profile

Select the profile you want to use for checkout. This profile’s billing, shipping, and payment details will be used.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#checkout-proxy)

Checkout Proxy

Select the [proxy](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
 group you want the task to use. It is currently recommended to use residental proxies unless you have working ISPs as most ISPs are not currently working on the site.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#sku-pid)

SKU (PID)

Crunchyroll uses a numeric Product ID.

Example product URL: [https://store.crunchyroll.com/products/solo-leveling-sung-jinwoo-trio-try-it-prize-figure-re-run-crunchyroll-exclusive-4571623504702.htmlarrow-up-right](https://store.crunchyroll.com/products/solo-leveling-sung-jinwoo-trio-try-it-prize-figure-re-run-crunchyroll-exclusive-4571623504702.html)

The SKU would be: 4571623504702

Only the numeric ID is required.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#quantity-qty)

Quantity (Qty)

*   Crunchyroll usually limits purchases to **1 per order**
    
*   Recommended quantity is **1**
    
*   Setting a higher quantity may cause checkout failure
    
*   Check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
     for more accurate QTY
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#captcha-provider)

Captcha Provider

Crunchyroll requires captchas during checkout.

Supported options include:

*   [Solver](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
     (manual, in-bot solving)
    
*   [CapSolver](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capsolver)
    
*   [AYCD](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
    

Choose whichever provider you are most comfortable with. Solver is beginner-friendly but requires manual interaction.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#delay)

Delay

Recommended checkout delay is around **3500 ms**.

Recommended monitor delay is around 6**500 ms**.

Recommended reset delay is below **5000 ms**. Lower delays may work but can increase error rates during traffic spikes.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#session-optional)

Session (Optional\*)

If selected, the task will checkout using a logged-in Crunchyroll account.

*   Sessions stay active for weeks once logged in
    
*   Tokens are automatically refreshed when needed
    
*   Not required for success, but can help in some cases
    
*   \*please not some drops **require** a paid membership to purchase select drops.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#watch-task)

Watch Task

When enabled, the Normal task waits for a Monitor task to ping it before checking out.

Benefits:

*   Lower proxy usage
    
*   Faster reaction time on restocks
    
*   Reduced chance of proxy bans
    

Important notes:

*   The Monitor and Watch Task must use the **same SKU**
    
*   If the product is already in stock, the Watch step is skipped automatically
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crunchyroll#start-time)

Start Time

Optional. Leave blank to start immediately, or set a specific start time for scheduled drops.

[NextCurryschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/currys)

Last updated 15 days ago
