# Menards | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FIQ1mMPsl8FPOZQZSaivo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5d4aa4a-d9e7-4c91-8550-a22597747e03&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e06aca0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Menards, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards#profiles)

**Profiles**

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards#cook-group-access)

**Cook Group Access**

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards#test-task)

**Test Task**

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profiles, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FcegwmpbcHpI7D9xBFOJa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9cbccc42-90ca-4f1e-9b80-0de2b876990d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8cea1777&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FceWIH34vtRdUjmOth9Oi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09a938e5-c679-4453-9078-1363ed732210&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=467f41b6&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor your desired items. When an item restocks, your monitor mode tasks will ping your running watch tasks (Normal mode) tasks to atc and checkout
        
    *   **Normal mode** is your normal checkout mode task
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and residentials will both work
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   Where do I find **URL**?
    
    *   Every product will have it's own unique Product URL. Ex. [https://www.menards.com/main/outdoors/outdoor-recreation/camping-rv-supplies/playing-cards/pokmon-trade-trading-card-game-ex-battle-deck-assorted-styles/1010131101/p-1642874373768775-c-6506.htmarrow-up-right](https://www.menards.com/main/outdoors/outdoor-recreation/camping-rv-supplies/playing-cards/pokmon-trade-trading-card-game-ex-battle-deck-assorted-styles/1010131101/p-1642874373768775-c-6506.htm)
         SKU is also supported and can be found directly on the product page ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FmR8DN9fGMIb6Y5mjCsvi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0e41d57-db7c-498b-8cd9-576f96d854c3&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6ae3756&sv=2)
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   A good default to use is 1, but if the listing on the site allows for multiple in one cart then feel free to increase the QTY. max quanitity varies by product but can be found within the product page.
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment between 4000 - 6000
        
    
*   What is **Reset Delay** and what should I use?
    
    *   **Reset Delay** is the time in ms your monitor mode tasks will restart and monitor the product again after it catches a restock
        
        *   Around `5000` is OK
            
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   **Watch tasks** and **non-watch tasks** are different
        
        *   **Non-watch tasks** will be monitoring the site, which means that it will be using proxies. When a product restocks, this same task will atc and checkout
            
        *   **Watch tasks** are "watching" your **Monitor Mode** tasks waiting for a product you're running for to restock. Your **watch tasks** will add to cart and checkout when its pinged from a **Monitor Mode** task
            
        
    *   Your Monitor mode tasks will ping/notify your running Normal mode watch tasks when the product has restocked so they'll attempt to atc and checkout
        
    

[PreviousMagic Madhousechevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/magic-madhouse)
[NextNewBalancechevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newbalance)

# FiveBelow | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fd3VBejKSospSGVCPnufQ%252FFive-Below-Emblem.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da13f15e8-2a77-4422-80fc-7ea1f79db6ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e12ab3f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fivebelow#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on FiveBelow, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fivebelow#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fsd8Uh3cGI1I9yBXs6vU0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77faf750-3321-4fac-b57b-4309636c3091&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56d6a70e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fivebelow#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FPTGMX82Uve8amie71xug%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1be3c662-b095-4e7f-839f-da0e159f10ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=883961db&sv=2)

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor Mode** is used to check for product availbility
        
    *   **Normal Mode** uses guest checkout.
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items.
        
    
*   What **proxies** should I use?
    
    *   FiveBelow typically allows all types of proxies from DCs to ISPs to Resis.
        
    
*   How do I find the **Product URL**?
    
    *   Go to the product page and copy the URL in task bar.
        
        *   Example: [https://www.fivebelow.com/products/rapid-pump-water-balloon-pumparrow-up-right](https://www.fivebelow.com/products/rapid-pump-water-balloon-pump)
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   We recommend running around 2500 delays.
        
    
*   What **quantity** do I use?
    
    *   FiveBelow usually limits the quantity to 1 per order. Recommended to use 1.
        
    
*   Which **Captcha Provider** should I use?
    
    *   There are currently 6 captcha providers you can use. [Solver](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
        , [2Captcha](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-2captcha)
        , [CapMonster](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
        , [AntiCaptcha](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-anticaptcha)
        , [Poseidon](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-poseidon)
         and [AYCD](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
        . You are welcome to choose your favorite but to give more information on Solver, it will use the in-bot captcha solver which will prompt you to solve captchas manually.
        
    
*   What is a **Watch Task** and should I select it?
    
    *   **Watch Tasks** waits until Monitor mode task to ping it to trigger to attempt to add to cart. The watch task product needs to be identical to the monitor mode product.
        
        *   The benefits of using watch tasks are 1) You'll use less proxy data as watch tasks do not use proxies while in Waiting status and 2) You'll be using less proxies overall which will reduce proxies being detected from the site.
            
        
    

[PreviousFanaticschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fanatics)
[NextFLX US & CAchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Preliminary Checklist](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fivebelow#preliminary-checklist)
    
*   [Monitor Mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/fivebelow#monitor-mode)

# Lego | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2F2%2F24%2FLEGO_logo.svg%2F408px-LEGO_logo.svg.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7fac625&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lego#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Lego, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lego#adding-accounts)

Adding Accounts

To add your Lego accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Sessions** tab > **Accounts** > Click on **Lego**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F5ufPOZSZmwRIX8Q1BVoa%252FLego%2520Acc.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ff316ce-5819-44a2-b193-bb2b77fceb39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d1c7734&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Account** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FXFI8r3AYxr66LAdIRGJV%252FAdd%2520Account.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1ce8dd9-f3d0-44b0-8e08-ca89cf447690&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ac118d2&sv=2)

1.  Enter your account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FU1YmSQ1EfbGobmtsO9w2%252FAcc%2520Setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a8e60da-f95c-4915-a654-8bf566864670&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8820975&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lego#lego-task-overview)

Lego Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lego#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FHuPXkMfVAcxzu56tZkHl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bb91e39-18dd-4ee2-ba34-babd3e346180&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f85310c4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lego#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F0mQ5dnS2a1dpDGS5eClG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D816915f2-df26-41c2-a653-5e8eec4aac5a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc36d352&sv=2)

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to check for product availability
        
    *   **Normal mode** uses guest checkout if you don't select an account. Works for all products that are loaded on the site [https://www.lego.com/arrow-up-right](https://www.lego.com/)
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs for monitoring and residentials for checkout tasks
        
    
*   Where do I find **SKU**?
    
    *   The **SKU** is unique for a product on Lego website. The SKU can usually be found at the end of the product URL
        
        *   Ex. [https://www.lego.com/en-us/product/fighter-plane-chase-77012arrow-up-right](https://www.lego.com/en-us/product/fighter-plane-chase-77012)
             the SKU for this product is `77012`
            
        
    
*   Which **Region** should I select?
    
    *   Select the region that applies to you
        
    
*   What is **Size**?
    
    *   Select the size(s) in shoes you'd like to purchase. There's also a **Random** option if you prefer any shoe size
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment around 2000 delays. This delay is the amount of time before the task retries after it encounters an error
        
    
*   What **Monitor** **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment around 2000-4000 delays. This delay is the amount of time your task will monitor for the product
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   A good default to use is 1, but if the listing on the site allows for multiple in one cart then feel free to increase the QTY
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousKohlschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/kohls)
[NextLidschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/lids)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Macy's | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FckUYFFxUjJUrvGPiMikE%252FMacy%27s_Logo_2019.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbca8438b-adc4-4893-9068-5091215bb4b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b76e0ed8&sv=2)

Our Macy’s module supports **guest checkout** only, making it one of the simpler and more consistent modules in Stellar. It’s primarily used for **retail restocks and in stock monitors**, ideal for Pokémon cards, collectibles and other high demand items that often return to stock without notice.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#quick-start-recommended-setup)

**Quick Start (Recommended Setup)**

_(For members who want a fast setup without reading everything)_

*   Create a checkout **Profile** with billing and shipping info
    
*   Use **ISP proxies** for monitoring and **Residential proxies** for checkout
    
*   Create **Monitor Mode** tasks for each SKU you want
    
*   Run matching **Normal Mode** checkout tasks with **Watch Task enabled**
    
*   Make sure checkout tasks show **“Waiting for Monitor Ping”** before drops
    
*   Enable **Use App** only for app only restocks (if applicable)
    
*   Set proper delays and QTY based on cook group guidance
    
*   Before major drops, run a **test task** on an in stock item
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Macy’s, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for monitoring tasks.
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for checkout tasks. Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook group](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profiles, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#supported-modes)

Supported Modes

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F5LSkRgmehAxxn1wZRp1J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82355e38-cbd6-4e73-a153-34b1f8c07474&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=569a5ae3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLkTcEixzYyQWc7AcDaDi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D778902ac-70fa-48d1-9094-f45472d868c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f346ad79&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#when-to-use-each-mode)

When to Use Each Mode

*   **Normal Mode** → For direct in stock checkouts.
    
*   **Monitor Mode** → For monitoring items that are currently out of stock.
    

You can combine both for optimal performance:

*   Monitor tasks watch for restocks.
    
*   Normal mode watch tasks with the same SKU wait for the monitor to trigger them.
    
    Make sure your Normal mode tasks show **“Waiting for Monitor”** before a drop.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#profile-selection)

Profile Selection

Select the profile you want to use under the **Profiles** dropdown. Your billing and shipping info from that profile will be used automatically during checkout.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#proxy-setup)

Proxy Setup

For the best performance:

*   Use **ISP proxies** for monitoring tasks.
    
*   Use **Residential proxies** for checkout tasks.
    

If you need reliable proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
 for high quality ISP and Residential options.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#sku-setup)

SKU Setup

To locate the SKU:

1.  Visit the Macy’s product page.
    
2.  Find the SKU in the product URL or source or get it from your [cook group](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
    .
    
3.  Paste the SKU into the product field in Stellar.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#delay-recommendations)

Delay Recommendations

Task Type

Delay Range

Notes

Monitoring Tasks

4000–7000 ms

Adjust based on proxy quality and site activity

Reset Delay

≤ 5000 ms

Controls retry frequency

Checkout Tasks

≤ 2000 ms

Faster delay for better speed at checkout

Tip: Always run at least **one Monitor Task per product** to catch restocks quickly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#discount-code)

Discount Code

*   Enter the discount code here in this field if you have one and make sure it's entered correctly, this is case sensitive. Also be sure to remove any unnecessary spaces.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#quantity-qty)

Quantity (QTY)

*   Check your cook group for product-specific quantity limits.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#use-app-option)

Use App Option

The **Use App** checkbox allows you to monitor and checkout products that are app only. Your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
 should inform you about app only drops and restocks including product information such as SKUs.

How it works:

1.  Enable **Use App** on your monitor and/or checkout tasks.
    
2.  Start your tasks.
    
3.  When there's an app only drop or restock, your tasks will detect it right away.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#max-price)

Max Price

You need to setup Max Price in Monitor mode if using _Watch Task,_ same logic as in every module with price check.

Price is checked on Monitor Step.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#watch-task-option)

Watch Task Option

The **Watch Task** checkbox allows checkout tasks to wait for a monitor task to detect a restock first instead of monitoring themselves.

How it works:

1.  Enable **Watch Task** on your checkout task.
    
2.  Start the task, it will show **“Waiting for Monitor Ping.”**
    
3.  When your Monitor Mode task detects a restock, it triggers your checkout task to run.
    

This method reduces site load and improves success rates during restocks.

If **Watch Task** is disabled, your checkout task will monitor and run independently.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#video-guides)

Video Guides

Coming soon...

*   Macy's Setup Overview
    

This video walkthrough will be available within the guide once uploaded.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#error-messages-and-fixes)

Error Messages & Fixes

*   **Payment failed**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Declined or flagged card
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_ Try another card or payment method
        
    
*   **Out of stock**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Product sold out before checkout
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_ Lower delays or use Watch Task for faster trigger
        
    
*   **Invalid SKU**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Incorrect or outdated SKU
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_ Verify SKU from product page or cook group
        
    
*   **Proxy banned**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Overused or flagged proxies
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_ Rotate proxies or lower monitor delays
        
    
*   **Task stuck on carting**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Site-side delay or queue
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_ Restart task or test alternative proxies
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/macys#summary)

Summary

Macy’s is one of the most stable and consistent retail modules in Stellar. It’s fast, beginner friendly and works great for restocks. With the right setup, solid proxies, smart delays and good monitor pairing, users can consistently secure high demand products.

# Home Depot | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FRT93KaVrQUzg87FIJwS3%252F5cb77aafa7c7755bf004c114_400x400.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2609482-b60c-4684-b46b-065b9f94c094&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbe63e70&sv=2)

Our Home Depot module supports both account based checkout and guest checkout and operates on a true first come first serve system with no queue, making fast monitoring and efficient task setup essential. Because HD restocks can appear without warning and sell out quickly, Stellar automates account login, carting and checkout flows to help secure high demand items consistently. This module is ideal for price errors, tools, appliances, seasonal items and limited retail products that drop or restock abruptly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Home Depot, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profile, account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#sessions)

Sessions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add your accounts to Stellar by following the steps below

1.  Go to Identities tab
    
2.  Go to Sessions
    
3.  Select on Home Depot
    
4.  Click the Add Session button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fec2etbJN3fqb7nJt9Tpp%252Fhdsession.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e4bc6f3-294b-43ec-a329-41d7a6350ecf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d37b239b&sv=2)

1.  Nickname your Session and add your account email and password
    
2.  Click Save. Your account will login when you start a Shipping or Pickup mode task
    

circle-info

Sessions are not needed for Home Depot. You can leave the Session field empty in task setup to use Guest checkout

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#task-overview)

**Task Overview**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#shipping-mode)

Shipping mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBYMZBKbCGEXZo6XGS4sK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da485d518-da03-4f57-adc6-c734e1cf94f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee023023&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#pickup-mode)

Pickup mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fcm98NRpxrJM1k8lnK9f6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D792cdb01-3189-4be4-9072-9b256dcfa0a0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30d917b0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FTNBpsjQcrBU72B0UiySi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9e4cda6-a600-4047-affc-0b05071e5a69&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57ef2597&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#monitor-pickup-mode)

Monitor-Pickup mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FqGaiLwk5TNL5s0uDkjqj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee5bfdfb-f9b0-4d4c-aec5-262aab1825ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=193535fd&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Shipping mode** works on all shipping products
        
    *   **Pickup mode** works on all pickup products
        
    *   **Monitor mode** will continuously check for product availability (Shipping fulfillment) and notify your checkout tasks when product is in stock
        
    *   **Monitor-Pickup mode** will continuously check for product availability (Pickup fulfillment) and notify your checkout tasks when product is in stock
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs for monitoring and residentials for checkout tasks
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What do I enter for **URL**?
    
    *   Copy and paste the **Product Page URL**. Make sure you're not pasting any unwanted characters or spaces
        
        *   For example [https://www.homedepot.com/p/Dr-Seuss-6-ft-Animated-Grinch-Christmas-Animatronic-22GM16953/320168369arrow-up-right](https://www.homedepot.com/p/Dr-Seuss-6-ft-Animated-Grinch-Christmas-Animatronic-22GM16953/320168369)
            
        
    
*   What is a **SKU** and how do I get it?
    
    *   A SKU is an item-specific identification ID that is special only to a single item. HomeDepot SKUs tend to be near the end of the link. ( ex. [https://www.homedepot.com/p/Dr-Seuss-6-ft-Animated-Grinch-Christmas-Animatronic-22GM16953/320168369arrow-up-right](https://www.homedepot.com/p/Dr-Seuss-6-ft-Animated-Grinch-Christmas-Animatronic-22GM16953/320168369)
         , SKU would be **320168369** )
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
         for quantity recommendations as different products may have different purchase limits set by the site
        
        *   Stellar does not automatically adjust the quantity if you set a number higher than what's allowed
            
        
    
*   What is **Session**?
    
    *   Select a Session (account) you want to use for your task(s)
        
        *   Leave this Session field empty for Guest checkout
            
        
    
*   What do I enter for **Zipcode**?
    
    *   On Home Depot, different zip codes will have different prices, including price errors. Input your zipcode into this field
        
    
*   What is **Radius**?
    
    *   **Radius** is necessary to put in the Pickup mode tasks. This is how far you're willing to pickup the item in miles
        
    
*   What is **Store IDs?**
    
    *   Put in comma separated format for example `storeid1,storeid2,storeid3,storeid4,storeid5`
        
    
*   What is **Maximum Price**?
    
    *   Maximum price is used in order to not purchase an item over the desired price value you would like. We recommend putting a price value slightly above the retail value to account for fees and shipping
        
    
*   What is an **Associate ID**?
    
    *   If you have one, enter your associate ID to get an extra 10% off your checkout
        
    
*   What **Monitoring** **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   We recommend delays around 4000
        
    
*   What **Reset** **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   We recommend delays around 5000
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the product, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    
*   What is **Express Delivery**?
    
    *   Check this box if you want to choose the Express Delivery option for shipping. Leave this box unchecked for standard delivery option
        
    
*   What is **Use TopCashBack?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [TopCashBack guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    

[PreviousHobbyLobbychevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/hobbylobby)
[NextHome Depot CAchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot-ca)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Preliminary Checklist](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#preliminary-checklist)
    
*   [Sessions](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#sessions)
    
*   [Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#task-overview)
    
*   [Shipping mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#shipping-mode)
    
*   [Pickup mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#pickup-mode)
    
*   [Monitor mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#monitor-mode)
    
*   [Monitor-Pickup mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/home-depot#monitor-pickup-mode)
    

Was this helpful?

# FLX US & CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.worldvectorlogo.com%2Flogos%2Ffoot-locker-logo.svg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=607c1f15&sv=2)

Our FLX module is built for **Foot Locker FLX (US + Canada)** and focuses on **account-based entry workflows**, including passing checkpoint steps and submitting entries for specific products/sizes. Because FLX flow is typically **first-come, first-processed** and can involve checkpoint validation, Stellar splits the process into dedicated task modes (Entry, Check-Points, and Account-Gen) to keep your setup clean, fast, and repeatable. This module is best suited for users running multiple accounts to maximize entry success for hyped footwear releases.

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#quick-start-recommended-setup)

Quick Start (Recommended Setup)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_(For members who want a fast setup without reading everything)_

*   Add FLX accounts under **Identities → Sessions (or Accounts) → FLX**
    
*   Use **high-quality ISP or Residential proxies** (avoid flagged pools)
    
*   Run **Check-Points** tasks first (to get accounts checkpoint-ready)
    
*   Run **Entry** tasks for the same SKU + size using those sessions
    
*   Keep delays moderate (start around **3000–5000ms**) and adjust based on proxy quality
    
*   Before a real release, run a **test Entry** (or a safe test flow if available) to confirm sessions + proxies work
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#profiles)

Profiles

Create and save your checkout profiles under the **Profiles** tab in Stellar. These contain your:

*   Billing information
    
*   Shipping information
    
*   Payment information (if applicable)
    

**Tip:** Even if FLX entry isn’t a traditional “checkout,” profiles are still used for identity/address fields when required.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#proxies)

Proxies

High-quality proxies are strongly recommended for FLX.

**Recommended types**

*   **ISP Proxies**: best balance of speed + trust (recommended default)
    
*   **Residential Proxies**: great for trust/rotation if you hit blocks more often
    

**Avoid**

*   Low-quality datacenter proxies (more likely to trigger checkpoint-related issues)
    

If you need proxies, [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
 offers both ISP and Residential options.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#sessions-accounts)

Sessions (Accounts)

FLX is **account-based**. You’ll need FLX accounts added in Stellar before running Entry or Check-Points tasks.

**Recommended**

*   1 task per account (don’t reuse a single account across too many tasks at once)
    
*   Keep account email/password correct and consistent
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#cook-group-access-optional-but-recommended)

Cook Group Access (Optional but recommended)

Your [cook group](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
 helps with:

*   SKU / product codes
    
*   Sizing guidance (which sizes are realistic)
    
*   Drop timing + region notes (US vs CA differences)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#test-task)

Test Task

Before a major release:

*   Run a small set of tasks (2–5 accounts)
    
*   Confirm proxies aren’t blocked
    
*   Confirm sessions load correctly
    
*   Confirm your mode flow works (Check-Points → Entry)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#task-modes-overview)

Task Modes Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

FLX includes these task modes:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#id-1-entry)

1) Entry

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAwlnQ8Yw6ccrUtmKuPok%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dada38ec1-4cfc-471e-8dd2-2631100ed803&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36d09c5c&sv=2)

Used to **submit an entry** for a specific product using:

*   SKU
    
*   Size
    
*   Session (account)
    
*   Profile
    
*   Proxies
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#id-2-check-points)

2) Check-Points

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FIw5XokOs51QCUjoht2An%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80dba658-ca6d-4ed3-b250-2e24a449f744&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47aecf90&sv=2)

Used to **prepare accounts for entry** by completing checkpoint-related steps. Recommended to run before Entry tasks, especially close to release windows.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#id-3-account-gen)

3) Account-Gen

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FJjH5wHE7yBpMBUoOvb6u%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D913ac0cc-d1e5-4363-92bf-130d91b2cc7f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2469e519&sv=2)

Used to **create new FLX accounts** (US/CA) directly inside Stellar. Includes support for:

*   Postal code
    
*   Password
    
*   Catchall (optional)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#id-4-cancel-entry)

4) Cancel-Entry

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F7tpwIdV31k3dpMXDHeAQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddda3d878-df63-4932-ba10-0684367bc54d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2117f04&sv=2)

Used to **cancel an entry** for a specific product using:

*   SKU
    
*   Session (account)
    
*   Profile
    
*   Proxies
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#creating-tasks-step-by-step)

Creating Tasks (Step-by-Step)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#entry-mode-new-task-mode-entry)

Entry Mode (New Task → Mode: `entry`)

Use this mode to submit an entry for a specific release.

**Required fields (from the task window)**

1.  **Name**: Give it a clear name (example: `FLX Entry - SKU - Size - Group1`)
    
2.  **Mode**: `entry`
    
3.  **Profile**: Select your profile
    
4.  **Checkout Proxy**: Select your proxy group (ISP or Resi recommended)
    
5.  **SKU**: Enter the product SKU/code
    
6.  **Size**: Choose your size (or the required selection)
    
7.  **Session**: Select the FLX account session you want to use
    
8.  **Delay**: Start around `3000–5000` and adjust as needed
    
9.  **Qty**: Keep at `1` unless the module explicitly supports other values
    

**Optional toggles**

*   **Add Address?**: Adds address info from your profile to your account
    
*   **Add Payment?**: Adds payment info from your profile to your account
    
*   **Start Time**: Schedule tasks to start automatically
    

**Recommended workflow**

*   Run **Check-Points** first
    
*   Then run **Entry** tasks (one per account)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#check-points-mode-new-task-mode-check-points)

Check-Points Mode (New Task → Mode: `check-points`)

Use this mode to pass checkpoint steps and reduce friction when running Entry.

**Fields**

1.  **Name**: Example `FLX Checkpoints - Group1`
    
2.  **Mode**: `check-points`
    
3.  **Profile**: Select profile (recommended)
    
4.  **Checkout Proxy**: Select proxy group
    
5.  **Session**: Select FLX session
    
6.  **Delay**: Start around `3000–6000`
    
7.  **Start Time**: Optional scheduling
    
8.  **Qty**: Keep at `1`
    

**Best practice**

*   Run Check-Points tasks **ahead of time** (or before you start Entry tasks)
    
*   If you have many accounts, stagger start times or delays to reduce proxy pressure
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#account-gen-mode-new-task-mode-account-gen)

Account-Gen Mode (New Task → Mode: `account-gen`)

Use this mode to generate new accounts directly in Stellar.

**Fields**

1.  **Name**: Example `FLX AccountGen - Batch1`
    
2.  **Mode**: `account-gen`
    
3.  **Profile**: Select a profile (recommended—especially if email is pulled from profile)
    
4.  **Checkout Proxy**: Use high-quality proxies (Resi often best here)
    
5.  **Postal Code**: Enter a valid US/CA postal/zip code for the account region
    
6.  **Password**: Enter a password (or follow your team’s standard format)
    
7.  **Delay**: Start around `5000` for stability
    
8.  **Catch All?**: Enable only if you’re using a catchall email setup
    
9.  **Start Time**: Optional scheduling
    
10.  **Qty**: Keep at `1`
    

**Important**

*   FLX module supports **US + Canada only** — ensure your postal code matches the region you intend to use.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#fields-and-options)

Fields & Options


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#name)

Name

A label for your task. Use a consistent naming pattern:

*   `FLX Entry - SKU - Size - AccountBatch`
    
*   `FLX Checkpoints - Batch1`
    
*   `FLX AccountGen - Batch2`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#mode)

Mode

Select what the task does:

*   `entry` = submit entry
    
*   `check-points` = checkpoint preparation
    
*   `account-gen` = generate accounts
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#profile-required)

Profile (Required)

The identity info used in the task flow (address/payment when needed).

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#checkout-proxy)

Checkout Proxy

The [proxy](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
 group used for the task’s requests.

**Recommended**

*   ISP for general stability
    
*   Resi if you see frequent blocks or checkpoint issues
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#sku-entry-only)

SKU (Entry only)

Product identifier. Usually provided by [cook groups](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
 or found in product metadata.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#size-entry-only)

Size (Entry only)

Select the size(s) you want to enter for.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#session)

Session

Your FLX account selection. Typically:

*   1 session = 1 account
    
*   Recommended: 1 Entry task per account
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#delay)

Delay

How often the task retries actions (milliseconds).

**Starting recommendations**

*   Check-Points: `3000–6000`
    
*   Entry: `3000–5000`
    
*   Account-Gen: `5000+` for stability
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#add-address)

Add Address?

When enabled, Stellar will apply address details from your profile to your account.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#add-payment)

Add Payment?

When enabled, Stellar will apply payment details from your profile to your account.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#payment-sms-input)

Payment SMS Input

Select either Manual or [Text Verified (US only)arrow-up-right](https://www.textverified.com/)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#start-time)

Start Time

Schedules tasks to begin automatically at a set time.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#qty)

Qty

Default `1`. Most entry flows don’t need higher quantities.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#postal-code-account-gen-only)

Postal Code (Account-Gen only)

Enter new zip code or the bot will use zip code from your selected profile.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#password-account-gen-only)

Password (Account-Gen only)

Enter your prefered password or the bot will automatically create one.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#catch-all-account-gen-only)

Catch All? (Account-Gen only)

Use only if you have a proper [catchall](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/catchall-email-guide)
 email setup.

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#recommended-task-setups)

Recommended Task Setups


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#standard-release-setup-most-common)

Standard Release Setup (Most Common)

*   1x **Check-Points** task per account
    
*   1x **Entry** task per account (per SKU + size)
    
*   ISP proxies preferred; use Resi if you encounter issues
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#safety-setup-if-you-see-more-blocks)

“Safety” Setup (If You See More Blocks)

*   Run Check-Points earlier (more time buffer)
    
*   Use Residential proxies for Check-Points + Entry
    
*   Increase delays slightly (ex: 5000–7000)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/flx-us-and-ca#common-status-messages-and-fixes)

Common Status Messages & Fixes


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Waiting for Start Time**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Task is scheduled
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Confirm the start time or remove it
        
    
*   **Logging In / Authenticating Session**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Normal login step
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Ensure session credentials are correct; try a different proxy
        
    
*   **Session Invalid / Login Failed**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Wrong password, locked account, or blocked IP
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Verify credentials, reset the account manually if needed, switch to cleaner proxies
        
    
*   **Checkpoint Required**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Account requires checkpoint flow
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Run **Check-Points** mode first, then retry Entry
        
    
*   **Failed to Pass Checkpoint**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Proxy flagged or checkpoint challenge failed
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Swap proxy pool (residential recommended), slightly increase delays
        
    
*   **Proxy Banned / Blocked**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Low-quality or flagged proxy
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Use higher-quality ISP/residential proxies; avoid reusing burned proxies
        
    
*   **Product Not Found / Invalid SKU**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Incorrect SKU or region mismatch
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Confirm SKU, verify US/CA region, confirm source with cook group
        
    
*   **Size Unavailable**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Size not selectable or outside entry range
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Try a different size or confirm size formatting
        
    
*   **Entry Failed / Submit Error**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Site response error, proxy issue, or session issue
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Restart task, change proxy, confirm session is healthy
        
    
*   **Rate Limited / Too Many Requests**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Too many tasks using the same proxy pool
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Reduce task count per proxy, increase delays, use a larger proxy pool
        
    
*   **Unknown Error**
    
    *   _Likely cause:_ Temporary site change or backend issue
        
    *   _Fix / Recommendation:_ Recreate task group, restart the bot, retry with different proxies

# NFL Shop | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FP1N8J2JcjMiSRSr8Lp0t%252Fnflshoppnglogo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b6fa8a-3b5b-4a68-9f7f-6655d89bc8a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe0d27e7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on NFL Shop, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FDEfg4XL1WC3A8IDmyIIn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79402f14-5b31-432a-aa3f-c12606fbc733&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4949d114&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop#checkout-mode)

Checkout Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FiXX7kZuI28pwM4Vf0LZt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71c20013-9511-460f-8803-90b9c93a7b75&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5ab2956b&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   Monitor mode is used to check for product availabilty
        
    *   Checkout mode uses guest checkout
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   All types of proxies from DCs to ISPs to Resis
        
    
*   What's **Event URL**?
    
    *   Paste the product/event URL here
        
    
*   What **Quantity** do I use?
    
    *   There may have quantity limits for certain hyped products (if so, set it to those) Overall it is recommended to use 1
        
    
*   What **Delay** should I use?
    
    *   Between 4000-6000 is OK
        
    
*   What is **Monitoring Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds before retrying when an item is back in stock. `4500` is OK which would be 4.5 seconds
        
    
*   What is **Discount**?
    
    *   If you have a discount code, you can enter it in this field
        
    
*   What is **Cheapest Shipping?** box?
    
    *   Check this box if you'd like to purchase your product with the cheapest shipping option available
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousNike (FCFS)chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nike-fcfs)
[NextNvidiachevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nvidia)

*   [Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop#task-overview)
    
*   [Monitor Mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop#monitor-mode)
    
*   [Checkout Mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop#checkout-mode)

# Nike (FCFS) | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FtvFF0vG1PhphSTVtjYni%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4dae41a-bc29-49f2-8f2c-d9fe25f368dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70b0af99&sv=2)

The **Nike module** supports **FCFS / Flow releases** for both **US and Canada**. This module is designed to monitor Nike product pages and react quickly to restocks or product availability, helping users secure items as soon as they become available.

For **US releases**, the module supports **fully automated checkout**, allowing tasks to add to cart and complete checkout automatically. For **Canada releases**, the module generates **cart links** which allow users to manually open the cart and complete checkout.

Nike Flow releases are typically **first come first served drops**, meaning speed and preparation are key. Monitor tasks are optimized to **detect product availability quickly**, allowing checkout tasks to trigger as fast as possible when stock appears.

This module focuses specifically on **Flow releases** rather than **Draw or Raffle entries**. Flow releases are significantly easier to run, require less setup, and are generally more beginner friendly compared to draw systems which require larger account preparation and longer setup processes.

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nike-fcfs#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before setting up tasks onNike(FCFS), make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Antibot-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Accounts (Sessions)**
    

> *   Accounts are needed for US but not needed for Canada
>     

*   **IMAP (Highly Recommended)**
    

> *   Lets Stellar automatically pull Nike verification codes from your email.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Antibot-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nike-fcfs#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nike-fcfs#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F4u8tYvqysaeWZ3SwiNhh%252FScreenshot%25202026-03-09%2520at%25209.56.25%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D702a33b2-356e-4348-a386-e8c2bc5e6222&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4deebb79&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nike-fcfs#fcfs-mode)

FCFS Mode


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F4CaqXasgS29Nafpo3t2T%252FScreenshot%25202026-03-09%2520at%25209.58.37%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9dedd2-95a9-48b3-8398-37b27e80e123&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d558977e&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   Monitor mode is used to check for product availabilty
        
    *   FCFS mode **requires** an account to checkout for **US**, guest works for **CA ONLY.**
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   All types of proxies from DCs to ISPs to Resis can be used for monitor, ISPs is recommended for checkout(FCFS) tasks
        
    
*   What's **SKU**?
    
    *   A SKU is a unique ID for a specific Nike item. You can find the SKU in the product page or from your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
        .
        
        You can only enter one SKU per task
        
    
*   What **Quantity** do I use?
    
    *   There may have quantity limits for certain hyped products (if so, set it to those) Overall it is recommended to use 1
        
    
*   What **Delay** should I use?
    
    *   we recommend to start with 3000 delay and adjust as needed.
        
    
*   What is **Monitoring Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds before retrying when an item is back in stock. `3000` is OK which would be 3 seconds
        
    
*   What is **Discount**?
    
    *   If you have a discount code, you can enter it in this field
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout

[NextNFL Shopchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop)

# Dropp | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fo.remove.bg%2Fdownloads%2F76f8bfaf-399a-4aac-b42a-3c212ed36f91%2F8CYA7jFL_400x400-removebg-preview.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89826856&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Dropp, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.
> 
> **Important:** DSG does **not** support 3DS cards, use a payment method that does not require 3D Secure.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp#h_581806b8b0)

**Sessions**

**Note:** Accounts that are generated with Stellar will be automatically added to the Sessions tab. Stellar will automatically pull emails from IMAP you have setup in bot. The password will override the default password.

1.  Navigate to the **Sessions tab** and click on **Dropp**
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgaMxXK94GEr4mMU4rC3Z%252FDroppp%2520Session.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd749e47e-c213-4664-a8d3-c7b9f549bbf2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21fe65ef&sv=2)
    
2.  Click on the **Add Session** button
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAWv6oLZEZw9mhU9onGin%252FAdd%2520Session_.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22263736-1ad1-4743-8206-47cd211a783c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e220c225&sv=2)
    
3.  Give your session a name and enter your accounts email and password
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdgFFsEh7ghQRc8RtGbYP%252FDroppp%2520session%2520setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf9c1386-81d5-4c47-a10c-9315edc1772b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46ec01e2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp#h_31c775b92f)

**Captcha Harvesters**

If you select the browser distribution method you'll need to follow the [Captcha Harvesters guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
. This will ensure the Captcha Harvesters will show the browser when it opens. You should open as many harvesters as you want browsers to open

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fd2hbZnJGaUMR9XEGtvQu%252FCaptcha.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2a17f7a-b2f9-4e7c-9ecc-2418d812845b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60e41247&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp#queueit-browser-extension)

Browser Extension

1.  **Download** Stellar-queue browser extension for Google Chrome: [Stellar AIO Chrome Extension V3arrow-up-right](https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/136nPcGwzFRLuLvtgaQyK1kVKf02QcQe9?usp=drive_link)
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAHRqmN8ivOO4vcejQx6C%252FSAIO%2520EXT%2520V3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee462893-1421-42c9-ab1e-b31c5e776cab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1764c6b4&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Extract All..."
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FU4ItmlMivPsAaw230rB8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df81ec76b-5f94-4d1e-b626-7e8f1bbab345&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cac4463d&sv=2)

1.  In Chrome, go to **Manage Extensions**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwmnhUm6l2azV30AUEHhH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39919511-46fa-40fe-a588-31df0675eec4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3b8f875&sv=2)

1.  On the top right corner of the Manage Extensions page turn on **Developer Mode** and click **Load Unpacked**. Now select the Stellar AIO Chrome Extension folder that you extracted, it'll be located in Downloads
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYh1VWAxvKbiCGcydttpw%252Fextensionfolder.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5464443f-2699-4242-a331-3e17f20f1143&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95661145&sv=2)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F82o0Ne5WzSNCZJRpllWT%252FSAIO%2520EXT%2520V3%2520Manage.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d4839ad-35ff-48f7-a4d0-def681f9a22b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64576229&sv=2)

1.  Go back to Chrome, click on the puzzle piece on the top right corner. You can now **pin** the **Stellar Extension** to your Chrome toolbar
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FEyuDqNyazdKsjlmpFEyR%252Fimageofextensionopen.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da28b28a7-236e-4955-91c0-a9508a5136c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c255a9f&sv=2)
