[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp#h_1373082702)

**Droppp**

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp#signup-mode)

**Signup Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fm7cPgdMGqf8DypV1u2Pa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D521d3770-92b1-406d-97e6-1d6af3587926&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a07f095a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp#queue-mode)

**Queue Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F1fQGyMpqrhTIxYlCIYQj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28c36412-bc26-4a41-9760-d0f15da05fd5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16e87de8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/dropp#purchaser-mode)

**Purchaser Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fk0QWoQjNGOByrkhYignw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0486c275-9ebc-489c-86bd-a96ab4412649&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ba6616d&sv=2)

*   What are the differences in the **modes**?
    
    *   **Signup mode** allows you to generate Dropp accounts in bot. These accounts generated will be automatically added to the Sessions tab. Stellar will automatically pull emails from IMAP you have setup in bot. The bot will use your profile email as your account email and the password field will override the default password
        
    *   **Queue mode** allows you to enter the queue for drop time
        
    *   **Purchaser mode** allows you to purchase items in this full request mode
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   We recommend a mix of ISPs, DCs or Resis
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What should I enter for **Password**?
    
    *   Enter the password you'd like to use for the account generation step in Signup mode
        
    
*   What is **Dropp Id**?
    
    *   The Dropp Id can be found in the product URL, it's the numbers after "drop" in the URL. Ex [https://droppp.io/drop/63/power-rangers-series-1/arrow-up-right](https://droppp.io/drop/63/power-rangers-series-1/)
         the Dropp Id is 63
        
    
*   What is **Pow Solve Type**?
    
    *   **GO** can handle more tasks and is generally faster than JS
        
    *   **JS** is more stable and current task limit is 200
        
    
*   What are the **Distribution Methods**?
    
    *   **Browser** will open a Chrome browser once it's time to purchase the item. The browser will open using the proxy that was used to pass queue. You need to have at least one [Captcha Harvester](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
         setup. You'll also need to have the [browser path](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-get-my-browser-path)
         setup in your Settings tab in bot
        
    *   **Link** will send you your link on your webhook. Proxy used to pass queue will be in the webhook
        
        ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2F568795724%2Fd82abd2bb894426aa162da1e%2FCapture325.PNG&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5b1e33f&sv=2)
        
    
*   Which **Captcha Provider** should I use?
    
    *   There are currently 3 captcha providers you can use. [CapMonster](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
        , [AYCD](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
         or [AntiCaptcha](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-anticaptcha)
        . You are welcome to choose your favorite but to give more information on Solver, it will open and use your Chrome browser as your captcha solver which will prompt you to solve captchas manually
        
    
*   What is **Quantity**?
    
    *   The amount of the product you are wanting to be in the cart at checkout. If left blank, then it is 1
        
    
*   What is **Minimum Price**?
    
    *   This allows StellarAIO to not purchase any items under the price inputted. Input the lowest dollar amount price of the product you would like to purchase
        
    
*   What is **Should AutoSolve**?
    
    *   If Droppp enforces a question, this allows Stellar to attempt to solve it

Error Message

Cause

Solution

Status 502

Dropp website issues

Let tasks run or restart tasks when website issues are resolved

# Newegg | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FWYKHKjkFoztdRIs3IK69%252Fnewegg.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9d94b20-d347-4469-8ebb-3a22545159d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39eff0b7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newegg#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Newegg, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newegg#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newegg#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FHgGIXkHI6ScfkBIwCbv2%252Fneweggmonitor1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D513a431a-b821-4f98-b3f4-30605c50c70a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d8a8bd2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newegg#desktop-mode)

Desktop mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fjoj9ANCFGe7F1RfBdoUN%252Fneweggdesktop1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D490fc98d-f057-4dd2-898c-93b506449f1b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ebeb150&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor your desired items. When an item restocks, your monitor mode tasks will ping your running watch tasks (Desktop mode) tasks to atc and checkout
        
    *   **Desktop mode** is your normal checkout mode
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs for monitoring and residentials for checkout tasks
        
        *   For Newegg, proxy quality is very important, use the highest quality proxies you have
            
        
    
*   Where do I find **SKU**?
    
    *   SKU can be found in the product URL. It will be towards the end of the URL
        
        *   Ex. [https://www.newegg.com/amd-ryzen-5-3600/p/N82E16819113569arrow-up-right](https://www.newegg.com/amd-ryzen-5-3600/p/N82E16819113569)
            
        *   Then find the Item number from the top bar as show below
            
        
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FM3lFCrcx9vDOn8GaYhNE%252FScreenshot%25202025-01-29%2520195725.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45187f53-67ef-45cd-8568-7850dec7057a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b61f395a&sv=2)

*   What is **Monitor Type**?
    
    *   **ATC** will monitor the frontend of Newegg
        
    *   **API** will monitor the backend of Newegg
        
        *   API is recommended but you may want to use a mix of both monitor types
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment between 4000 - 6000 delay. It's in milliseconds
        
        *   `5000`
            
        
    
*   What is **Reset Delay**?
    
    *   After your Monitor Mode task picks up a restock, it'll use your reset delay before monitoring again. So if you have a Reset Delay of 60000, it'll wait 60 seconds before attempting to monitor for the item again. We recommend having a high reset delay to prevent any spamming of your tasks being pinged
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   A good default to use is 1, but if the listing on the site allows for multiple in one cart then feel free to increase the QTY
        
    
*   What should my **Max Price** be?
    
    *   A max price is set to not purchase the item you want for resell price. For example, if you have an item which is $20 retail, the max price should be around $30
        
        *   Ex. 30
            
        
    
*   What is **Combo Mode** checkbox?
    
    *   Only check this box if the item is stated as a "Combo". You can find this out by going to the product page
        
        *   Ex. this product is combo [https://www.newegg.com/Product/ComboDealDetails?ItemList=Combo.4594456arrow-up-right](https://www.newegg.com/Product/ComboDealDetails?ItemList=Combo.4594456)
             the SKU is **4594456**
            
        
    
*   What is the **J1g Email Address** checkbox?
    
    *   Only check this box if you want to [j1g](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles)
         the email address to prevent blocks. Stellar will automatically j1g your email address from your profile
        
    
*   What is **Use TopCashBack?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [TopCashBack guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    

[PreviousNewBalancechevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newbalance)
[NextNike (FCFS)chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nike-fcfs)

Last updated 3 months ago

# NewBalance | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLoJ1FZfqY8vNP9q19ldB%252Fnew-balance-2-logo-png-transparent.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D561a2e90-0d98-4f71-9742-0a1570e918e8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b443915&sv=2)

[https://www.newbalance.com/arrow-up-right](https://www.newbalance.com/)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newbalance#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on NewBalance, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newbalance#new-balance-task-overview)

New Balance Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newbalance#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCSCj8XjrozKyyCx8Qamq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0623b37f-0eab-46e0-9683-573b777f99cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55904d2a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newbalance#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FOXJy5Wf1Ckk9skXx9ghg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f6b18a0-48d8-45ca-9e33-5f8fd90c35ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5da74e43&sv=2)

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to check for product availbility
        
    *   **Normal mode** allows you to use your profiles to purchase products fully automated
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   Both ISPs and Resis work. Localhost will not work
        
    
*   Where do I find **PIDs**?
    
    *   The **PIDs** are unique for a product on New Balance website usually located at the end of the product URL
        
        *   Ex. [https://www.newbalance.com/pd/fresh-foam-x-more-trail-v3/MTMORV3-MPS.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.newbalance.com/pd/fresh-foam-x-more-trail-v3/MTMORV3-MPS.html)
            
            *   The PID would be `MTMORV3-MPS`
                
            
        
    
*   What are **Variants**?
    
    *   **Variants** allow you to filter down to a specific product ID, color, size etc.
        
        *   Ex. `MTMORUD3-D-10,MTMORUD3-D-11`
            
            *   Make sure you split the variants with a comma like the above format
                
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment around 2000-4000 delays
        
    
*   What **Size** should I use?
    
    *   This field is optional by default but is required if you're running a product that has multiple sizes
        
        *   Ex. `L` for clothing. `11` for shoes or `Random` for random sizing
            
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousMenardschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/menards)
[NextNeweggchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/newegg)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Office | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FsixfpkdZJYianKkgBkKK%252F1560264344014.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2943f1e2-9769-45d0-86c4-9203ae732d4d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2dacd8b3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/office#office-task-overview)

Office Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/office#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Office, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/office#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F637zHbis6WpADfOxPVwa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd642a662-9801-4858-97b4-0004c9e24606&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd640fc5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/office#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FzDBizNRRV6b6JEbSsxk7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95f3f825-5ec4-4919-b3f5-a32fe3a00a50&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7495bee&sv=2)

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to check for product availability
        
    *   **Normal mode** is used for normal guest checkout
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **proxies** should I use?
    
    *   **DCs** and **ISPs** are the best due to speed but residentials also work but might have a large data usage
        
    
*   What is the **Product** **PID** and how do I get them?
    
    *   The **Product PID** is usually at the end of the product link (ex. [https://www.office.co.uk/view/product/office\_catalog/2,60/3921216608arrow-up-right](https://www.office.co.uk/view/product/office_catalog/2,60/3921216608)
        ) The PID for this product would be `3921216608`
        
    
*   What **Size** to use?
    
    *   Input the **Size** you'd like to run for. One size per task. For example `10.5`
        
        *   You can type `Random` for random sizing
            
        
    
*   Which **Currency** do I select?
    
    *   Select the currency that relates to your region USD, GBP or EUR
        
    
*   What is **Payment Method**?
    
    *   You can select Credit Card or PayPal
        
        *   **Credit Card** option is for full ACO
            
        *   **PayPal** option will send you a checkout link to you via webhook
            
        
    
*   What **delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment anywhere between 3000 and 5000
        
    
*   What is **Use Collect Method**?
    
    *   If selected, your product will be shipped to the closest store depending on your profile billing zip code
        
        *   Your profiles address must be identical to the format used on Office website. You can manually check via browser to see which address is working and use the exact format
            
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout

# AmazonV3 | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FZZSBuvZF5p8hMMfPWF6P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5adc8c10-3785-4c34-9df8-bc3e629dddcd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5bd7c4db&sv=2)

Our Amazon module supports account based checkout and offers several modes to handle monitoring, special restocks, timed drops and invite only releases. While Amazon uses strict bot protection, Stellar simplifies the process with automated logins, 2FA integration, OfferID support, and high speed task modes. This module is best suited for retail restocks, high demand products, household goods, collectibles and electronics that can appear or disappear from stock without warning.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#h_3e01888755)

**Amazon Video Guide**

`New video guide coming soon...`

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#quick-start-recommended-setup)

**Quick Start (Recommended Setup)**

_(For members who want a fast setup without reading everything)_

1.  Add your Amazon session under **Identities → Sessions** using **Request Login**
    
2.  Add your **2FA Authenticator Key** into your Amazon session
    
3.  Create 1-3 **Monitor tasks** for every SKU you want
    
4.  Run **Special Mode** checkout tasks for the same SKUs. You can run multiple checkout tasks per Amazon account allowing you to run for multiple products at the same time
    
5.  Use **ISP proxies**
    
6.  Before major drops, run a **test task** on an in stock item
    
7.  Use **OfferIDs only when required** (e.g., exact timed drops)
    
8.  Leave **Shipping Speed** field empty if your Amazon account has Prime membership
    
9.  Keep your **Amazon account updated** with default payment + address
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Amazon, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   ISPs recommended
>     
> *   Use login proxy for better session stability
>     
> *   DCs can be used
>     
> *   Avoid burning residentials for monitoring
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP proxies
>         
>     

*   **Amazon Accounts**
    

> *   Account required
>     
> *   Make sure billing, shipping, and payment methods are correct
>     
> *   Keep default address + default payment active
>     

*   **Authenticator App (Required)**
    

> *   Install Google Authenticator on your phone or computer (recommended)
>     
> *   Needed for Request Login setup
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#h_3e01888755-1)

**OfferID Overview**

An **OfferID (OID)** identifies the exact seller, price, and listing configuration.

*   OfferIDs are **unique to a specific item + seller**
    
*   Incorrect OID = buying incorrect or overpriced items
    
*   [Cookgroups](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
     usually supply accurate OfferIDs
    

> **Note:** When using OfferIDs, Stellar ignores the “Max Price” field because the OID already locks the exact offer.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#h_8da3b91861)

**Sessions & Login**

1.  Go to the **Identities** tab
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FGd6LcvDZ7a6RfzcYcBd9%252Famzsession.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0a94a76-8162-4d70-a260-91675e05bc31&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19f11af9&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Add Session** and name your Session
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSxi7jWExkJvbs3evhkjZ%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-24%2520162343.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df444014f-ae56-4ff0-953e-9811a4f828c6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7b30c8c&sv=2)

1.  Enter:
    

*   Region
    
*   Account Email
    
*   Account Password
    
*   Account Type - Personal or Business (If you only have a single account tied to your login, you can ignore this setting and keep your current setup.)
    
*   Authenticator Key (Request Login only)
    
*   CVV - Enter CVV of your payment method saved on your Amazon account that's set as Default/Preferred
    
*   Login Method - Request Login or Browser Login
    
*   Login Proxy - This is highly recommended for Amazon. This will heavily reduce the number of times you have to re-login for multiple tasks. ISP proxies are recommended
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FXdylHJahftogrJpzXenP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6420018-4436-4723-a66a-d4a65789f3e2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5c10549&sv=2)

Make sure you have Google Chrome on your computer, this is required for the login step

Here’s a **cleaned-up, shorter version** you can drop straight into the Amazon guide:

**Important:** If your Amazon accounts are **re-logging in frequently**, it’s usually proxy-related.

Use **clean ISP proxies assigned directly to your sessions**. Residential proxies rotate IPs, which forces Amazon to re-login on every change. A single clean session IP can stay stable for **1–2 weeks** without issues.

Avoid running **multiple tasks on the same account at the same time**. Logging in or checking out from different IPs simultaneously will almost always trigger a re-login.

For best results:

*   Assign **one dedicated, clean ISP** per Amazon account
    
*   Do not rotate session IPs
    
*   Avoid sharing accounts across tasks
    

Amazon aggressively protects accounts and re-login is one of their most common safeguards.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#account-type-setting-personal-vs-business)

**Account Type setting (Personal vs Business)**

Amazon sessions include an Account Type option that lets you choose whether the bot logs into a Personal or Business account.

*   **Only required for linked accounts** This is only needed if **one Amazon login has both Personal and Business accounts linked**. The selector tells Stellar which one to use during login
    
*   **Checkout remains fully automated** The module still handles checkout automatically. This setting only affects which account type is selected at login
    
*   **Troubleshooting** If login hangs or behaves unexpectedly, make sure you’re on the latest version and open a support ticket. Some Amazon logins return multiple variants that require additional handling
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#login-methods)

**Login Methods**

**Request Login (Recommended)**

Uses your [Authenticator Key](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#authenticator-app-required)
 to log in via request (no browser pop-up). Most stable and fastest.

**Browser Login**

A browser window will appear and Stellar will auto-fill your credentials. Use if Request Login is failing.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#h_50c8b20444)

**Authenticator Key Setup**

Required for Request Login

To setup and find your Amazon 2FA authenticator key follow these steps

1.  Login to your Amazon account and locate the **Account** section on the Amazon site
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F0NHbXBVcrIrTVURCP2ky%252Famzaccount.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D162cdc19-fedc-482d-a2d2-4c31fcd0b4fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=869fd40c&sv=2)

1.  Next go to the **Login and Security** tab
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FmoIuokUTZciVD6vxCToy%252Famzloginsecurity.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13c37790-fb14-452c-8d75-0af85fb8a110&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8a0d0b6&sv=2)

1.  Now click the **Edit** button next to (in the same row as) "Two-Step Verification (2SV) Settings:"
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FfuTQGZqDvhBdyOpa0wX4%252Famz2sv.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1f20cb2-33ff-4f13-a86e-9c3f32735b14&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b0162e3&sv=2)

1.  Click **"Get Started"**
    
2.  Click the **Authenticator App** option (Not the phone number one)
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F5gvZVXaugAzYv6LjC53Q%252F2svbackup.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db98ac2b2-ac51-4f75-b999-dc2c1e615fcc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a4c7d20&sv=2)

1.  Click the **"Cant scan the barcode?"** dropdown
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FECHZS2SMPIUxiVha2Pn6%252Fqrcode.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df80c8a1f-d861-4dfe-94c5-2f52ac966ae1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2cdfa93c&sv=2)

1.  Now copy the **authenticator key**, it should be in bold and around 30 characters, save this key somewhere (Will be needed later)
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYEHvBhuoghjTduuP1uEQ%252F2fakey.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D575ce372-a08a-4ac6-b5a6-2d1bf8b23db8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4216576&sv=2)

1.  Next scan the QR code with an authenticator app you have on your phone (Recommended to use Google Authenticator). **Scan the QR code** in the authenticator app and **enter the code** (usually 6 digits) that is generated into the OTP section above in Amazon.com. Click **Verify OTP and Continue**
    
2.  Enter your Authenticator Key (around 30 characters) into your Amazon session
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F8Zui06QHzeo3Pp6OmEp4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72d99f5e-e20f-4914-9a88-74e25cc942fb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b42f84be&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#h_50666e31cc)

**Amazon Mass Import Sessions**

To Mass Import Amazon accounts go to **Sessions** tab > Click **Mass Import Sessions**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FVcVGRWnbsVIwhI9fjCfd%252FMass.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91cfecff-3136-4d26-a10e-f912fdfe8bc5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dfe4540d&sv=2)

**Format:** `Email;Password;LoginProxy;Region;AuthenticatorKey`

or

**Format:** `Email;Password;;`

**Example:** `[[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;Stellar9;;USA;XXXX`

This is an example of a mass import account without a login proxy with the United States region REGION: You must put `USA` or `CA` as your region code, and an authenticator key. If no region is input then it will default to `USA`

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FtdnN1z5Bf90TgmaRR2oL%252FMass%2520Import.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1476276-151b-4474-9821-530c0c3db3da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f76dc40&sv=2)

Click **Save** once you're done

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#task-strategy-and-timing)

Task Strategy & Timing

**How Many Monitor Tasks Should I Create?**

*   Run **1 Monitor task per Tag Group**.
    
*   A single monitor can safely handle up to **30 SKUs** within one Tag Group.
    
*   You can run multiple Monitor tasks if you want redundancy, but it’s **not required** and usually unnecessary.
    
*   Monitor tasks are lightweight and can run 24/7.
    

**Recommended:** 1 Monitor task per Tag Group is sufficient for most users.

* * *

**How Many Checkout Tasks Per Account?**

*   **Strictly 1 checkout task per Amazon account using fast mode, you can run mulitple SKUs that does NOT match the fast mode SKU.**
    
*   Running more than one checkout task using fast mode on the same account will cause:
    
    *   Account locks
        
    *   Checkout failures
        
    *   Login/session instability
        
    

**Rule:** 1 account = 1 checkout task (no exceptions).

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#h_e7a25c9cd4)

**Task Overview**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#when-to-use-modes)

When to Use Modes

circle-exclamation

You need to have a default payment method, default shipping and billing information saved in your Amazon account. Make sure this is updated and Stellar will be using this information for your orders

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#special-mode-1)

**Special Mode**

*   Watch Task is ON by default
    
*   Works for Prime or non-Prime accounts
    
*   Best for most Amazon drops/restocks
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#fast-mode-1)

**Fast Mode**

*   **Strict 1 task per account, 1 ASIN per task** No multi-SKU support. Do not run more than one Fast task on the same account or you will get rate limited for several hours
    
*   **Simple setup, no monitors or captchas** Fast Mode does not require monitor tasks or captcha solving. Just enter ASIN, Offer ID (OID), quantity, delay and max price
    
*   **Delays and rate limits** You can run delays as low as 1000ms. If you hit rate limits, stop tasks and wait at least 2 hours before retrying
    
*   **Proxy and usage limits** 1–2 Fast tasks can run without proxies; more than that should use proxies. There is currently a limit of 20 Fast Mode tasks per instance. Fast Mode only supports US and UK Amazon regions
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#invite-mode-1)

**Invite Mode**

Used to request **Amazon Invite-Only** product access (e.g., PS5/GPUs historically).

This mode is only for EU / UK regions

You can enter multiple SKUs for Invite Mode

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#monitor-mode-1)

**Monitor Mode**

*   Required for all normal checkouts
    
*   Only monitors stock, does NOT checkout
    
*   Should match the SKU(s) of your checkout task
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#proxies)

Proxies

The best type of **proxies** to use are ISPs and DCs. This is because you can run your tasks for a longer period of time without eating away your residential data

*   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
     for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#bulk-csv-list)

Bulk CSV List

This option allows you to create monitor mode tasks in bulk so you don’t have to click and create them one by one. This will save you a lot of time.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#skus-and-input-list)

**SKUs & Input List**

**What is a SKU?**

Example link:

SKU = **B07RQ1HNFQ**

**Input List**

You may enter:

*   A single SKU (recommended)
    
*   SKU:OfferID format (only for spam ATC or timed drops)
    

You can enter multiple SKUs for Invite Mode

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#important)

Important

Using **SKU:OfferID** format in checkout tasks such as Special mode disables monitoring, it spams ATC directly. You cannot use SKU:ID format for monitor mode tasks.

This is only recommended for **precise timed drops**. It's not recommended to use this SKU:OID format for random restocks

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#offerid-section)

OfferID Section

Enter an OfferID supplied by your [cookgroup.](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)

OfferIDs look like long encoded strings:

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#delays)

**Delays**

_(Recommended — always test your own setup)_

**Monitor Mode**

*   ~5000ms
    

**Special Mode**

*   ~1000ms
    

**Cloud Mode**

*   ~1000ms
    

**Invite Mode**

*   ~1000ms

Use the region where the product is dropping.

**Quantity (QTY)**

Check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
, limits vary by item.

Amazon may auto adjust quantities even if you set 99.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#sessions)

**Sessions**

This lets you pick which stored Amazon session/account to use.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#monitoring-methods)

Monitoring Methods

**Fast Method**

*   Requires OfferID
    
*   Independent of account cookies
    
*   Less likely to soft ban proxies
    
*   Fastest monitoring
    

**Scrape Method**

*   Does NOT require OfferID
    
*   Reads frontend webpage
    
*   More prone to soft bans
    
*   Set proper price checks
    

**Business Method**

*   Designed for Amazon Business accounts
    
*   Uses Business specific stock and pricing
    
*   Recommended for Business only listings
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#captcha-provider)

**Captcha Provider**

*   Choose **Capmonster** if you want auto-solving
    
*   If left blank, the bot rotates proxies instead
    
*   Amazon eventually detects proxies; Capmonster helps prevent stalls
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#should-solve-captcha)

**Should Solve Captcha**

*   ON → solve captchas
    
*   OFF → rotate proxies instead
    

* * *

*   Stops task if site limit is reached

**Clip Discount**

*   Automatically clips coupons on product page

###

**Skip 3DS**

*   ON → attempts to skip 3DS challenge (faster, but riskier)
    
*   OFF → normal checkout flow; may require manual approval
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#use-topcashback)

**Use TopCashBack**

Earn cashback when enabled.

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#endless-mode)

**Endless Mode**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#endless-limit)

**Endless Limit**

Sets max number of checkouts (works only with Endless Mode enabled).

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/amazonv3#h_b51f24136c)

**Common Status Codes**

*   **Amazon Antibot | Rotating Proxy**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Account or proxy is being flagged by Amazon antibot during the flow
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Let the task run and allow proxies to rotate
            
        *   Try different proxies
            
        *   Increase task delays
            
        
    
*   **Captcha Detected | Rotating Proxy**
    
    *   _Cause:_ A captcha appeared during the flow
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Try different proxies
            
        *   Check if the account has a soft ban (dogs)
            
        *   If soft banned, let the account rest for a couple of days
            
        *   Temporarily switch login method to browser
            
        *   Restart task to log in, then switch back to request login
            
        
    
*   **Waiting For Monitor**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Waiting to be pinged from another source
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Let the task run
            
        *   Status will update once pinged from a monitor task or server-side
            
        
    
*   **Looping on “Placing Special Order” / “Waiting for Monitor” (no checkout)**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Usually an issue on the site’s end
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Manually re-enter CVV in your Amazon account
            
        *   Amazon periodically requires CVV re-entry
            
        
    
*   **Getting Rendered Addresses**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Proxy issue or ZIP code issue
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   If stuck for several seconds, change proxy list
            
        *   Do not use ZIP code if not needed
            
        *   ZIP code is mainly required for UK (not US)
            
        
    
*   **Adding to Cart 302**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Product went out of stock during checkout
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Restart tasks
            
        
    
*   **Failed to Find OID**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Bot issue
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Switch modes
            
        *   Try Special mode

# Shape | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FzM89nUd9SyQC6JCIxnNy%252FShape_Connect_full_color_whitebg_Logo-removebg-preview.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6958daa5-1c44-449a-8df6-a5b86a51e61b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52f1bedf&sv=2)

This module allows you create cookies for Target, Sportchek CA or Pokemon Center JP, these cookies are needed for login, monitoring and/or checkout

If you're running Target, we recommend you use the browser extension over the Shape module

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/shape#shape-task-overview)

Shape Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/shape#gen-mode)

Gen mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FbdWgvG9rYooQbLgbo6c5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc16de2d2-351a-49d9-a860-a02e6f6f0f4b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89b004cb&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Gen mode** will allow you to generate Shape cookies for sites like Target which need these cookies to purchase specific products
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs are most recommended but you can also try good quality resis
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is **Site**?
    
    *   Select the site you want to create cookies for
        
    
*   What is **Shape Intervals**?
    
    *   Time in ms you want to generate cookies
        
        *   Ex. `20000-30000` would be random number between 20 and 30 seconds
            
            *   Recommended to use `20000-30000`
                
            
        
    
*   What is **Cookie Expiration**?
    
    *   Time in ms how long you want the cookies to last
        
        *   Ex. `120000` would be 120 seconds
            
            *   Recommended to use `3600000`
                
            
        
    
*   What is **Endpoint?**
    
    *   Select the endpoint you want to generate cookies for
        
        *   Login: Generate cookies for login step
            
        *   ATC: Generate cookies for ATC/Checkout step
            
        
    
*   What is **Browser**?
    
    *   Select any browser you want
        
    
*   What is **Invisible**?
    
    *   This Invisible experimental feature allows cookies to be generated without displaying a browser window
        
        *   **Recommended usage:** Keep your current Shape setup and harvester count (both in-bot and extension) and switch **one harvester** to Invisible mode to test performance. At this time, device spoofing is not implemented so **do not increase your total number of harvesters** as this may increase the risk of device level Shape bans
            
        
    

[PreviousScotty Cameronchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scotty-cameron)
[NextShopDisneychevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/shopdisney)

Last updated 1 month ago

# QueueFair | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBp9TdQ03ddV6AZyzhgWR%252Fqueue-fair-removebg-preview.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87ec50f5-1ee1-4a6e-a6f1-c1943d545dac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cc9d42ad&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queuefair#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on QueueFair, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queuefair#queuefair-task-overview)

QueueFair Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queuefair#queue-mode)

**Queue Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCQRK8dgLA89puGvU8XBs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D851f51b9-9bd8-4250-b293-9afc5b5d1df3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c16de193&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Queue Mode** will allow you to wait in queue with multiple tasks at a time
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   Which **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and Resis are both OK
        
    
*   How do I find the **Queue** **URL**?
    
    *   **Queue URL** is the entire URL of the product queue
        
        *   For example [https://ravensburger.queue-fair.net/lorcana?target=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ravensburger.us%2Fproducts%2Fdisney-lorcana%2Ftrove-packs%2Fdisney-lorcana-the-first-chapter-tcg-illumineer-s-trove-11098174%2Findex.htmlarrow-up-right](https://ravensburger.queue-fair.net/lorcana?target=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ravensburger.us%2Fproducts%2Fdisney-lorcana%2Ftrove-packs%2Fdisney-lorcana-the-first-chapter-tcg-illumineer-s-trove-11098174%2Findex.html)
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Delays around 4000 are OK

# Offspring | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F7rRu6e9CF4O8nX7exBQ6%252FOffspring_Head%252BLogo.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9224be70-9fd9-44b9-966a-52a664ac5159&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=483f47fc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/offspring#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Offspring, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/offspring#queueit-browser-extension)

Browser Extension

1.  **Download** Stellar-queue browser extension for Google Chrome: [Stellar AIO Chrome Extension V3arrow-up-right](https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/136nPcGwzFRLuLvtgaQyK1kVKf02QcQe9?usp=drive_link)
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAHRqmN8ivOO4vcejQx6C%252FSAIO%2520EXT%2520V3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee462893-1421-42c9-ab1e-b31c5e776cab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1764c6b4&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Extract All..."
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FU4ItmlMivPsAaw230rB8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df81ec76b-5f94-4d1e-b626-7e8f1bbab345&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cac4463d&sv=2)

1.  In Chrome, go to **Manage Extensions**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwmnhUm6l2azV30AUEHhH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39919511-46fa-40fe-a588-31df0675eec4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3b8f875&sv=2)

1.  On the top right corner of the Manage Extensions page turn on **Developer Mode** and click **Load Unpacked**. Now select the folder that you extracted, it'll be located in Downloads
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F82o0Ne5WzSNCZJRpllWT%252FSAIO%2520EXT%2520V3%2520Manage.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d4839ad-35ff-48f7-a4d0-def681f9a22b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64576229&sv=2)

1.  Go back to Chrome, click on the puzzle piece on the top right corner. You can now **pin** the **Stellar Extension** to your Chrome toolbar
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/offspring#offspring-task-overview)

Offspring Task Overview

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fu8kX5xJIRYwpEWeVS1iN%252FXnip2025-07-18_21-46-56.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ae2de4c-4520-4199-9f08-692baf407c69&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=440d0fe9&sv=2)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fap9AThWVK4AZ4YJliURL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D731665c3-9b58-4be5-8903-f12175a3c068&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e9c18ab&sv=2)

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is used for normal guest checkout
        
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to monitor product availability, these tasks will notify/ping your Normal mode watch tasks
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **proxies** should I use?
    
    *   **DCs** and **ISPs** are the best due to speed but residentials also work but might have a large data usage
        
    
*   What is the **Product** **PID** and how do I get them?
    
    *   The **Product PID** is usually at the end of the product link (ex. [https://www.offspring.co.uk/view/product/offspring\_catalog/5,22/4142825243arrow-up-right](https://www.offspring.co.uk/view/product/offspring_catalog/5,22/4142825243)
         ) The PID for this product would be `4142825243`
        
    
*   What **Size** to use?
    
    *   Input the **Size** you'd like to run for. One size per task. For example `10.5`
        
        *   You can type `Random` for random sizing
            
        
    
*   Which **Currency** do I select?
    
    *   Select the currency that relates to your region USD, GBP or EUR
        
    
*   What is **Payment Method**?
    
    *   You can select Credit Card or PayPal
        
        *   **Credit Card** option is for full ACO
            
        *   **PayPal** option will send you a checkout link to you via webhook
            
        
    
*   What **delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment anywhere between 3000 and 5000
        
    
*   What is **Use Collect Method**?
    
    *   If selected, your product will be shipped to the closest store depending on your profile billing zip code
        
        *   Your profiles address must be identical to the format used on Offspring website. You can manually check via browser to see which address is working and use the exact format
            
        
    
*   What is a **Watch Task** and should I select it?
    
    *   The **Watch Task** option allows your checkout task (e.g., Normal mode) to work together with a **Monitor mode task**. Here's how it works:
        
        *   If you check this box, your **checkout task** will not monitor for restocks directly. Instead, it will wait for a **Monitor mode task** (with the same SKU) to detect a restock
            
            *   Once the Monitor task detects the restock, it will "ping" your running checkout (with the same SKU) tasks to ATC and checkout
                
            
        
        When using the **Watch Task** option:
        
        1.  Start your checkout task. It will display the message: **"Waiting for Monitor Ping."** This means it's ready and set up correctly
            
        2.  When the Monitor task detects a restock, it will automatically trigger the checkout task (with the same SKU) to run
            
        
        If you leave the **Watch Task** checkbox **unchecked**, the checkout task will act independently. It will monitor the SKU itself, add the item to your cart, and checkout directly
        
    

[PreviousOfficechevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/office)
[NextPaninichevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Preliminary Checklist](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/offspring#preliminary-checklist)
    
*   [Browser Extension](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/offspring#queueit-browser-extension)
    
*   [Offspring Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/offspring#offspring-task-overview)

# Costco US/CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1000logos.net%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2021%2F04%2FCostco-logo-500x281.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=84d9c19e&sv=2)

Our Costco module supports account based checkout and is designed to handle both API and frontend monitoring, multiple queue entry attempts and standard add to cart flows. Costco often uses queues, strict cart validation and fast sellouts but Stellar streamlines the process with session based logins, watch task pairing and optional queue farm setups. This module performs best for high demand products, electronics, limited drops and products known to appear with little warning.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#quick-start-recommended-setup)

**Quick Start (Recommended Setup)**

1.  Add your Costco session under **Identities → Sessions**.
    
2.  Make sure your Costco account has **default shipping address** saved.
    
3.  Create profiles with full billing, shipping, and payment information.
    
4.  Run:
    
    *   **1 Monitor task** per product (API or ATC)
        
    *   **1 Normal mode checkout task** per account
        
    
5.  Clear your Costco cart **before starting tasks**.
    
6.  If the product uses a QueueIt system, run **Queueit Mode** tasks (hundreds recommended) and enable _Wait for Queue Pass_ on your Normal mode checkout task. Don't use watch task for normal mode if Queueit system is live
    
7.  Use ISPs, DCs, or resi proxies depending on your setup.
    
8.  Keep checkout delay low (around 2000 ms).
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Costco, make sure you have everything below prepared:

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#profiles)

**Profiles**

> *   Accounts are **required** for checkout.
>     
> *   Account email must match the profile email for best performance.
>     
> *   Make sure default shipping address is saved inside your Costco account.
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#proxies)

**Proxies**

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#costco-accounts)

**Costco Accounts**

> *   Accounts are **required** for checkout.
>     
> *   Account email must match the profile email for best performance.
>     
> *   Make sure default shipping address is saved inside your Costco account.
>     

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#cook-group-access)

**Cook Group Access**

> Optional but recommended. Your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#test-task)

**Test Task**

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#h_d1a2cff968)

**Sessions & Login**

1\. Go to **Sessions** tab

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FVWmI5zgMGyeIefsEx2NR%252FCostco%2520Session.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b0617c9-c2bf-489b-9525-4bbfc8c4c4af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e49ec2e9&sv=2)

2\. Click on **Add Session**

3\. Enter:

*   **Session Name**
    
*   **Email** (Costco account email)
    
*   **Password** (Costco account password)
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F3agKJfHopvW1bRfLYxpS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D011a351a-f89e-41ca-b101-edf29663dabe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62d6cab1&sv=2)

4\. Click **Save**

5 . Session logs in automatically when starting a **Normal mode** task

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#task-strategy-and-timing)

Task Strategy & Timing

**How Many Monitor Tasks Should I Create?**

*   Run **1 Monitor task per SKU**.
    
*   You can run multiple Monitor tasks if you want redundancy, but it’s **not required** and usually unnecessary.
    
*   Monitor tasks are lightweight and can run 24/7.
    

**Recommended:** 1 Monitor task per SKU is sufficient for most users.

* * *

**How Many Checkout Tasks Per Account?**

*   **Strictly 1 checkout task for each SKU per Costco account.**
    
*   Running more than one checkout task on the same account can cause:
    
    *   Account locks
        
    *   Checkout failures
        
    *   Login/session instability
        
    
*   you can run as many queueit tasks as your pc can handle as those do not use accounts.
    

**Rule:** 1 account = 1 checkout task (no exceptions).

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#task-overview)

Task Overview

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FC304EjcCKjGeOjMRG4Q2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded20a07c-9882-46aa-b136-b8fd1c4c1773&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c4965a3&sv=2)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fohcec7YFQoEAHrScavZ9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D369dee0f-df1d-41a5-b81b-ab5392fb2f41&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3be13157&sv=2)

**Queueit Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwRwtgtk5a4T4kwGCxhNB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd66dd9f4-f082-413c-bd07-f2190c168077&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64503870&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#when-to-use-modes)

When to Use Modes

circle-info

**Important:** Your Costco account **logs in when tasks start**, not when the session is created. **Always clear your cart manually before running tasks.**

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#normal-mode-checkout-mode)

**Normal Mode (Checkout Mode)**

*   Standard checkout flow
    
*   Logs in → ATC → checkout
    
*   Uses session credentials
    
*   Best for direct restocks and fast moving items
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

*   Monitors the product (API or ATC)
    
*   Pings any checkout task with **Watch Task enabled**
    
*   Does not add to cart or checkout
    
*   Unlimited number of monitor tasks allowed
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#queueit-mode)

**Queueit Mode**

*   Creates many queue entries
    
*   Each task receives a different queue position
    
*   When a task passes queue, it pings your **Normal Mode** checkout task (if “Wait for Queue Pass” is enabled)
    
*   Ideal when Costco uses QueueIt for hot products
    
*   Users often run **hundreds** of Queueit Mode tasks
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#profile)

**Profile**

*   Select the profile you want to use for checkout
    
*   If “Use Account Address” is off → uses profile’s address
    
*   If “Use Account Address” is on → uses Costco account default address (recommended)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#proxies-1)

**Proxies**

You may use:

*   ISP
    
*   DC
    
*   Residentials
    
    *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    

All three work depending on your strategy and budget.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#product-url)

**Product URL**

Find the product on Costco and copy the full product URL.

Example:

Paste into your task’s URL field.

Your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
 will provide product URLs

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#monitor-type)

**Monitor Type**

*   **ATC** → frontend monitoring (via Costco.com)
    
*   **API** → backend monitoring
    
    *   Usually detects faster
        
    *   More intense on proxies
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#delays)

**Delays**

Recommended:

*   **Monitor Delay:** ~5000 ms
    
*   **Checkout Delay:** ~1000 ms
    
*   **Reset Delay:** ~5000 ms
    

Adjust based on your proxies and cook group guidance.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#quantity-qty)

**Quantity (QTY)**

*   Check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
     for product specific quantity rules
    
*   Stellar does _not_ auto adjust if you set quantity too high
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#session)

**Session**

Allows you to pick which Costco session to use for the task.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#queue-captcha-provider)

**Queue Captcha Provider**

Choose how to solve Costco QueueIt captchas:

*   [**Bot**](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
     → built-in harvester
    
*   [**Capsolver**](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capsolver)
     → automatic via third-party
    
*   [**Capmonster**](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
     → automatic via third-party
    
*   [**AYCD**](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
     → via AYCD toolbox
    

Configure depending on your provider.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#login-method)

Login Method

Costco is known for frequently **temp banning or flagging accounts**, which can interrupt task flow. To help with this, Stellar supports **Passcode (OTP) Login**, allowing you to fetch the verification code through **IMAP** or **Manual Input**.

At the moment, OTP Login works even on temporarily flagged accounts, but Costco may tighten security at any time. For best results, we recommend running a **50/50 mix of Regular Login and OTP Login**, while still using **one account per task**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#use-account-address-recommended)

**Use Account Address (Recommended)**

*   ON → uses address saved in Costco account
    
*   OFF → uses Stellar profile address
    

ON is recommended for smoother checkouts.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#skip-cart-clear)

**Skip Cart Clear**

*   ON → wont clear cart upon starting task meaning you will check out item(s) you already have carted in your account along with the item you're running in bot
    
*   OFF → cart will be cleared upon starting task
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#send-cart-webhook)

**Send Cart Webhook**

*   ON → You'll receive a [Discord webhook](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-to-set-up-discord-notifications)
     when your task carts an item
    
*   OFF → No Discord webhook will be sent
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#task-stop-after-carting)

**Task Stop After Carting**

*   ON → Your task will stop after successfully carting your item(s)
    
    *   **Open Browser (Globe Icon)** The globe icon allows you to open a logged in browser session directly from a running task with the account already authenticated and ready to checkout. This is especially useful for users running a few accounts or troubleshooting ACO issues as it lets you manually complete checkout without restarting tasks
        
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FNj4gwi4t11xiLyu7E1oh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb4ae6fc-7eca-4cf1-b0cd-79b4ca864941&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1a89665&sv=2)
    
    Image of the globe icon
    
*   OFF → Your task will not stop after successfully carting your item(s), it'll continue the normal ACO process and attempt to checkout
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#watch-task)

**Watch Task**

Helps reduce proxy bans and improve speed.

If enabled:

*   Checkout task waits for Monitor task
    
*   Monitor task pings checkout when product is in stock
    
*   Checkout task immediately starts ATC + checkout
    

If disabled:

*   Checkout task monitors, ATCs, and checkouts independently
    
*   Higher request load
    

Disable Watch Task if product is using queue system

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#wait-for-queue-pass)

Wait For Queue Pass

*   ON → Your task will wait for a queueit mode task to pass queue before attempting to checkout
    
*   OFF → Your task will not wait for a queueit mode task to pass queue
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#common-errors-and-fixes)

Common Errors and Fixes

*   **Akamai Ban**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Account- or proxy-related issue
        
    *   _Fix:_
        
        *   Try different proxies
            
        *   Reset the Costco account password
            
        
    
*   **Kasada Ban**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Account- or proxy-related issue
        
    *   _Fix:_
        
        *   Try different proxies
            
        *   Reset the Costco account password
            
        
    
*   **Waiting For Monitor**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Normal status message
        
    *   _Fix:_
        
        *   Task is waiting for a monitor-mode task or server-side monitor
            
        *   Will proceed once the product is detected in stock
            
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/costco-us-ca#costco-queue-drop-faq)

Costco Queue Drop FAQ

**Do I use the regular Queue-It module or Costco module?**

*   Use **Costco module** with **Wait for Queue Pass** enabled and **Queue-It MODE** tasks started.
    

**How many Queue-It tasks should I run?**

*   There’s no fixed number, but don’t run 10–20 tasks. That won’t pass in time.
    

**Do I use residential proxies or ISPs?**

*   Use a mix of both and see what performs better for you.
    

**Is it one account per task?**

*   Yes. Strictly one account per task.
    
*   Using multiple tasks on one account will clip it instantly.
    

**Do I use “Stop Task After Carting”?**

*   Use it if you constantly have issues with ACO.
    
*   Some members prefer manual checkout because Costco’s protection can be inconsistent.
    

**I’m using AMEX and my tasks are showing errors - what do I do?**

*   AMEX isn’t supported at Costco. Only Visa and Mastercard work.
    

**“adding to cart - akamai ban”**

*   Proxy block. Try different providers - ideally residential proxies.
    

**“initiating checkout - akamai ban”**

*   Account temporary block or proxy block.
    
*   Try running tasks with **Stop Task After Carting** enabled and check out manually.
    
*   If you see **ERR\_HTTP2\_PROTOCOL\_ERROR** or **“Costco mobile services unavailable”**, it’s a 100% account block. Let the account rest for a while.
    

**“error submitting order - server error”**

*   Caused by profile issues or Costco itself.
    
*   We pushed three updates to improve handling of this error, but if it’s profile-related it may not be solvable.
    
*   Test your profile on an in-stock item:
    
    *   If it works, it’s site-related and our updates should improve it further.
        
    

**Where do I check out once my task carts and I have “Stop Task After Carting” enabled, or when the task tells me to check out manually after failing Akamai on initiating checkout?**

You have three options:

1.  **Globe icon next to the task status**
    
    *   This loads your logged-in session directly.
        
    *   Just follow the normal checkout steps.
        
    *   [More info herearrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417581701315428493/1450832305089286215)
        
    
2.  **Open Browser in Sessions**
    
    *   Same as the globe icon next to the task.
        
    *   Opens the session with your account already logged in.
        
    *   [More info herearrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1417577339671285984/1417581701315428493/1450832305089286215)
        
    
3.  **External browser or tools (e.g. AYCD)**
    
    *   Possible, but very time-consuming.
        
    *   This is why using the in-bot browser is strongly recommended.
        
    

**In-bot browser requirement**

*   Chrome must be installed in the default system path.
    
*   Just install Chrome normally and it will configure itself automatically.
    

[PreviousCanon UKchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/canon-uk)
[NextCrocschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/crocs)
