# Pokemon Center JP | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwuNHXdQIhWEbxmO4OOvs%252Fimages.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbbfc5f39-9392-4044-8de4-b514aebf07fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee40cc77&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center-jp#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Pokemon Center JP, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center-jp#adding-accounts)

Adding Accounts

1.  Navigate to Accounts tab in bot and click on Pokemon Center JP
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FpDBS4VqaERhPjVujSXSa%252FPKC%2520JP%2520ACC.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D910c9471-91c0-484b-928e-c3e1ce72e37b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b231322&sv=2)

1.  Click 'Add Account'
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FR1ONClHaS0WuobPE06EK%252FAdd%2520Account.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39356015-cdce-403b-85c1-216812888760&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=304a6d8e&sv=2)

1.  Enter your account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FUzqXF3i7FU3EJroPErx0%252FAcc%2520Setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df71eb6c1-6058-44bb-af49-012bb42d5ca1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee3882d8&sv=2)

1.  Click 'Add' and your account info can be used for future purchases
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center-jp#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center-jp#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgyBkyZuhUVVpufInRKjv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D906138b3-c759-4ef9-92ae-ea3ebb2c99d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=983f4f59&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center-jp#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F6cSGekzBsz3oVgbdB42K%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D461a4590-22c1-404e-a0ab-731ac557ae20&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c00f02aa&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center-jp#account-gen-mode)

Account Gen Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fyx29vwxbfISLP25mOOwb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43dfd616-3451-4201-a976-1470ad876033&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16a19a00&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is used for normal account checkouts
        
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to check for product availability
        
    *   **Account Gen mode** is used to generate accounts for Pokemon Center JP
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   **DCs** and **ISPs** are the best due to speed but residentials also work but might have a large data usage
        
    
*   What is the **PID** and how do I get it?
    
    *   The **PID** is usually at the end of the product URL (ex. [https://www.pokemoncenter-online.com/?p\_cd=4521329331362arrow-up-right](https://www.pokemoncenter-online.com/?p_cd=4521329331362)
        ) PID for this product is `4521329331362`
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment anywhere between 3000 and 5000
        
    
*   What is **Product Quantity**?
    
    *   Enter the number of products you'd like to checkout
        
    
*   What is **Payment Method**?
    
    *   You can select COD or Credit Card as your payment method
        
    
*   What is **Account**?
    
    *   This option is to select the account you would like to checkout on. These accounts are entered through the [Accounts tab of Stellar](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center-jp#adding-pokemon-center-jp-accounts)
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout

[NextPopmartchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart)

# Does StellarAIO support Mac and Windows? | Stellar

**Yes, StellarAIO supports Mac and Windows!** When there's a new update, the windows version update is released first and the Mac version is available shortly after. Make sure you are up to date with #change-log channel in the StellarAIO Discord server for updated downloaded links and notes!

# FunkoShop | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flogodownload.org%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2019%2F08%2Ffunko-logo-0.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=380b9320&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on FunkoShop, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop#h_bfc14e47bb)

**Adding Accounts**

To add your FunkoShop accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Sessions** tab > **Accounts** > Click on **FunkoShop**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgBGahkBHQARsDTl43Ijn%252FFunko%2520Account.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b6d4e26-ad7e-45e3-a7fb-080edc5642fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8c0a45e&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Account** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAmGlG1s1DRCvZeIXCkaS%252FAdd%2520Account.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7bbb9ed-e0a8-49e1-a0a4-ec198e13937a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93503c1b&sv=2)

1.  Enter your account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FxbSTOWtFD3e8H2xZjf8j%252FAcc%2520Setup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D36ee1bd9-80b9-44de-860c-507f27013668&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa605ffb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop#h_bfc14e47bb-1)

**FunkoShop Task Overview**

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop#normal-mode)

**Normal mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBeRn7wgtqPaXzDhlW2cE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D687fe7e1-90f3-4a39-820b-4184ca583dc3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=698ccf27&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop#draw-mode)

**Draw mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FP2slfseF3PvelTrfswjD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df16f08c7-4e68-4192-abb0-a739cdaa5d90&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6107da98&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop#monitor-mode)

**Monitor mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FtWcwwRy0X8aIfKEnDWI7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ac79089-30ea-42aa-9cae-dbbf71107b8d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=61e2f836&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop#acc-gen-mode)

**Acc Gen mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FKW9mIQ8bI1RzhwXfNL6K%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc8a5590-9a44-4bba-8f63-53b487607f2f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=587d5de1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/funkoshop#reset-password-mode)

**Reset Password mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FoGoFuMFyHKKjM8BvL5Dh%252FScreenshot%25202026-02-28%2520at%25204.34.42%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D680f0ae4-0919-4b27-b72e-b5f3382792b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7dea2a83&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to check for product availability
        
    *   **Normal mode** uses guest checkout if an account is not selected. These tasks auto registers for fan rewards as well
        
    *   **Draw mode** is used to enter Funko draws. These tasks auto registers for fan rewards as well
        
    *   **Account-gen mode** is used to create Funko accounts
        
    *   **Reset Password Mode** - Used to reset the password to the account, the new password is automatically updated within the account session.
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   FunkoShop typically allows all types of proxies from DCs to ISPs to Resis
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is a **SKU** and how do I get it?
    
    *   Look for the item you want to run for. An example link would be [https://funko.com/pop-barry-allen-in-monkey-robe/66635.htmlarrow-up-right](https://funko.com/pop-barry-allen-in-monkey-robe/66635.html)
         and the SKU would be **66635**
        
    
*   What **Quantity** do I use?
    
    *   FunkoShop may have quantity limits for certain hyped products (if so, set it to those) Overall it is recommended to use 1
        
    
*   What **Delay** should I use?
    
    *   This is highly dependent on how many proxies you own, if running 24/7 on FunkoShop, it is recommended to go no less than 6000 delay, unless you have a lot of proxies to work with
        
    
*   What's **Is Points Drop?** option?
    
    *   This should be enabled for **Funko points drops** where purchasing requires an account. Since monitoring on Funko is account-less, relying on Watch Tasks can be unreliable during these drops
        
        *   The recommended and most reliable solution is to **enable Is Points Drop** and don't use watch task. When enabled the task will add the item to cart and proceed to checkout immediately without waiting for a monitor ping
            
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task**?
    
    *   The **Watch Task** option allows your checkout task (e.g., Normal mode) to work together with a **Monitor mode task**. Here's how it works:
        
        *   If you check this box, your **checkout task** will not monitor for restocks directly. Instead, it will wait for a **Monitor mode task** (with the same SKU) to detect a restock
            
            *   Once the Monitor task detects the restock, it will "ping" the checkout (with the same SKU) task to run. The checkout task will then add the item to your cart and proceed to checkout
                
            
        
        When using the **Watch Task** option:
        
        1.  Start your checkout task. It will display the message: **"Waiting for Monitor Ping."** This means it's ready and set up correctly
            
        2.  When the Monitor task detects a restock, it will automatically trigger the checkout task (with the same SKU) to run
            
        
        If you leave the **Watch Task** checkbox **unchecked**, the checkout task will act independently. It will monitor the SKU itself, add the item to your cart, and checkout directly
        
    
*   What is Captcha Provider?
    
    *   Select a Captcha Provider to solve the captchas this site has
        
        *   [Bot](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
            
        *   [AYCD](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
            
        *   [Capmonster](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
            
        *   [Capsolver](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capsolver)
            
        
    
*   What is **IMAP Session**?
    
    *   You'll need to select a precreated [IMAP Session](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/imap-overview)
         for account-gen mode
        
    
*   What is **Catchall**?
    
    *   You can use your [catchall](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/catchall-email-guide)
         domain to create accounts
        
    

[PreviousFraserschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/frasers)

# How do I create a Task Group? | Stellar

One of the main ideas behind task groups is that each one will be Site-specific. Making task organization much easier since all tasks within that task group will be using the same site.

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F0G3fSRkyk1jfiYmFnkzZ%252Fplussign.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93bd9ea0-1164-4ea5-8433-824d550827c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34f9f6ec&sv=2)

After clicking on the green + sign you'll be prompted to enter a group name and to select a site

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAYwskxGa5Lmc8A6LwJO1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f3e01e2-7043-4bfc-bd7f-6683d081897e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6b530a2&sv=2)

[NextHow do I delete a Task Group?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tasks-tab/how-do-i-delete-a-task-group)

# How much does StellarAIO cost? | Stellar

Stellar AIO offers multiple plans to fit different budgets and commitment levels:

*   **Quarterly** – $199 every 3 months
    
*   **Yearly** – $599 per year
    
*   **Lifetime** – $1499 one-time payment
    

All plans include full access to the Stellar AIO bot, real-time support, guides and our active Discord community

View or purchase a plan here: [https://whop.com/stellaraio/arrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio/)

# Toys R Us CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2Fa%2Fa7%2FToys_%2522R%2522_Us_logo.svg%2F450px-Toys_%2522R%2522_Us_logo.svg.png%3F20200426234115&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=119fc712&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/toys-r-us-ca#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Toys R Us CA, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/toys-r-us-ca#toys-r-us-ca)

Toys R Us CA


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/toys-r-us-ca#guest-mode)

Guest Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F5u6O17sGm4PWP7s6zlw5%252FToys%2520R%2520Us%2520CA%2520Guest.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9f5288d-f4bd-4761-9ee1-ac6feb5ba088&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4014ec6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/toys-r-us-ca#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F8AoBBgvfL5yqnpdoVsxz%252FMonitor.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e0ce9c8-52ff-4f19-b401-32cffe9a7672&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a5509f47&sv=2)

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   Only one mode is available for Toys R Us CA. This mode is guest and will use guest checkout when attempting to checkout.
        
    
*   What type of **proxies** should I use?
    
    *   DCs and ISPs are the best for Toys R Us CA due to speed. Residentials also work but may have high usage.
        
    
*   What is a **SKU** and how do I get them?
    
    *   A SKU is an item-specific identification ID that is special only to a single item. Toy R Us SKUs tend to be near the end of the link. (ex. [https://www.toysrus.ca/en/Pokemon---Lights-and-Sounds---Pikachu/74B2F99F.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.toysrus.ca/en/Pokemon---Lights-and-Sounds---Pikachu/74B2F99F.html)
        , the SKU is 74B2F99F)
        
    
*   What **delays** should I use?
    
    *   For Toys R Us Ca, any delay between 3000 and 5000 is good for running 24/7
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   A good QTY to use is 1. The reason is that most items (more hyped items) have a 1 per cart limit and possibly a 1 per person or household limit. Most orders wont be able to place if there is more than 1 quantity in the cart.
        
    

If you're receiving an error message you can look here in the Status Codes article

[PreviousTopps US & EUchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu)
[NextVery UKchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/very-uk)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Toys R Us CA](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/toys-r-us-ca#toys-r-us-ca)

# Smyths Toys | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FEUa04jt7eC1mrLPFNn12%252Fimages-removebg-preview.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd60dbf01-f09e-460d-bd1c-f857ec4c5efb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24ea9c0e&sv=2)

UK region only

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/smyths-toys#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Smyths Toys, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/smyths-toys#task-overview)

Task Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/smyths-toys#shipping-mode)

Shipping mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FePoNoqf6V2Nlv7Kx336h%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd26c0a65-3554-4ded-8718-3dcfd3bdf0df&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=effc940b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/smyths-toys#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdE2UMUcdacEsClQIfNMu%252Fsmyth2.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31e5a3db-5599-43a9-8c11-a67c60e29cc5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c820a35&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor and ping your watch tasks when they detect the item you're monitoring is in stock
        
    *   **Shipping mode** is your checkout task is to be used for normal checkout flow
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   You need to use high quality proxies, usually ISPs but can also use resis
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is **Product URL**?
    
    *   For example [https://www.smythstoys.com/uk/en-gb/brand/pokemon/pokemon-trading-cards-game/pokemon-trading-card-game-tcg-scarlet-and-violet-stellar-crown-elite-trainer-box/p/237414arrow-up-right](https://www.smythstoys.com/uk/en-gb/brand/pokemon/pokemon-trading-cards-game/pokemon-trading-card-game-tcg-scarlet-and-violet-stellar-crown-elite-trainer-box/p/237414)
        
    
*   What is **QTY**?
    
    *   The number of items you want in one order
        
    
*   What is **Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error
        
        *   You can start your delays around `2000` and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
            
        
    
*   What is **Monitoring Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product
        
        *   You can start your delays around `5000` and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
            
        
    
*   What is **Reset Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product again after it has detected the item is in stock
        
        *   You can start your delays around `5000` and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
            
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousShopifychevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/shopify)
[NextSportChek CAchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/sportchek-ca)

# How do I delete a Task Group? | Stellar

# BestBuy | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2Ff%2Ff5%2FBest_Buy_Logo.svg%2F2560px-Best_Buy_Logo.svg.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13258bff&sv=2)

Our Best Buy module supports both account based and guest checkout, with dedicated modes for shipping, pickup, account generation, monitoring and invite flows. Best Buy is heavily queue based, but Stellar helps manage sessions, IMAP verification, and monitor to checkout workflows so you can focus on timing and product selection. This module is ideal for high demand products, electronics, GPUs, consoles, PCs and accessories that release in waves, use queues or restock at random.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#h_360c341843)

**Video Guide**

`New video guide coming soon...`

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#quick-start-recommended-setup)

**Quick Start (Recommended Setup)**

1.  Add your Best Buy account under **Identities → Best Buy.**
    
2.  Enable **IMAP** for your email so Stellar can auto pull Best Buy verification codes.
    
3.  Create profiles with matching **email = Best Buy account email**.
    
4.  For each SKU, run:
    
    *   **1 Monitor task** **per SKU** (Monitor and/or Monitor-zip modes)
        
    *   **Strictly 1 Shipping task OR 1 Pickup task** per account per SKU
        
    
5.  Use **ISPs for monitoring** and **residentials for checkout**.
    
6.  Before big drops, **reset passwords** the day before using unique proxies per account.
    
7.  Use **Watch Task** for restocks so Monitor tasks do the heavy lifting.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on BestBuy, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Best Buy Accounts**
    

> *   Required for account based checkout.
>     
> *   Each session stores login, proxies, and (optionally) tax exempt details.
>     

*   **IMAP (Highly Recommended)**
    

> *   Lets Stellar automatically pull Best Buy verification codes from your email.
>     
> *   Greatly reduces friction during resets/logins.
>     

*   **Password Reset (Optional Strategy)**
    

> Resetting your Best Buy account passwords the day before a drop can help reduce queue loops and weird login behavior.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profile, account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#h_360c341843-1)

**Sessions & Login**

Follow the steps below to start adding your BestBuy accounts to Stellar. If you have a lot of accounts and want to mass import them quickly go [here](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#mass-import-accounts)

1\. Go to **Identities** tab and select **BestBuy**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FyDef9HKkntqO6RdwqXgc%252FBB%2520Session.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15beb639-2ae0-49a7-917d-cd2cd7f9fd77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6bedc01&sv=2)

2\. Click on **Add Session** and name your Session

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F2RocydSBfY5Ti4g1ffK1%252FAdd%2520Session.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f55a88e-cf78-47f3-89e8-585833018c22&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3836551&sv=2)

3\. Fill fields:

*   **Email** – Best Buy account email
    
*   **Password** – Best Buy account password
    
*   **Login Proxy** – ISP proxy recommended (used for queues + login)
    
*   **Tax Exempt Number** – if using business account with tax exemption
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FpHayu76M3o43WWr9VJjQ%252Fbbsession.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D889b6d95-1b6b-4574-a5fb-4406a2fdb3cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd02d229&sv=2)

4\. Click **Save** and your Session should say **Ready To Login**. Your task will log into your account upon starting. The BestBuy account email has to exactly match (case sensitive) the email you have in your [profile](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/profile-overview)
. You can run a test task on an in stock item to ensure everything is setup correctly. Your sessions will then change to **Ready** once your task once was able to log into your Best Buy account successfully

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#sessions-stages)

**Sessions Stages**

*   **Not Ready** – Session missing or invalid email/password
    
*   **Ready To Login** – Session created; will log in when a task starts
    
*   **Ready** – Session successfully logged in
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#mass-import-sessions)

Mass Import Sessions

1.  Go to the **Identities tab** in bot and click on BestBuy. Then click the **Mass Import Sessions** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FO9Wd7mnYJWas66x4rug9%252Fmass%2520import.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D401f6635-d616-4381-ad9c-54939d080ded&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7fe8a66c&sv=2)

1.  Paste in your accounts following the format in the text box `Email;Password;` For example
    
    *   [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1231!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1232!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1233!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1234!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1235!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1236!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1237!;
        
    
2.  Save
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#h_fea44d7fbf)

**IMAP Overview**

*   Add an IMAP session
    
*   Connect your email provider
    
*   Select it in your Best Buy task under **IMAP Session**
    

Follow your [IMAP guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/imap-overview)
 to:

*   Faster logins
    
*   Smoother password resets
    
*   Less manual code entry
    

IMAP lets Stellar read verification codes sent by Best Buy automatically.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#h_8c874beeca)

**Password Reset Strategy**

Sometimes queue times/loops improve after a fresh password reset.

Basic In Bot Flow

1.  Create Reset mode task
    
2.  Select Profile (same email as BestBuy account)
    
3.  Select high quality proxies
    
4.  Select IMAP session
    
5.  Start task
    

**Basic Desktop Flow (per account):**

1.  Turn on your proxy switcher (e.g., BP Proxy Switcher).
    
2.  Assign a **unique proxy per Best Buy account**.
    
3.  Go to bestbuy.com.
    
4.  Sign in → go to **Account Settings**.
    
5.  Click **Change Your Password**.
    
6.  Enter current password + new password.
    
7.  Save changes.
    
8.  Repeat steps with a new proxy for each account.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#task-strategy-and-timing)

Task Strategy & Timing

**How Many Monitor Tasks Should I Create?**

*   Run **1 Monitor task per SKU**.
    
*   You can run multiple Monitor tasks if you want redundancy, but it’s **not required** and usually unnecessary.
    
*   Monitor tasks are lightweight and can run 24/7.
    

**Recommended:** 1 Monitor task per SKU is sufficient for most users.

* * *

**How Many Checkout Tasks Per Account?**

*   **Strictly 1 checkout task for each SKU per Bestbuy account.**
    
*   Running more than one checkout task per sku on the same account can cause:
    
    *   Account locks
        
    *   Checkout failures
        
    *   Login/session instability
        
    

**Rule:** 1 account = 1 checkout task (no exceptions).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#h_95e81b9b2a)

**Task Overview**

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#reset-mode)

**Reset Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fcds0ZqvMahTUpPwW0DVB%252Fbbresetmode.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe853b37-0e35-445a-acd1-27558a9153cc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7881cf7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#account-gen-mode)

**Account-Gen Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FWgOd7oUJDTTy15BzTRI6%252Fbbaccountgen.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87666fce-a56e-4c3b-a9dc-cbec9788f666&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aa4cbec7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#shipping-mode)

**Shipping Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FNQ9aEkoR1O8mfNIM6qRY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd227ebd1-7fa3-4523-8bfb-0ad0ccf96245&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d80a4d5b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#pickup-mode)

**Pickup Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAppsJ0igol6w6zj4PY8b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b31ff18-ccfe-4b0c-9076-1a3a082a0c25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8048be3c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#monitor-mode)

**Monitor Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FXzhw2sQY1FEK3lILAfn8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c83c4d4-d89d-4246-ab03-a9aa92d39408&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e17984f7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#monitor-zip-mode)

**Monitor-zip Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FRgxXcbcwXDld9HfYpnaJ%252Fbbmonitorzippp.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2edb67f2-a45e-4410-959b-ab95c044aac5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88f760bb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#monitor-stores-mode)

**Monitor-stores Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FlOTKrFIR64gycoR3SXxC%252Fbbmonitorstores.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07244859-c3c9-4962-a970-e01b6c3c7f43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4468a5aa&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#invite-mode)

**Invite Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F3uVsi95Tx3jqe50BD5rn%252Fbestbuyinvite.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddcb72ac3-8630-4aad-b308-c02776a7b49d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ca87335&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

Run only **one checkout task per SKU per Best Buy account per fulfillment method** (Shipping or Pickup). Monitor mode tasks have no limit.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#when-to-use-modes)

When to Use Modes

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#reset-mode-1)

**Reset Mode**

*   Resets the password for the Best Buy account tied to the selected profile.
    
*   Ideal when accounts lock or as part of pre-drop prep.
    
*   Requires **IMAP** to retrieve reset codes.
    
*   After reset, the new password can be viewed in Best Buy Sessions in Stellar.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#account-gen-mode-1)

**Account-Gen Mode**

*   Generates new Best Buy accounts directly in Stellar.
    
*   Sessions are created automatically for each generated account.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#shipping-mode-1)

**Shipping Mode**

*   Used when you want items shipped to your address.
    
*   Make sure the product supports **shipping** (some SKUs are pickup-only).
    
*   Your cook group can confirm fulfillment type.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#pickup-mode-1)

**Pickup Mode**

*   Used when you want in store pickup.
    
*   Works with **Pickup Radius** and/or **Store IDs** depending on monitor mode.
    
*   Only use for products that offer pickup.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#invite-mode-1)

**Invite Mode**

*   Used to request invites for limited stock, invite-only, high-demand items.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#monitor-mode-1)

**Monitor Mode**

*   Monitors products by SKU (no zip/store filters).
    
*   Pings checkout tasks with matching SKUs when stock appears.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#monitor-zip-mode-1)

**Monitor-zip Mode**

*   Monitors products based on a **zip code**.
    
*   Useful for region-based availability.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#monitor-stores-mode-1)

**Monitor-stores Mode**

*   Monitors products based on specific **Store IDs**.
    
*   Great for targeting specific physical locations.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#profile)

Profile

*   Choose a profile that has the **same email** as the Best Buy session you want to use.
    
*   If **Guest Mode** is enabled, it uses profile info without the account.
    
*   For account checkouts, the email must match **exactly (case sensitive)**.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#proxies)

**Proxies**

*   **ISPs** → best for monitoring/login
    
*   **Residentials** → best for checkout tasks
    
*   Combine as needed based on your setup.
    
    *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#skus)

**SKUs**

A SKU is a unique ID for a specific Best Buy item. You can find the SKU in the product page or from your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
.

You can only enter one SKU per task.

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fm8Pw4c8mahO17ROtww2l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd060bf9e-49c9-4133-a698-075184dc0a9f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eddd07a0&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#store-ids-monitor-stores-mode)

**Store IDs (Monitor-stores Mode)**

*   Used when monitoring for store-specific availability.
    
*   You can find Store IDs at: `https://stores.bestbuy.com/index.html` Click a state → click a store → note the store ID.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#delays)

**Delays**

*   General recommended delay: **~4500 ms**
    
*   Adjust based on proxies and site behavior; always test before big drops.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#quantity-qty)

**Quantity (QTY)**

*   Check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
     for recommended QTY per product.
    
*   Stellar does not auto adjust QTY if you exceed site limits.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#pickup-radius-pickup-fulfillment-only)

**Pickup Radius (Pickup Fulfillment Only)**

*   Used with **Pickup Mode**.
    
*   Represents the **max distance (miles)** from your profile’s shipping zip code.
    
*   Max: **250**
    
*   Blank = default **25 miles**
    
*   Only enter whole numbers (e.g., 50, 75).
    
*   Leave this blank when running **Shipping** fulfillment.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#imap-session)

**IMAP Session**

*   Choose which [IMAP](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#imap-highly-recommended)
     session to use for this task.
    
*   Needed for account verification, 2FA emails, password resets.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#guest-mode)

**Guest Mode**

*   Check this box for **guest checkout** (no Best Buy account).
    
*   Uses profile info only.
    
*   Uncheck to use an account based checkout via sessions.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#watch-task)

**Watch Task**

**Highly recommended for restocks.**

When enabled:

*   Checkout task (Shipping or Pickup) waits for Monitor task
    
*   Monitor task (with same SKU) detects restock
    
*   Monitor task pings the checkout task
    
*   Checkout task adds to cart and completes checkout
    

Behavior:

*   When started, checkout task shows: **“Waiting for Monitor Ping.”**
    
*   Monitor finds stock → checkout begins immediately
    

If you leave Watch Task unchecked:

*   Checkout task monitors and checks out on its own
    
*   Higher load and more requests from a single task
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#skip-prelogin)

**Skip Prelogin**

*   **Enabled** → Bot skips pre-login and waits directly for Monitor Ping.
    
    *   Useful when there is a known queue; avoids pre-login slowing things down.
        
    
*   **Disabled** → Bot logs into account when starting the task.
    
    *   Better for using stored payment methods or when no heavy queue is expected.
        
    

If a queue is active, enabling **Skip Prelogin** is recommended.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#rakuten-and-topcashback)

**Rakuten & TopCashback**

*   **Use Rakuten** → check after following [Rakuten guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-rakuten-cashback)
     to earn cashback.
    
*   **Use TopCashback** → check after following [TopCashback guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
     to earn cashback.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#delivery-options)

**Delivery Options**

*   **Later Delivery** → selects the latest delivery window.
    
*   **Fastest Delivery** → selects the soonest delivery option (may cost more).
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/bestbuy#common-errors-and-fixes)

**Common Errors and Fixes**

*   **Submitting Order:** `**orderAlreadySubmitted**`
    
    *   _Cause:_ Order already placed on this account or a different account using the same address
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Stop the task
            
        *   Run a different account **or** jig the address
            
        
    
*   **Submitting Email:** `**LOSERROR**`
    
    *   _Cause:_ Item is out of stock (OOS)
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Let the task run and wait for restock
            
        *   Or stop all tasks
            
        
    
*   **Submitting Shipping:** `**status 400**`
    
    *   _Cause:_ Item is out of stock (OOS)
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Let the task run and wait for restock
            
        *   Or stop all tasks
            
        
    
*   **Task: Site Does Not Have Session**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Profile email does not match the email used in BestBuy Sessions
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Double-check both emails match **exactly** (case-sensitive)
            
        
    
*   **Login Detected Proxy Ban**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Proxy is banned
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Switch to different proxies
            
        
    
*   **Fetch Akamai**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Tasks are fetching Akamai data
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Let the task continue
            
        *   May take up to ~2 minutes to pass
            
        
    
*   **Sending Recovery Option:** `**Status 400**`
    
    *   _Cause:_ IMAP issue
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Confirm IMAP is set up correctly in Stellar
            
        *   Ensure IMAP session shows **“Ready”** (green)
            
        *   Delete and recreate the email app password if needed
            
        *   Optionally forward all account emails to the IMAP email
            
        
    
*   **Waiting for Code – Setting Up**
    
    *   _Cause:_ IMAP issue
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Verify IMAP setup in Stellar
            
        *   Confirm IMAP session shows **“Ready”**
            
        *   Recreate app password if necessary
            
        *   Forward account emails to IMAP if needed
            
        
    
*   **Cart Reserve Selected Store Unavailable**
    
    *   _Cause:_ Product is not available in your area
        
    *   _Solution:_
        
        *   Let tasks run briefly
            
        *   Or restart tasks

# SportChek CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2F9%2F92%2FSportChek_logo.svg%2F1200px-SportChek_logo.svg.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b44c0ba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/sportchek-ca#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on SportChek CA, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your profile, account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/sportchek-ca#how-do-i-generate-atc-shape-cookies)

How Do I Generate ATC (Shape) Cookies?

These cookies are required for Sportchek checkout

Use the [Shape module](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/shape)
 and let it run

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/sportchek-ca#sportcheckca-task-overview)

SportCheckCA Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/sportchek-ca#guest-mode)

**Guest Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FE4tuSwH7dbw8qmwvmfI7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D481c6a9b-f6f0-48aa-8742-1379e21102fd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d54216bf&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/sportchek-ca#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FrQKBWFN9sij6yH9NGv4z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5d703e00-de2a-45bf-94f8-8cd8adc5853d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c03668b6&sv=2)

*   What M**ode** do I use?
    
    *   Guest - Attempts to checkout normal Products
        
    *   Monitor - for now, only monitors release items.
        
    
*   What type of P**roxies** should I use?
    
    *   DCs and ISPs are the best due to speed. Residentials also work but may have high usage.
        
    
*   Where do I Find the Product **Variant**?
    
    *   Product **Variant** can be found in the product page, in the example above the product page is [https://www.sportchek.ca/en/pdp/asics-men-s-gel-excite-9-running-shoes-13967115f.333644411.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.sportchek.ca/en/pdp/asics-men-s-gel-excite-9-running-shoes-13967115f.333644411.html)
         Variant is `333644411`
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   A shorter Delay will result in proxy banns faster, whilst a shorter delay is idea for checking out hyped items. A safe delay to start off should be 5000
        
    
*   What **Qty** should I utilize?
    
    *   Qty should typically be 1, most in-hype item have a qty limit of 1
        
    
*   What Maximum Price should I use?
    
    *   Maximum Price is an optional field, this number will be used to check the unit price of the product before attempting to checkout.

[NextTargetGOchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/targetgo)

# PlayStation Direct | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fnh2wPfZWqcG3WVROgkcf%252FPlayStation-Logo-PNG-Photos.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D600c9fef-5541-407e-b833-b57a79f96132&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c33b9ce5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Playstation Direct, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Playstation accounts**
    

> This module requires an Playstation account. Before you start, double-check that your billing and shipping information lines up with the profile you’ll be using.

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct#add-sessions-and-login)

Add Sessions & Login

circle-exclamation

PS US = Your placed orders will use the data from your profile (address + card) PS EU = Your placed orders will use your address from your profile, payment method from the PlayStation account

1.  Go to Identities tab > Sessions > PlayStation > "Add Session"
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FVaQKEs2KgA75GFoVWpuh%252Fpssession.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D326bf2ab-1a14-4ca2-ac46-2b66a304a43b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f33676f6&sv=2)

1.  Name your session and enter your PlayStation account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FvHEwcFzMfdWdC5v8crGf%252Fpsaccountinfo.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9168c0b2-4195-4107-8595-b5da701daab0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eda9993e&sv=2)

1.  A unique Login Token is required for every PlayStation account. To make a login token you must follow the steps below
    
    *   For US: Link for US region [Stellar PS Direct US Login Token Extension V3arrow-up-right](https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/136nPcGwzFRLuLvtgaQyK1kVKf02QcQe9?usp=drive_link)
         go [here](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/arcteryx#queueit-browser-extension)
         for step by directions on how to download and use the Stellar AIO extension
        
        *   Non-US Regions: Install [EditThisCookie Extensionarrow-up-right](https://chromewebstore.google.com/detail/editthiscookie-v3/ojfebgpkimhlhcblbalbfjblapadhbol)
            
        
    *   Log into your PlayStation account
        
    *   Go to: [https://ca.account.sony.com/api/v1/ssocookiearrow-up-right](https://ca.account.sony.com/api/v1/ssocookie)
        
    *   Ignore the results on that webpage
        
    *   Open the EditThisCookie Extension
        
    *   Copy NPSSO Cookie found below
        
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FlcETco2ldOd8psVmqm1t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e64cbeb-816c-4db7-acdf-ec296f625297&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=325ffc64&sv=2)
    
    *   Paste the cookie into the Login Token field in your session
        
    

circle-exclamation

**DO NOT SIGN OUT OF YOUR PLAYSTATION ACCOUNT**

You can just close the tab/window and open a new incoginto window or new Chrome user. If you sign out of your account, your login token will no longer be valid

To use this extension in Incognito windows, go to Manage Extension > Details > Allow in Incognito

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FKwpVYN7klG0qwk8pZzWV%252Fee.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc357b81-82c9-46d1-822e-9089aadc4bd6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b22f788&sv=2)

Your Login Token can last up to 2 months and will change if you make any changes to your account such as changing your name, address, etc.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct#h_53f185929e)

**Mass Import Sessions**

You can also mass import sessions, this comes in handy when having a bulk number of accounts.

Click "Mass Import Sessions" and follow the format in the text box

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FEMU9RqMRQRunQWenF1Sf%252Fmassimport.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c84c00b-7389-4318-ba01-70f2a354da9c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=107def19&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct#logging-into-psd-accounts-help)

Logging Into PSD Accounts Help

In an attempt to assist people who are having trouble logging into their Playstation Direct US accounts, we have created a video below

*   Make a new chrome profile. Have the latest version of Google Chrome downloaded. Use Localhost. DO NOT USE ANY PROXY SWITCHING EXTENSIONS.
    
*   Paste [https://ca.account.sony.com/api/v1/ssocookiearrow-up-right](https://ca.account.sony.com/api/v1/ssocookie)
     in the same tab/browser immediately after logging in.
    
*   Paste the token into Stellar Identities and try to test "Account" mode from that point.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FlxgI7AE3x0uMRVlJfh7G%252Fpsdirectnewmonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3db6166a-cd26-49d6-9c9e-1faed0ea6be7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c1fd248&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct#account-mode)

Account mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBiG5o8HF9HfO0cwPXKLU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c2df769-56a8-4d53-b2a3-22604383c75b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e79e0409&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

PS US = Your placed orders will use the data from your profile (address + card) PS EU = Your placed orders will use your address from your profile, payment method from the PlayStation account

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor your desired items. When an item restocks, your monitor mode tasks will ping your running watch tasks (account mode) tasks to atc and checkout
        
    *   **Account mode** is your normal account checkout mode
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and resis will both work
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **Product** **URL** and how do I get them?
    
    *   The URL is a link that identifies the item you would like to run. Ex. [https://direct.playstation.com/en-us/buy-games/horizon-forbidden-west-launch-edition-ps5arrow-up-right](https://direct.playstation.com/en-us/buy-games/horizon-forbidden-west-launch-edition-ps5)
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   Enter the product quantity you wish to checkout. A safe QTY to use is 1 but you can increase this
        
    
*   What do I select for **Session**?
    
    *   Select a [session](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct#add-sessions-and-login)
         (account) that you named from the Identities tab in bot you'd like to use for your task
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment between 4000 - 6000
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   **Watch tasks** and **non-watch tasks** are different
        
        *   **Non-watch tasks** will be monitoring the site, which means that it will be using proxies. When a product restocks, this same task will atc and checkout
            
        *   **Watch tasks** are "watching" your **Monitor Mode** tasks waiting for a product you're running for to restock. Your **watch tasks** will add to cart and checkout when its pinged from a **Monitor Mode** task

[NextPokemon Centerchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center)

# What is the Dashboard tab? | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdpQ7g9UQtgUA88p4O2QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae0f21bb-a3eb-40ed-898b-3fa1c8af8a98&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60fc2a11&sv=2)

**Dashboard Tab**

The Dashboard tab will keep track of all your checkouts, declines, and money spent all in one tab with a visual representation of money spent, items purchases, how many items purchased on sites, and more!

**What is the "Checkouts" box for?**

*   The checkouts box is to keep track of how many checkouts you've had while using StellarAIO. Keep in mind that some checkouts are unlogged on occasion.
    

**What is the "Declines" box for?**

*   The declines box is to keep track of how many declines you've had while using StellarAIO. Keep in mind that declines can happen due to invalid card information, inefficient funds, items going OOS, etc.
    

**What is the "Spent" box for?**

*   The Spent box keeps track of how much money you have spent while using StellarAIO. The bot will recover any checkouts and track how much you have spent.
    

**What is the "Product Orders" section?**

*   The Product Orders section will keep track of any purchases by showing the site where the item was purchased, a picture of the item, the name of the item, the price of the item, and the date it was purchased on.
    

**What is the "Sites Checkouts" section?**

*   The Sites Checkouts section will keep track of the purchases you've made on each site and will make a pie chart with each site you've had successful purchases on.
    

**What is the "Amount Spent" section?**

*   The Amount Spent section is a visual graph of the Spent box and will progressively increase each day you spend money.
    

[PreviousWarhammerchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/warhammer)
[NextWhat is the Tasks tab?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tasks-tab)

Last updated 5 months ago

# Nvidia | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FzocvIYeHGFMZjSiMlXSP%252F02-nvidia-logo-color-grn-500x200-4c25-p.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59f21cf0-a160-40b6-a37c-257db10b669d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7cd614d&sv=2)

Our NVIDIA module supports guest checkout and is designed to handle high demand GPU drops protected by Akamai and captcha challenges. NVIDIA releases are typically true first come first serve with extremely fast sellouts, making proxy quality, captcha solving and properly tuned delays critical for success. Stellar streamlines the checkout flow using profile based checkout, PID targeting and multiple captcha provider options to help secure GPUs during restocks and scheduled releases.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nvidia#quick-start-recommended-setup)

**Quick Start (Recommended Setup)**

_(For members who want a fast setup without reading everything)_

*   Create a checkout **Profile** with billing, shipping and a payment method
    
*   Use **high-quality ISP or Residential proxies**
    
*   Enter the correct **PID** provided by your cook group
    
*   Run **Monitor Mode tasks** and **Normal Mode** tasks (guest checkout)
    
*   Select a **Captcha Provider** (Bot, AYCD, CapSolver, or CapMonster)
    
*   Use delays **6000–9000 ms** for restocks and **3000–5000 ms** for releases
    
*   Set **QTY to 1** unless otherwise allowed
    
*   Before major drops, run a **test task** on an in-stock product
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nvidia#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on Nvidia, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   Test Task
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nvidia#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fv0er8KE3OaB2gtoiySwG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e257386-8cb7-4ca3-b552-9e1f31f7140c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a2054dcd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nvidia#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FomHV5dYRG8PUlJ4pZhEY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5305b89c-7b4b-4d87-b53e-7af72edf45dd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0c1420c&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is your normal checkout mode and will use guest checkout
        
    *   **Monitor mode** will check for stock availability and will ping your running normal mode watch tasks when that item is in stock
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs and residentials will both work
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **PID** and how do I get them?
    
    *   To get PID, you need to view source of HTML and search for data-pid and remove all commas.
        
        PID for this item: https://marketplace.nvidia.com/en-us/consumer/graphics-cards/nvidia-geforce-rtx-5090/ is `1149380`
        
        *   Your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
             should provide all PIDs as well
            
        
    
*   What is **QTY**?
    
    *   Enter the product quantity you wish to checkout. A safe QTY to use is 1 but you can increase this
        
    
*   What is **Max Price**?
    
    *   Enter the max price you're willing to pay for your item. This is the max price for 1 QTY even if you have QTY field as a greater number
        
    
*   Which **Captcha Provider** should I use?
    
    *   Captchas will need to be solved to checkout, you can select one captcha solving provider from the dropdown list
        
        *   [Botarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
             (Recommended if you want to solve captchas manually in bot)
            
        *   [AYCD](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
            
        *   [CapSolverarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capsolver)
             (Recommended if you want to use a 3rd party service to solve the captchas for you automatically)
            
        *   [CapMonsterarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Experiment between 6000 - 9000 for restocks
        
    *   Try 3000 - 5000 for releases
        
    *   Reset delay is between 5000 - 10000
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on your monitor mode tasks to monitor and ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box, your task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your normal mode task will monitor the product, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    

[PreviousNFL Shopchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/nfl-shop)
[NextOfficechevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/office)
