# What is the Tasks tab? | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FOOQmYUAP0yDwMKze32sm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb2f47c3-6252-4f82-928b-6da0e49a24b4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=109853cf&sv=2)

**Tasks Tab**

The Tasks tab will allow you to create tasks for the retail sites you choose from. These tasks will have specific modes for specific sites to help maximize the odds of purchasing sought-out items.

**What is "New Task Group"?**

*   The New Task Group button allows you to create and name task groups that will be site-specific. After creating a task group, you will be able to create tasks for the retail site you selected.
    

**What is the "Search Tasks" section?**

*   The Search Tasks feature can be used to look up certain SKUs, Profiles, Proxy List, and more to make editing, starting, stopping, deleting, and duplicating tasks much simpler.
    

**What is the "Create Task" button?**

*   The "Create Task" button will allow you to create tasks once you've made a task group. Once clicking the button, you will be prompted with selecting a Mode, Profile, Monitor Proxies, and Checkout Proxies. After selecting the mode you will be prompted to fill out more site-specific information.
    

**What is the "Start All" button?**

*   Once the Start All button is pressed, it will start all the tasks made in the task group to start up and start monitoring/checking out on the site.
    

**What is the "End All" button?**

*   Once the End All button is pressed, it will stop all tasks within that task group from doing any sort of monitoring or checking out.
    

**What is the "Edit All" button?**

*   Pressing the Edit All button will allow you to edit all the tasks within that task group. This will allow you to change the mode, proxies, SKU, delays, etc. to whatever you please.
    

**What is the "Clear All" button?**

*   Pressing the Clear All button will prompt you with a confirmation page that will allow you to delete ALL tasks within the designated task group. Only use this if you want a fresh start.
    

**What is the "Monitor" button?**

*   The Monitor button will open up a popup that will show restocks of the items that are being monitored on the serverside for both Amazon and Walmart.
    

**What is the "Import" button?**

*   The Import button will allow you to import any exported tasks for faster task creation.
    

**What is the "Export" button?**

*   The Export button will export all tasks within that task group into a file which can be used to Import into the bot once more for fast task creation.
    

[PreviousWhat is the Dashboard tab?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-dashboard-tab)
[NextHow do I create a Task Group?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tasks-tab/how-do-i-create-a-task-group)

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Overview of Buttons on a Task | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fc2TNGNmHeXYThJNlapuU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D831e41f1-7517-4c03-8bcc-75b91747a9bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc7ae9fe&sv=2)

*   What is the **Pause/Start Button**?
    
    *   By clicking this button, you will either start the task or stop the task.
        
    
*   What is the **Pencil Button**?
    
    *   By clicking this button, you will be allowed to edit a task's information such as delays, URL, SKU, Proxies, QTY, and more
        
    
*   What is the **Box Over Box Button**?
    
    *   By clicking this button, you will be duplicating the task and the task will contain the exact same information.
        
    
*   What is the **Sorted Lines Button**?
    
    *   By clicking this button, you will view task logs which will show any errors, carts, checking out, or more task logs to get more insight as to what your tasks are doing and how to fix errors.
        
    
*   What is the **Trashcan Button**?
    
    *   By clicking this button, you will be deleting the task and all the information in the task. Deleting a task is irreversible, so be careful when clicking this button.

# What is the Captchas tab? | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F0ta8l4rBosiqvB4qkIRj%252F3.0capharvester.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc021e263-88ed-45c6-9d7e-8a492068729a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f828fe8e&sv=2)

**Captchas Tab**

The Captchas tab will allow you to create captcha solvers which will allow you to sign into One-Click Gmails and solve captchas for sites that might require captchas such as Newegg, AMD, Walmart, GameStop, and Shopify.

**What is the "Add Captcha" button?**

*   The Add Captcha button will allow you to create more captcha solvers to use in case if you need more. One reason to create multiple captcha solvers is that you may have multiple One-Click Gmails you can use in these solvers. Another reason could be that you have multiple tasks that require captchas to be solved.
    

**What do we input in the "Enter Proxy" box?**

*   Technically, you can leave this box blank. Leaving the box blank will have the solvers use your localhost IP. Inputting a proxy is completely optional and not required in order to have functional captcha solvers.
    

**What does the box with the arrow popping out button do?**

*   Clicking this button will have the captcha solver pop up physically which will allow you to solve them. Click this button before running tasks so you don't miss any captchas.
    

**What does the YouTube box do?**

*   Clicking the YouTube box will allow you to sign in to your Google account in order to use it to solve captchas.
    

**What does the eraser button do?**

*   Clicking the eraser button will log you out of your Google account and clear any information from that captcha solver.
    

**What does the trash can button do?**

*   Clicking the trash can button will delete the captcha solver altogether.
    

**What does the floppy disk button do?**

*   The floppy disk button will save any information that was used on the captcha solver such as logging into your Gmail account, setting a proxy, or just clearing the information.
    

[PreviousIMAP Overviewchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/imap-overview)
[NextHow do I set up the Captcha Harvester?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)

# Scan UK | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fs3-eu-west-1.amazonaws.com%2Ftpd%2Flogos%2F46dc5b450000640005011f3d%2F0x0.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=477fa989&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scan-uk#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Scan UK, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scan-uk#atc-mode)

ATC mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FTowQTqpIM0mgzx2IBPE5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7cb77011-d479-407e-a528-0bfd21f217b6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d14a8345&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scan-uk#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FtoQYBvxnCWRpMdJXzylN%252Fscanmonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80d7742e-d56f-46c2-b608-192599bfe327&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67c25069&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scan-uk#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLjhVqImsXiY2HhLPwuFj%252Fscannormal.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc67c8619-67cf-4c3b-ade5-4118bfc91a2d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c79633a&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

Scan is known to be very harsh and can cancel orders if you go over the purchase limit. Adhere to the limit set, most likely 1 per person per profile. Use multiple profiles for the best amount of success, with different emails, cards etc.

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is your checkout task is to be used for normal checkout flow
        
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor and ping your Normal mode watch tasks when they detect the item you're monitoring is in stock
        
    *   **ATC mode** is used to only add item(s) to your cart, this is not full ACO mode. For fully automated checkout, you should be using Normal mode
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   You need to use high quality proxies, usually ISPs but can also use resis
        
        If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    
*   What is **SKU**?
    
    *   For example: https://www.scan.co.uk/products/palit-nvidia-geforce-rtx-5090-gamerock-32gb-gddr7-ray-tracing-graphics-card-21760-core-tbd-mhz-boost The link below is where you can find all the graphics cards; https://www.scan.co.uk/shop/computer-hardware/gpu-nvidia-gaming/all
        
    
*   What is **QTY**?
    
    *   The number of items you want in one order
        
    
*   What is **Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error
        
        You can start your delays around `3333` and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is **Monitoring Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product
        
        You can start your delays around `5000` and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is **Reset Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product again after it has detected the item is in stock
        
        You can start your delays around 5000 and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is the **Watch Task?** checkbox?
    
    *   The **Watch Task** option allows your checkout task (e.g., Normal mode) to work together with a **Monitor mode task**. Here's how it works:
        
        *   If you check this box, your **checkout task** will not monitor for restocks directly. Instead, it will wait for a **Monitor mode task** (with the same SKU) to detect a restock
            
            *   Once the Monitor task detects the restock, it will "ping" the checkout (with the same SKU) task to run. The checkout task will then add the item to your cart and proceed to checkout
                
            
        
        When using the **Watch Task** option:
        
        1.  Start your checkout task. It will display the message: **"Waiting for Monitor Ping."** This means it's ready and set up correctly
            
        2.  When the Monitor task detects a restock, it will automatically trigger the checkout task (with the same SKU) to run
            
        
        If you leave the **Watch Task** checkbox **unchecked**, the checkout task will act independently. It will monitor the SKU itself, add the item to your cart, and checkout directly
        
    

circle-exclamation

Using Watch Task is highly recommended for restocks because it allows the Monitor task to do the heavy lifting. This improves performance and helps avoid overloading the site.

[NextScheelschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels)

# How do I set up the Captcha Harvester? | Stellar

Many stores use “Captcha” which is a ‘test’ offered by Google that many retailers utilize to try and combat bots on their stores. This ‘test’ comes in the form of the “I’m not a robot” box you are likely familiar with, where a sequence of images is generally needed to be selected and submitted to continue.

Google gives “One Clicks” to accounts that they deem active/human, where this ‘test’ can be automatically solved – thus drastically increasing your checkout time if these are utilized, therefore it is important to have Gmails that are deemed active/human so that this can be used to your advantage.

**Note:** Captcha solvers use your Chrome Browser so you'll need Google Chrome installed

1.  Go to the **Captchas Tab** and click **Add Captcha**
    
2.  If you would like to use a specific proxy ip to solve captchas please enter the proxy ip in the **Enter Proxy** field
    
3.  Click on the **YouTube** button and **sign in** (you don't need to sign into YouTube for Pokemon Center)
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FTxGDhdPBfN5GxrYe0Z9c%252Fyoutube.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd16c96a0-83a1-47bf-8afe-5bc5293f13a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44a9db58&sv=2)
    
4.  After you successfully signed in, you can close YouTube window. You can solve all Captchas with just **one** Harvester, you don't need to have multiple harvesters open
    

if you can't sign into Gmail, you should delete and create a new harvester

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester#auto-click-and-auto-solve-toggles)

Auto Click and Auto Solve Toggles

*   **Auto Click** works for all modules and will auto click some of "checkbox" oneclick captchas
    
*   **Auto Solve Serverside** is only for [Pokemon Center](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center)
     and it means we'll solve captchas for you on our end using our resources. There's a limit of 3 of these enabled at the same time. Ideally you should use serverside option if you're running on a server. If you're on local pc you can use serverside but local ai is meant for those on a local pc with decent gpu and cpu.
    
*   **Auto Solve Local AI** is only for [Pokemon Center](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center)
     and it means we'll solve the captchas for you usng your resources primarily being your GPU and CPU on your computer. Use this option if you're on local pc and your computer has a decent gpu and cpu. If not, then you can use serverside.
    

We’ve added a **Local AI Solver** alongside our serverside solver to better handle heavy traffic when the Pokémon Center module unlocks. This helps offload server load and provides a smoother, more consistent captcha solving experience.

To use it, enable **Local AI** in the Captcha page. The model will download automatically and only needs to be installed once (or when updates are released). Installation may take a few minutes. Before a Pokémon Center drop, make sure the solver status shows **“Ready”** and use the **Test** button to confirm functionality off drop.

Performance depends on your hardware. A stronger GPU allows faster solves and supports more captcha harvesters. A minimum of **8GB VRAM is required**. CPU fallback is supported but is significantly slower and not recommended for high traffic drops.

For reference, **5 harvesters on an RTX 4060 (8GB VRAM)** solved captchas quickly and consistently. GPUs such as the **RTX 3060, 3070, and 4060** were all tested successfully.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester#proxy-field-inside-captcha-harvester)

Proxy Field Inside Captcha Harvester

You have an option to input a proxy in this Proxy field

For Captcha sites like Pokemon Center, your proxies in your task will have priority and be used instead of the proxy you input here in the captcha harvester

For ReCaptcha sites, your proxy in the captcha harvester will be used for captchas instead of your proxies in your tasks

[PreviousWhat is the Captchas tab?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab)
[NextWhat is the Tags tab?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tags-tab)

Last updated 24 days ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Auto Click and Auto Solve Toggles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester#auto-click-and-auto-solve-toggles)
    
*   [Proxy Field Inside Captcha Harvester](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester#proxy-field-inside-captcha-harvester)

# Warhammer | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FTYPTcQVfLMANVXXrmnXO%252F1MidhtTm_400x400.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa047e78-5b75-425d-842f-841fa8bb995d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=987bf15f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/warhammer#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Warhammer, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/warhammer#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/warhammer#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F3QZHca1tYFJTrveUI88W%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9e3e2d2-a47a-4ae6-b668-3fc2af6877ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80e96b8d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/warhammer#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXetp_J4vpX3fqZ9w4cqeZuR7PAIutu42E1_qikofSibzPU2ey5qWGABXqEQQsmdI373UU7DA-O6W66aoVUdjyXqwgK5l-F4IXKtyATrfiGBYWsd4atFphYTomuMtaMux_PvGqTxIg%3Fkey%3Dwklw-0LfEtwtxmhD8-J0C6g4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8183406&sv=2)

*   Which Mode do I use?
    
    *   Monitor mode will only monitor and ping your watch tasks when they detect the item you're monitoring is in stock
        
    *   Normal mode is your checkout task that is to be used for normal checkout flow. You can select a watch task, and this task will then sleep until the monitor picks up the item as being in stock.
        
    
*   What does Profile mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items. Warhammer uses guest checkout, so all information is pulled from the profile. Warhammer is also very relaxed about Jigging, so minor 3 letter jigs tend to work.
        
    
*   What type of Proxies should I use?
    
    *   You need to use high quality proxies, we recommend fast ISP’s. You can use these on both monitor and normal mode.
        
    
*   What is the Product URL?
    
    *   The URL will show on the website with queryID at the end, example below.
        
    *   [https://www.warhammer.com/en-GB/shop/gorbag-and-shagrat-2025?queryID=a79b6e7711f9da84899861dcdaeb3479arrow-up-right](https://www.warhammer.com/en-GB/shop/gorbag-and-shagrat-2025?queryID=a79b6e7711f9da84899861dcdaeb3479)
        
    *   This full URL isn’t needed in the bot, and you can remove the ? and everything after it, so the URL you’d run in the bot will be below. [https://www.warhammer.com/en-GB/shop/gorbag-and-shagrat-2025arrow-up-right](https://www.warhammer.com/en-GB/shop/gorbag-and-shagrat-2025)
        
    
*   What is QTY?
    
    *   The number of items you want in one order. Warhammer usually limits to 1 per order, unless stated otherwise on the product page.
        
    
*   What is Delay?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error
        
    *   You can start your delays around 2000 and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is Monitoring Delay?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product
        
    *   You can start your delays around 3500-4000 and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is Reset Delay?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product again after it has detected the item is in stock
        
    *   You can start your delays around 5000 and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    

Top tip for Warhammer:

Drops always take place at 9.55am on a saturday, for a drop you don’t need to run monitor mode, and instead can just run normal mode, starting 30-60 seconds before drop time.

Links can be found, in the New & Exclusive section of the website, under the category “Pre-Orders”

# What is the Tags tab? | Stellar

_Full Tags guide_ [_here_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tags-tab/tags)

**Tags Tab**

The new tagging system will allow you to create your own custom tags / select the default tags that are present

**What is the "Default" button?**

*   Stellar has default/premade tags created for all users to use. You can click on each tag group and scroll up and down to see the items in each group
    

**What is the "Custom" button?**

*   Clicking on the Custom button will allow you create your own tag groups. You can enter SKUs in the Manage Products area.

# What is a proxy? | Stellar

A proxy is a way to mask your own IP which can be used to run multiple tasks at once without having to worry about getting your localhost IP from getting banned. Multiple types of proxies can be used.

The best proxy type in terms of speed and discreetness are ISPs. ISPs are basically a mix of DC proxy speeds and Residential proxies hiddenness.

DC proxies tend to be super fast, but in return get banned easily due to the reason that they can get traced back to a corporation or data center that is associated with it.

Residential proxies are known to be the slowest of the bunch, but in return, these proxies are least likely to get banned as they are linked to a home address. It is recommended to use these proxies for sites that tend to ban proxies pretty easily. Since Residential proxies can be generated in mass, you will be able to create a huge pool of proxies that StellarAIO can rotate through in case of any proxy bans. Keep in mind that Residential proxies are only functional if you have enough data allocated. This data is like your cellular plan and how much data of service you get.

[PreviousWhat is the Proxies tab?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab)
[NextHow do I add proxies?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab/how-do-i-add-proxies)

# What is the Profiles tab? | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FitphQkrtQebxbX76evSD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5b8aa84-b3a9-401c-9648-f5c4d3928398&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6368040&sv=2)

**Profiles Tab**

The Profiles tab will allow you to create profiles to utilize with the bot to create tasks. These profiles will be used to bot the site you choose and use your information to have items shipped to your house and bought on your information.

**What is the "New Profile Group" button?**

*   The New Profile Group button will allow you to create a profile group that can contain multiple profiles inside. These profile groups with multiple profiles in them can be used to create multiple tasks at once.
    

**What is the "Add Profile" button?**

*   Clicking on the Add Profile button after creating a task group will allow you to create a profile with a profile name, email, phone number, shipping, billing, and card information.
    

**What is the "Import" button?**

*   Clicking on the Import button will prompt up a File Explorer tab which will allow you to select a file that can contain profiles. You can get these files by exporting directly from StellarAIO or using third-party software such as AYCD, Essentials, and more.
    

**What is the "Export" button?**

*   Clicking on the Export button will export any profiles inside the profile group into a file that can be used to import into StellarAIO.

[NextProfile Overviewchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/profile-overview)

# Tags | Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tags-tab/tags#what-are-tags)

What are Tags?

Tags let you monitor and/or checkouta group of products with one task instead of running multiple tasks with different SKUs. This makes it easier to track restocks and manage tasks more efficiently

Currently, **Tags are supported on Amazon** and **Target**

**How do I use Tags?**

1.  Create a Tag group
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBiNTjwZ8u9iNCUQVoS0m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3418fc61-793d-44f7-99f0-46e6f2aa987a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e96609ac&sv=2)

1.  Give this group a name and click on the **Manage SKUs** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FO4TpeIYtlP1iaKTehgzZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbdc752b9-6bac-4378-991b-02a0512aa123&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f19bb0c7&sv=2)

1.  Enter in the product SKUs line by line. If you want to enter a product name as well use this format `SKU;PRODUCTNAME`
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F8ef9IccxUHrS6P0KkHqe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfdc385db-124f-4e9e-b1bc-fb1ef2c59f0e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e96a8a29&sv=2)

1.  You can now select the Tag group in task creation
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FUiIzWgoRmegLnLptgply%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75ecc4a8-c89b-4410-bd02-268b792846ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfe9dbb1&sv=2)

StellarAIO is one of the most powerful and user-friendly retail-focused automation tools available in 2025. Whether you're a beginner looking to get your first successful checkout or an experienced reseller aiming to scale profits, StellarAIO was built with you in mind.

Our software helps users secure high-demand products for **retail prices**, giving you the opportunity to resell for profit across a wide range of markets including electronics, collectibles, trading cards, toys, household goods and more.

    *   Smart captcha handling

# BP Proxy Switcher | Stellar

[_What is BP Proxy Switcher?_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/bp-proxy-switcher#h_339be4183e)

[_Installation_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/bp-proxy-switcher#h_da60f54688)

[_Adding Proxies_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/bp-proxy-switcher#h_d9118bb4df)

[_Using BP Proxy Switcher_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/bp-proxy-switcher#h_b23ab919f4)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/bp-proxy-switcher#h_339be4183e)

**What is BP Proxy Switcher?**

BP proxy switcher is a google chrome extension which allows you to run google chrome windows on different proxies. This is helpful when dealing with different accounts or generating cookies/headers.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/bp-proxy-switcher#h_da60f54688)

**Installation**

1.  On Google Chrome, go to this [linkarrow-up-right](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/bp-proxy-switcher/bapeomcobggcdleohggighcjbeeglhbn?hl=en)
    
2.  Click the **Add to Chrome** button
    
3.  Click **Add Extension** in the pop up window
    
4.  You have successfully installed BP Proxy Switcher. If you want to use it now just click the **puzzle icon** in the top right of your Google Chrome browser
    
5.  Click **BP Proxy Switcher**
    
    1.  If you want to **bookmark** the extension (meaning have it visible on your Google Chrome Tool bar), click the **pin icon**
        
    
6.  Now **BP Proxy Switcher** is open
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/bp-proxy-switcher#h_d9118bb4df)

**Adding Proxies**

1.  Click the **puzzle icon** in the top right of your Google Chrome browser
    
2.  Click **BP Proxy Switcher**
    
3.  Click the **Edit** button
    
4.  **Copy and paste** your proxies into the **blank box** (1 per line)
    
5.  Click the **OK button** in bottom right of the extension
    
6.  Your proxies are now saved and can be used in your browser
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/bp-proxy-switcher#h_b23ab919f4)

**Using BP Proxy Switcher**

1.  Open a **Google Chrome** browser
    
2.  Click the **puzzle icon** in the top right of your Google Chrome browser
    
3.  Click **BP Proxy Switcher**
    
4.  Click the **Proxy Drop Down Window**
    
5.  Select the **proxy** you would like to use
    
6.  **Open the website** you would like to use an account or generate cookies/headers on
    

[PreviousWhat are the minimum system requirements?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/general-stellaraio-faq/what-are-the-minimum-system-requirements)
[NextWebSocket Integrationchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/developing-software-compatible-with-stellar/websocket-integration)

# Very UK | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FInOqVoF8G9OBD3kETXKA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D120971fb-b9cb-4b4d-9a47-b3ccd1af8712&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d854ccf&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/very-uk#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Very UK, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/very-uk#normal-task)

Normal Task

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FWRjofELwdZgA2HD1yj8n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ed3f781-8633-46a6-a594-ea417a0a690b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9004a6b3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/very-uk#monitor-task)

Monitor Task

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F1QrXVWIQYjoacAoRyTK1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6d3ba35-df8f-4ab0-8118-1a1f5c38441e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c76f884&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/very-uk#cart-task)

Cart Task

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYhhhP3v1y5ouCHaw46VF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd5d7aa1-20db-4837-bd01-daca9c5d0556&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39e73686&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is your checkout task is to be used for normal checkout flow
        
    *   **Monitor mode** will only monitor and ping your Normal mode watch tasks when they detect the item you're monitoring is in stock
        
    *   **Cart mode** is used to only add your item(s) to your cart, you'll need to manually checkout if you use this mode
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a Profile you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   You need to use high quality proxies, usually ISPs but can also use resis
        
        If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    
*   What is **SKU**?
    
    *   For example: `1600919386` You can find this at the end of the URL you are trying to run, for example; https://www.very.co.uk/pokemon-tcg-scarlet-amp-violet-35-151-booster-bundle/1600919386.prd
        
    
*   What is **QTY**?
    
    *   The number of items you want in one order
        
    
*   What is **Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will retry to checkout after it encounters an error
        
        You can start your delays around `3333` and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is **Monitoring Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product
        
        You can start your delays around `5000` and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is **Reset Delay**?
    
    *   The time in milliseconds the bot will monitor the product again after it has detected the item is in stock
        
        You can start your delays around 5000 and adjust accordingly due to proxy quality
        
    
*   What is **Session**?
    
    *   Session is account support, logging into the account before checking out so that you can ensure a fast checkout.
        
        *   In order to set up a session for Very, go to:
            
            *   Identities > Sessions > Very > Add Session
                
                *   Then you can add your sessions accordingly. For Very, you need to use your account number instead of your email. You can find this by logging in on the website and it is on the landing page. You also need to put the postcode that you signed up with
                    
                
            
        
    
*   What is the **Watch Task?** checkbox?
    
    *   The **Watch Task** option allows your checkout task (e.g., Normal mode) to work together with a **Monitor mode task**. Here's how it works:
        
        *   If you check this box, your **checkout task** will not monitor for restocks directly. Instead, it will wait for a **Monitor mode task** (with the same SKU) to detect a restock
            
            *   Once the Monitor task detects the restock, it will "ping" the checkout (with the same SKU) task to run. The checkout task will then add the item to your cart and proceed to checkout
                
            
        
        When using the **Watch Task** option:
        
        1.  Start your checkout task. It will display the message: **"Waiting for Monitor Ping."** This means it's ready and set up correctly
            
        2.  When the Monitor task detects a restock, it will automatically trigger the checkout task (with the same SKU) to run
            
        
        If you leave the **Watch Task** checkbox **unchecked**, the checkout task will act independently. It will monitor the SKU itself, add the item to your cart, and checkout directly
        
    

circle-exclamation

Using Watch Task is highly recommended for restocks because it allows the Monitor task to do the heavy lifting. This improves performance and helps avoid overloading the site.

*   What is **Use TopCashBack?** box?
    
    *   Follow the [TopCashBack guidearrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         to set it up and check this box to earn cashback on eligible purchases
        
    
*   What is the **Task Limit**?
    
    *   Currently at 200 but may change at any time

[NextWalmart CAchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/walmart-ca)

# Should I use DC, Residential, or ISP Proxies? | Stellar

*   **ISP Proxies**
    
    *   ISP Proxies are on a data center server supported by an ISP network circuit. This gives added advantages against bans on a large scale as the IPs appear as residential while producing speeds as fast as DC proxies. These proxies are the best type to use for the majority of the sites we support on StellarAIO
        
    
*   **DC Proxies**
    
    *   Datacenter proxies are meant to be fast but in return is very easily traced back to the corporation or datacenter associated with it. These proxies work best for sites that do not ban easily.
        
    
*   **Residential Proxies**
    
    *   Residential proxies are not meant to be super fast, but are meant to be the least likely to be banned. This might sound like a downside, but in return you are able to generate thousands of proxies at once to be able to cycle through any proxies that do get banned. Keep in mind that usage is based off of how much data you have purchased along with your plan of residential proxies.
        
    

**Summary**

*   It's recommended to have both ISPs and Residential proxies

# Profile Overview | Stellar

Profiles are essential for checking out on each site. It is recommended to run 1 profile per task and not to repeat information on the profiles. It's ideal to have multiple profiles all with unique information.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/profile-overview#h_2bb4370322)

**Profile**

*   **Profile Name:** Enter a name for this profile. This is the name that will be viewed during Task Creation.
    
*   **Email:** Enter the email you want to use for this specific profile.
    
*   **Phone Number:** Enter the phone number you want to use for the profile.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/profile-overview#h_6945fea54a)

Payment Details

*   **First Name:** Enter the First Name on the card.
    
*   **Last Name:** Enter the Last Name on the card.
    
*   **Card Number:** Enter the long number on the front of your credit/debit card.
    
*   **Card Type:** Select the card provider (Visa, MasterCard, American Express, Discover, Mastercard)
    
*   **MM/YY:** Enter the expiration date of your credit/debit card. (Ex. 03/25)
    
*   **CVV Code:** Enter the security code, which is usually three digits and found on the reverse side of your credit/debit card. For American Express, this is four digits and located on the front of the debit/credit card.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/profile-overview#h_0c607e5ac2)

Shipping Information/Billing Information

*   **First Name:** The First Name of the person to be shipped/billed to.
    
*   **Last Name:** The Last Name of the person to be shipped/billed to.
    
*   **Address Line 1:** The first address of where it will be shipped to.
    
*   **Address Line 2:** The seconds address of where it will be shipped to (Used for Apartments, Jigging, ETC)
    
*   **Country:** The Country the address is in.
    
*   **State:** The State the address is in.
    
*   **City:** The City the address is in.
    
*   **Postal Code:** The Postal/Zip Code the address is in.
    

There is **no** limit to the amount of profiles you can make.

[PreviousWhat is the Profiles tab?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab)
[NextHow do I add a Profile?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

# Sessions Overview | Stellar

Firstly navigate to the sessions tab of StellarAIO

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FEIuBatqAWwIllRntRhSo%252Fsessiontab.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1cf4af5-dd42-4d56-b1ab-19dbe6653fd2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c744db7&sv=2)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FkonSMYXg1bjRpb7yxTIR%252F3.0sessionstab.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc8796bf-cfdc-4d57-ad67-e763135196f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76590c88&sv=2)

1.  Each site has their own categories for sessions
    
2.  The "Add Session" option is used to add a new session for a certain site - Make sure to be in a site specific category before clicking add session
    
3.  Sessions last for certain times depending on the user. Sessions dont last for one set amount of time!
    
4.  Make sure to checkout each session's individual guide for more information on each
    
5.  When adding a session for any site click the "Add Session" button in the top right corner, name the session, and lastly press "Save"
    
6.  The pencil icon is used to edit the session, the middle icon (orange colored and kind of looks like two pages on top of each other) is used to clone or copy a session, and the trash can is used to delete a session
    

[PreviousWhat is the Identities tab?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab)
[NextHow do I add a session or mass import sessions?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/how-do-i-add-a-session-or-mass-import-sessions)

# What is the Identities tab? | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FRDbsJ1NxDXM83NQ1fzG2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8602a9bf-69c7-4e34-8b10-5fc25ea15f8a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32091cf8&sv=2)

**Identities Tab**

The Identities tab is an account login hub where you will be able to sign into your accounts in various ways in order to create tasks with ease.

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FxEhVA5UlevGqkxraLy7l%252Feditsessionn.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D67280370-d57d-4dce-b5dc-6a50ed95d128&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f27e8e04&sv=2)

This will allow you to sign in to your accounts by starting a checkout task and keep the cookies saved for future task creation use. These sessions should allow you to need to only sign in once and have infinite uses of the session.

**What is the IMAP section?**

*   The IMAP section will allow you to input your IMAP sessions and login for future task creation use. Check out the [IMAP guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/imap-overview)
    

[PreviousPurchase In-Bot Proxieschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab/purchase-in-bot-proxies)
[NextSessions Overviewchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/sessions-overview)

# How do I create a task? | Stellar

Disclaimer: This guide will be for regular tasks that do not require additional information. A more in-depth guide for site-specific tasks will be in their designated article!

1.  Create a task group by pressing on the green + sign and select your task group
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F9ueCAebsOo3gMgiOLAOE%252Ftaskgroups.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68112598-1982-4244-ad3e-62f6788bc0e2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc8b1099&sv=2)
    
2.  Click the "**Create Task**" button
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FuZi4utdoEMkWlIWul5kV%252Fcreatetaskbutton.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D53893ecd-9c57-41c5-88ee-4a0cf1b58748&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2b698da&sv=2)
    
3.  You will be prompted with the following popup
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FzhdoWlDvMwrlT4wlFihQ%252Fnewtask.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df42c94ed-6010-436c-a263-f0341f7d730e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35fb16c4&sv=2)
    
4.  Select a **Mode**
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FmJZ1hMsydV0dNOHgK4Rv%252Fnewmode.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a720f31-a2a4-4b4c-86e8-bebc2bdf564a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=774b8e4b&sv=2)
    
5.  Select a **Profile** or **Profile Group**
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FzIveDkShkpBDLY1TBHWj%252Fselectprofile.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2258d1c8-4fc7-4687-b79a-fc11b4b8736d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e3f4ac47&sv=2)
    
6.  Select a **Monitor** and **Checkout Proxy Groups** (Optional: Leave blank if you want to use Local Host)
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FOuhDu7SSnI4MeViG2N3Y%252Fselectproxygroup.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc63431b7-8dec-431a-832c-dcc5e743b94b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=803ab28b&sv=2)
    
7.  Proceed to fill out the rest of the information
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FCsBWb8e5VZualdTH119Y%252F3.0newtask.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1700f1d-e9ce-49a4-8de8-0de370b9a7d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a75aed8&sv=2)
    
8.  Click on "**Create**" to complete the task creation
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FjdG11NV9fJcStCkdlyLP%252Fcreatebutton.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e1f1b7d-86f7-43ee-a423-6742d49a2f19&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb4780e8&sv=2)
    
9.  You've completed creating a task
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FiQQiIPRyPCmFByTBTLCO%252Ftaskline.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4cb84c44-0555-4307-9601-30980c28f3ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8bd9a44&sv=2)

[NextOverview of Buttons on a Taskchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tasks-tab/overview-of-buttons-on-a-task)

# How do I run StellarAIO with logs? | Stellar

1.  Open command prompt app on your desktop
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FFtHVnvZJFALanTqpa33h%252Fcmdprompt.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8aae5f7c-051b-4afd-8e07-a9866a518d9c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=baa72080&sv=2)

1.  When opened drag the StellarAIO shortcut (desktop icon) onto the command prompt
    
2.  Press enter on the command prompt and now the bot will run with logs filling the command prompt

# Panini | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FS4XOwHyXRMnCrWfytfqt%252FPanini_group_logo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df27c3950-a09e-4605-8fd3-b0b22bd4e496&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=836b413a&sv=2)

[Adding Accounts](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#adding-accounts)

[Mass Import Accounts](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#mass-import-accounts)

[Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#task-overview)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#preliminary-checklist)

Preliminary Checklist

Before setting up tasks on DSG, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profilesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   High-quality **ISP** or **Residential** proxies are required.
>     
> *   Low-quality or flagged proxies will cause **Akamai-related errors.**
>     
> *   For reliable performance, consider using **Stella Proxies ISPs or Residentials.**
>     
>     *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>          for high quality ISP and Residential proxies.
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#adding-accounts)

Adding Accounts

To add your Panini accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Identities** tab > **Accounts** > Click on **Panini**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FuwiZtLgUfB62ev3oAEod%252Fpanaccounts.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c3354db-2176-42b4-b87f-1a0eeecb5de3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f38d309a&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Account** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FoCPHLeuNfAAWXn8nCCku%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da862da76-5168-4a0d-99fa-88af3ac23802&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22432606&sv=2)

1.  Enter your accounts email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSru4kjTjXtY8TEhnobeY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d029384-0dbd-43fa-85de-39cde4be8d27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=293bc556&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#mass-import-accounts)

Mass Import Accounts

If you have a lot of accounts and want to add them in Stellar quickly, you can mass import them using the steps below

1.  Go to the **Identities tab** in bot and click on **Panini**. Then click the **Mass Import Sessions** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FVao260FeHLrMFp1NUonP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff7845c0-4ddf-4214-a10b-76e55ebde6d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc488cb4&sv=2)

1.  Paste in your accounts following the format in the text box `Email;Password;` For example
    
    *   [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1231!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1232!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1233!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1234!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1235!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1236!; [\[email protected\]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
        ;testing1237!;
        
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FSxAk9o8tJKmnOpgKTqFx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9df03d5a-7603-43be-bddc-bca08f2f5502&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a1e4163&sv=2)

1.  Click **Save** and you're all set!
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#normal-mode)

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYxlPBmNa12jCvJ6YkVU7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a022190-37b5-4a4f-8642-ea5e3fdd175d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=33ca0ed5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#dutch-mode)

**Dutch Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FabRN9sRXTYTvLLovDLq0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc18a5c1e-1853-4164-b4cb-0b1b512000f8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=acb94b0e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/panini#mobile-mode)

**Mobile Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FrMZBuEmCdMhcSG2v74vn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dedcedfc2-382b-4513-a177-de221240807b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=316e13f2&sv=2)

*   What **mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is used for normal desktop checkout flow
        
    *   **Dutch mode** is used for Dutch Auction releases
        
    *   **Mobile mode** is used for mobile checkout flow which can perform better than Normal mode
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   **DCs** and **ISPs** are the best due to speed but residentials also work but might have a large data usage
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **URL** and how do I get them?
    
    *   The URL is a link that identifies the item you would like to run. (ex. [https://www.paniniamerica.net/puma-suede-classic-x-panini-authentic.htmlarrow-up-right](https://www.paniniamerica.net/puma-suede-classic-x-panini-authentic.html)
         , the URL would be the whole link)
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Any where between 3000 and 5000 is good for normal mode while for Dutch auction you can lower slightly
        
    
*   What is a good **QTY** to use?
    
    *   It's best to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
         for quantity recommendations as different products may have different purchase limits set by the site
        
        *   Stellar does not automatically adjust the quantity if you set a number higher than what's allowed
            
        
    
*   Which **Captcha Provider** should I use?
    
    *   Captchas will need to be solved to checkout, you can select one captcha solving provider from the dropdown list
        
        *   [Bot](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
             [AYCD](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
             [CapSolver](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capsolver)
             [CapMonster](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
            
        
    
*   What should my **Max Price** be?
    
    *   A max price is set to not purchase the item you want for resell price. For example, if you have an item which is $20 retail, the max price should be around $30
        
    
*   What should my **Min Price** be?
    
    *   Panini tends to have fake dummy products to confuse bots. These items are usually super cheap. It is recommended to use a Min price of 10 - 20 dollars less than the retail price of your item
        
    
*   What is **Account**?
    
    *   This option is to select the account you would like to checkout on. These accounts are entered through the accounts page of Stellar
        
    
*   What is **Preload?** and should I enable it?
    
    *   This is a preload shipping method. What this does is selects the shipping method before running the task which speeds up the checkout process. It is recommended to run tasks on both preload on non-preload
        
    
*   What is **Guest Mode?** box?
    
    *   Check this box if you want to use Guest checkout (no Panini account). Keep in mind Panini accounts are required for certain releases/products
        
    

[PreviousOffspringchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/offspring)
[NextPlayStation Directchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/playstation-direct)

# Purchase In-Bot Proxies | Stellar

In order to have the ability to purchase proxies, one must first create a Proxy Group.

All Proxies are fulfilled through our preferred proxy partner, [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FyR7vA3sx8nCmLIOyxmJn%252Finbotproxies.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db047834c-344e-47ff-9efc-47ad4f53dffa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6640b99&sv=2)

Select your respective Quantity and be taken to a Stripe Checkout Page.

After successfully checking out, your order will automatically be on the ISP Proxy Group Tab.

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FxE5tAOLoUEMA8t5f8p5x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafeda786-7e97-4373-b07c-e1407278ceee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d75f4a3&sv=2)

# How do I Mass Import & Export Profiles | Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-mass-import-and-export-profiles#h_d3a0cd31fd)

**Who do I export my profiles?**

1.  Locate the **Profiles** tab
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FqBvxwXkfmSZ4w3PqQUj8%252Fprofilestab.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4822fa1-5c13-4284-8fe5-0883f651bdc8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8540d861&sv=2)
    
2.  **Locate** the profile group that you would like to export profiles from and click **Export**
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FX7Wy4vXj4M7YA4ZOWWBm%252Fexportprofilegroup.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4485ab7-de10-4174-adc1-475644ec8aa1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e49a2077&sv=2)
    
3.  **Locate** where you want to export your profiles to and click "**Save**"
    
4.  Your profiles are now exported
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-mass-import-and-export-profiles#h_f440c09eac)

**How do I import my profiles?**

**Download Import CSV Template**

1.  Create a new profile group
    
2.  Click **Download CSV Template** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fjk2iEK0MBf2VWV24xjcA%252Fdownloadcsvtemp.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0f12f23-aa75-42d9-866e-b28aaf339ffd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=acf6f2da&sv=2)

1.  Open the CSV file with excel or google sheets
    
2.  Enter in your new profile information
    
3.  Save as CSV
    
4.  Click the **Import** button inside Stellar
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F8r2QYafFfSCJJJ2mXC1r%252Fimportprofiles.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcdd72a6e-26ae-493d-92d1-06c01cc6e4aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85b3ff26&sv=2)

1.  You have now imported your profiles
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F056C2MWrvIiGRq12rrnO%252Fnewprofilessavedinbot.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da058e3df-5dee-4ffb-88d4-580420da50fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cea2e806&sv=2)

# Resy | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdpVKRLZTgxuHeTTmVYu9%252Fimage%2520%289%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b37630e-61c2-46a0-9e9e-8743422427e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6169cfb6&sv=2)

[Adding Accounts](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#adding-accounts)

[Mass Import Accounts](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#mass-import-accounts)

[Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#task-overview)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Resy, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#adding-accounts)

Adding Accounts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add your Resy accounts to Stellar please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  In bot, navigate to **Identities** tab > **Accounts** > Click on **Resy**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FXBKloBwyiQYUmME0n0Ae%252Fresyaccounts.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc00e40fb-6652-4b82-876e-095eae13f7bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e672031&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Add Account** button and enter your account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F9mmUSlORk4E0zjn6gZkv%252Fresyaccountinfo.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0d88881-6091-4b22-9de6-2dbe273116b5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e20b60a0&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#mass-import-accounts)

Mass Import Accounts


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have a lot of accounts and want to add them using Mass Import feature, please follow the step by step instructions below

1.  Instead of clicking on **Add Account** button, click the **Mass Import Accounts** button
    
2.  Enter your account email and password in the format shown in the text box. In this case for Resy, the format must be email;password
    
    1.  Ex.
        
        *   `[[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;testing1231! [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;testing1232! [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;testing1233! [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;testing1234! [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;testing1235! [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;testing1236! [[email protected]](https://guides.stellaraio.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ;testing1237!`
            
        
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fk6HfzmnTabPXWkH54Kh4%252Fresymassimportaccounts.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd500f54f-c82c-45eb-bd60-def618402a3b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8122be7&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#task-overview)

Task Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FckmCT7JENXssXuMxXn5S%252Fresymonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D518c5ab6-8660-45a7-9afc-55889a86ca75&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c1385a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#reserve-mode)

Reserve mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FFYz0UTqyX1kWDxtHEgBC%252Freseyreserve.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad497ed5-11c2-4bf4-ab6e-17556e9b1fab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58cc1278&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** is used to monitor reservations available for specific venues and party size
        
    *   **Reserve mode** is used to book the reservation specific to the venue and party size you entered
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   **DCs** and **ISPs** are the best due to speed but residentials also work but might have a large data usage
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **Reservation URL** and how do I get it?
    
    *   The Reservation URL is a link that identifies the venue you would like to run. (ex. [https://resy.com/cities/new-york-ny/venues/carbonearrow-up-right](https://resy.com/cities/new-york-ny/venues/carbone)
         , the URL would be the whole link)
        
        *   These URLs are often provided from your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
            
        
    
*   What is **Party Size**?
    
    *   Enter the headcount of the party you'd like to book your venue for
        
    
*   What is **Delays** and what should I use?
    
    *   This is the time in ms your task will check for product availability
        
        *   Any where between 3000 and 5000 is good
            
        
    
*   What is **Reset** **Delays** and what should I use?
    
    *   This is the time in ms your task will restart after picking up product availability
        
        *   Any where around 5000 is good
            
        
    
*   What is **Account**?
    
    *   This option is to select the account you would like to checkout on. These accounts are entered through the [Accounts page](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy#adding-accounts)
         of Stellar
        
    
*   What is **Start Date**?
    
    *   Enter the earliest reservation date
        
    
*   What is **End Date**?
    
    *   Enter the latest reservation date
        
    
*   What is **Captcha Provider**?
    
    *   This site has captcha checkpoints, meaning captchas will need to be solved to progress to the next step of the checkout process. Select a way to solve these captchas
        
        1.  [Botarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
             option is if you want to solve the captchas manually in bot, These captchas will pop up and appear in a small window inside the bot
            
        2.  [Capsolverarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capsolver)
             option is a 3rd party captcha solving service that uses AI to automatically solve captchas for you, hands free. You need to create a free account and deposit as little as $5 to get started
            
        3.  [Capmonsterarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
             option is a 3rd party captcha solving service that uses AI to automatically solve captchas for you, hands free. You need to create a free account and deposit as little as $5 to get started
            
        
    
*   What is **Watch Task?** box?
    
    *   Using watch task will help your proxies encounter less proxy bans and less proxy errors overall. Using a watch task essentially means you want your task to rely on other sources to monitor, in this case your monitor mode task will ping the watch task when a restock has happened
        
        *   If you check this box (recommended) your running checkout task will wait for a monitor mode task to ping it then it'll proceed to add item to cart and checkout
            
        *   If this box is unchecked, your checkout task will monitor the sku, add to cart and checkout
            
        
    
*   What is **Presolve Captcha?** box?
    
    *   Check this box if you want to presolve captchas, keep in mind these tokens are valid for about 2 minutes
        
    

[PreviousQueueItchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queueit)
[NextSams Clubchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/sams-club)
