# What is Serverside monitoring? | Stellar

**Serverside Monitoring** has been reintroduced to Stellar, offering an additional layer of restock detection across supported sites like **Amazon, Walmart, Costco, Sam’s Club** and others.

This feature allows Stellar to detect restocks directly from our servers, reducing the chance of missing drops when your local monitor tasks are rate limited or throttled.

* * *

**How It Works**

*   **No Setup Needed** – Just make sure your bot is on the latest version. It will automatically listen for Stellar's serverside pings.
    
*   **Enhances Local Monitoring** – Serverside monitoring works _with_ your monitor tasks, not instead of them. Continue running **one monitor task per product** as usual.
    
*   **Use "Watch Tasks"** – Ensure your checkout tasks are set as Watch Tasks to take advantage of serverside triggers.
    
    *   Amazon checkout tasks are watch tasks by default
        
    

* * *

**Where to Check for Supported Products**

*   Since supported SKUs can change frequently, we do **not** list them in this guide. You can open a ticket in our Discord server to find out which SKUs are supported.
    

* * *

**Why It Matters**

*   **Faster Detection** – Receive instant pings from Stellar’s backend, helping you stay ahead during high traffic drops.
    
*   **More Reliable** – Minimizes missed restocks from local monitor rate limits or blocks.
    
*   **Optimized for Key Retailers** – Supported on major retail sites including **Amazon US, Walmart US & CA, Costco US & CA and Sam’s Club**.
    

* * *

**Request a Product**

If there’s a high demand item you'd like monitored via serverside, open a ticket, we’ll review and add it if eligible.

* * *

**Final Tips**

*   **Keep Running Local Monitor Tasks** – Serverside is an enhancement, not a replacement.
    
*   **Stay Updated** – Our supported sites and SKU lists are updated frequently behind the scenes.
    

This system helps ensure faster, more reliable restock detection while reducing your chances of missing drops.

# How to test my proxies? | Stellar

1.  Locate the proxy group you want to test
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FOjbbDjhpLLxkXbdTOBnK%252Fproxygroupnew.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69773d49-d5ce-454f-b490-9bdc9020f158&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59eb3a1c&sv=2)
    
2.  Select the site you want to test on, for the guide's purpose, I will be choosing Amazon.
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F74ViAhUMGYHYzxYvF1pS%252Ftestproxiesurl.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da571d6cb-d5ad-4f62-bb34-be174a4d4e81&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a56ac3a&sv=2)
    
3.  Click on "Test All" or the Play button to test individually
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fls8nYatDVALU4mDJvrAn%252Ftestproxies.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88118b96-95b8-4e51-96a4-f596c750a21f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd6d216e&sv=2)
    
4.  You will now be presented with your proxy speeds
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FJuwW6g0e5xTbVgmHZUkA%252Fspeed.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da03c79ef-587b-4c6a-8330-1f840e572eed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1917b56&sv=2)
    

[PreviousShould I use DC, Residential, or ISP Proxies?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab/should-i-use-dc-residential-or-isp-proxies)

# How do I delete slow or expired proxies? | Stellar

1.  Locate the proxies that might be either too slow or expired that you want to delete and click the **Trashcan Button** to delete
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fh78fgcZCtlJfTdXfsPa3%252Ftrashcanproxies.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2388f709-722c-4bf2-89f9-e1425333cd9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56b9c499&sv=2)

# What is the Proxies tab? | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fwr8MtYnSgLPtZrZPoeY4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e4488c2-c797-42ef-af0a-f6878eebdda0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c029c030&sv=2)

**Proxies Tab**

The Proxies tab will help you maintain your proxies in proxy groups which can be organized into specific proxy groups or can maintain all your proxies in a singular proxy group. You will be able to test speeds and check for any dead proxies to filter out.

**What is the "New Proxy Group" button?**

*   The New Proxy Group button will allow you to create a proxy group that you can name to have a more organized experience. These proxy groups will allow you to input as many proxies as you feel.
    

**What is the "Manage Proxies" button?**

*   After successfully creating a proxy group, this button will allow you to input proxies. After inputting proxies, you will be able to test or delete them whenever you feel.
    

**What is the "Select Site" dropdown menu?**

*   The Select Site dropdown menu will allow you to select one of four sites on which you can test your proxies. Amazon, Target, Walmart, and Google.
    

**What is the "Test All" button?**

*   After selecting a site you want to test one, pressing the Test All button will allow you to test all your proxies at once for a speed test. Note that testing all proxies at once may affect speeds and can possibly be inaccurate. Testing proxies one by one is recommended for more accurate speeds.
    

[PreviousHow Do I J1g My Profiles?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles)
[NextWhat is a proxy?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab/what-is-a-proxy)

Last updated 5 months ago

# QueueIt | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic.carahsoft.com%2Fconcrete%2Ffiles%2F3916%2F7026%2F6637%2Flogo_green.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d4e5f84&sv=2)

**Index**

[_Captcha Harvesters_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queueit#h_f5c264464a)

[_Browser Extension_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queueit#queueit-browser-extension)

[_QueueIt_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queueit#h_56a1ac81b8)

[_Some Common Errors and Fixes_](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queueit#if-youre-receiving-an-error-message-thats-not-on-this-common-errors-table-you-can-look-here-in-the-s)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queueit#h_f5c264464a)

**Captcha Harvesters**

If you select the browser distribution method you'll need to follow the [Captcha Harvesters guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
. This will ensure the Captcha Harvesters will show the browser when it opens. You should open as many harvesters as you want browsers to open. You'll also need to have the [browser path](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-get-my-browser-path)
 setup in your Settings tab in bot

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queueit#queueit-browser-extension)

QueueIt Browser Extension

In rare cases the link Stellar sends you in [webhook](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-to-set-up-discord-notifications)
 after you pass queue won't work because of the site you're trying to run. To counter this we have a browser extension that will send you another link once you pass queue. Follow the steps below to download and set up the extension

1.  **Download** Stellar-queue browser extension for Google Chrome: [Stellar AIO Chrome Extension V3arrow-up-right](https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/136nPcGwzFRLuLvtgaQyK1kVKf02QcQe9?usp=drive_link)
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAHRqmN8ivOO4vcejQx6C%252FSAIO%2520EXT%2520V3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee462893-1421-42c9-ab1e-b31c5e776cab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1764c6b4&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Extract All..."
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FU4ItmlMivPsAaw230rB8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df81ec76b-5f94-4d1e-b626-7e8f1bbab345&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cac4463d&sv=2)

1.  In Chrome, go to **Manage Extensions**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FwmnhUm6l2azV30AUEHhH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39919511-46fa-40fe-a588-31df0675eec4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3b8f875&sv=2)

1.  On the top right corner of the Manage Extensions page turn on **Developer Mode** and click **Load Unpacked**. Now select the Stellar AIO Chrome Extension folder that you extracted, it'll be located in Downloads
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FYh1VWAxvKbiCGcydttpw%252Fextensionfolder.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5464443f-2699-4242-a331-3e17f20f1143&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95661145&sv=2)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAfI7WVyETPILuwg0hteg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb850a36-51a1-4062-92d2-b4403ef074f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=879fb462&sv=2)

1.  Go back to Chrome, click on the puzzle piece on the top right corner. You can now **pin** the **Stellar-Queue-Extension** to your Chrome toolbar
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FzyBTBUjLQOZ25FDmSawm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b97299c-aa40-4681-b84f-b0d98b0bc8f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=793f9ad7&sv=2)

1.  When you pass queue, you will receive a second [webhook](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-to-set-up-discord-notifications)
     titled "New Extension Link" with a very long link below it. Copy the very long extension link and paste into the same browser you downloaded the browser extension on
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FBHeSNn398uTK1UQecmLw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98fb14a1-ecc6-408d-b2d4-c4bb97579b5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97930924&sv=2)

1.  The new extension link can only work if you have the browser extension downloaded and set up by following the instructions above
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queueit#h_56a1ac81b8)

**QueueIt**

**Normal Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F6JCIn5Za99ztp0NmOfKk%252Fqueueuitnormal.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da05bb893-f101-404c-aad9-6d89bd9472d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=321708ed&sv=2)

**Test Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FKmWUCGhF93OVTiWObkQQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ce35072-a689-46c4-8e8b-43d45d1d4e69&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbe0fd91&sv=2)

*   Which **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** is used for waiting and queue and passing it. Normal mode will allow your tasks to wait in QueueIt and results either be distributed via link or browser
        
    *   **Test mode** is used to make sure the bot is working on the queue and POW. This mode will test on the Footlocker staging site
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   You can use any type of proxies here, ISPs DCs and Resis. Resis may perform a little better but it's best to test the different types you have and see which work best for you
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **URL** and how do I get them?
    
    *   Copy the URL from the search bar into the URL section. An example URL should look like [https://direct-queue.playstation.com/?c=sonyied&e=urivyju6ha&ver=v3-javascript-3.6.3&cver=311&man=Assign%20Action%20SafetyNet-Prod%20&t=https%3A%2F%2Fdirect.playstation.com%2Fen-us%2F&kupver=akamai-1.0.2arrow-up-right](https://direct-queue.playstation.com/?c=sonyied&e=urivyju6ha&ver=v3-javascript-3.6.3&cver=311&man=Assign%20Action%20SafetyNet-Prod%20&t=https%3A%2F%2Fdirect.playstation.com%2Fen-us%2F&kupver=akamai-1.0.2)
        
    
*   Which **Captcha Provider** should I use?
    
    *   [Bot](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
         will use your Gmail attached to your captcha harvesters to solve captchas automatically, once your Gmail score drives down then you'll have to solve captchas manually
        
    *   [AYCD](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-integrate-aycd-into-stellaraio)
         will use their Autosolve feature to solve captchas
        
    *   [Capsolver](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capsolver)
         is a 3rd party captcha provider that automatically solves captchas for you using their UI
        
    *   [Capmonster](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-capmonster)
         is a 3rd party captcha provider that automatically solves captchas for you using their UI
        
    
*   What is **Pow Solve Type**?
    
    *   **GO** can handle a lot of tasks and very reliable
        
    
*   What is **Distribution Method**?
    
    *   **Browser** will automatically open a Chrome browser once it's your turn to purchase the item
        
    *   **Link** will send you your link on your [webhook](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-to-set-up-discord-notifications)
        
        ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdyjujoZQBOPGdbrYNBPp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97602a3c-d06e-4eca-b079-d17a03215312&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6e39d5&sv=2)
        
    

[PreviousQueueFairchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/queuefair)
[NextResychevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/resy)

# How do I add a Profile? | Stellar

1.  Navigate towards the **Profiles** tab
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FqBvxwXkfmSZ4w3PqQUj8%252Fprofilestab.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4822fa1-5c13-4284-8fe5-0883f651bdc8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8540d861&sv=2)
    
2.  Click on the "**New Profile Group**"
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FQyeUZDicFCd6sjrHc6qA%252Fprofilesplus.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D850ebc87-e2c3-4694-bb07-7520ba90e10c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b04daa57&sv=2)
    
3.  Enter a **Group Name** and click on "**Add**" after.
    
    1.  ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fdqg1hbnqSWW6MsKfjGos%252Fprofilegroupname.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bed035a-14eb-4c1c-863d-5a565cccafe7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0c1f122&sv=2)
        
    2.  Click **Add Profile** button
        
        ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLq7VrPz32yfBnAvWGVef%252Faddprofile.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df28050ed-a856-47f1-b5b4-a22311a2afd0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c503075&sv=2)
        
    
4.  You will now be prompted with a profile creation menu
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FtnGalMa1SmRtDiulDcWR%252F3.0profilestab.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee985b7b-2fa5-40e0-9de2-15585eeedb06&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6926ee4&sv=2)
    
    1.  What is Profile Name?
        
        1.  A profile name is what your profile will be called when creating tasks, this way you can distinguish profiles apart and their information
            
        
    2.  What is Email?
        
        1.  This is where you input your email. We support all sorts of emails including catchall emails, just make sure you can receive emails, or else you might miss out on purchases.
            
        
    3.  What is Phone Number?
        
        1.  This is where you input your phone number. Make sure when inputting your phone number that you don't add any extra information. Must be formatted in a number-only entry (ex. 8888888888). Please do **NOT** add any "-" or "( )" or else you might run into problems when trying to purchase items.
            
        
    4.  What is First Name?
        
        1.  This is where you input your first name.
            
        
    5.  What is Last Name?
        
        1.  This is where you input your last name.
            
        
    6.  What is Address Line 1?
        
        1.  This is where you input your address that includes the street number as well as the street name.
            
        
    7.  What is Address Line 2/ House Number?
        
        1.  This is optional to add in any apartment numbers, house numbers, etc. to provide an exact address. Keep in mind, if not needed, you can just leave this section blank.
            
        
    8.  What is Country?
        
        1.  This is where you select your country. Currently, we only support the United States and Canada.
            
        
    9.  What is State?
        
        1.  This is where you select the state you reside in, must be correct, or else you will have issues with purchasing items.
            
        
    10.  What is City?
        
        1.  This is where you input the city you reside in, must be a valid city, or else you will have issues with purchasing items.
            
        
    11.  What is Postal Code?
        
        1.  This is where you input your postal code aka zip code, this must be a valid postal/zip code or else you will have issues with purchasing items.
            
        
    12.  What is the "Use Shipping information as Billing information for checkout" button?
        
        1.  This button means that both your Billing and Shipping information is the same, so it will use the same information for both. Only use this button if both are the same. Please fill out the Billing Informations section if it's different than the Shipping Information.
            
        
    13.  What is Card Number?
        
        1.  This is where you input a valid card number to use to purchase items using the bot. Failure to input a valid card number will result in failures to purchase items. Must be formatted in a number-only entry (ex. 8888888888888888) or else you will have errors with some sites. Do **NOT** have any extra spaces when inputting your card number.
            
        
    14.  What is Card Type?
        
        1.  This is where you select which type of card you have. Currently, we only support Visa, Discover, MasterCard, and AMEX.
            
        
    15.  What is MM/YY?
        
        1.  This is where you input your card's expiration date. Keep in mind that you do not need to input the "/" manually, the bot will automatically add it, so only input numbers. (ex. 03/21)
            
        
    16.  What is CVV Code?
        
        1.  This can be located at the back of your card. Usually 3 to 4 numbers.
            
        
    
5.  After filling out all this information, click on the "**Save**" button to save your profile for use.
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FLWr1acJ5heJ6hB5L0tK8%252Fsave.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6dad200-c7b9-4b2c-b216-ec5ca049b437&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb380641&sv=2)
    
6.  If you filled out everything properly, you will have created a profile that you can use on the bot
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FAMhS4o7pThs7j8erTjIB%252Fprofiledone.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91e307d0-0b12-4937-8b8b-bfb2c74ae2cc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86c5e639&sv=2)
    

[PreviousProfile Overviewchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/profile-overview)
[NextHow do I Mass Import & Export Profileschevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-mass-import-and-export-profiles)

# Failed to activate license key? | Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/status-codes-and-troubleshooting/failed-to-activate-license-key#h_15bd9d1717)

**Why am I getting Failed to Activate License Key?**

**Please try each potential solutions below**

1.  Close Stellar, go to the [Stellar Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://whop.com/stellaraio)
    , reset your key and try again
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FdGIGXCmbBXronhnCMmtO%252Fnewwhoplocatekey.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da332486c-9985-4fcc-a1fe-539d20d81b8b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55f41671&sv=2)

1.  Make sure your clock is synced. To make the clock synced, go to "Adjust Date/Time" settings from the bottom right corner of the taskbar and sync the clock
    
2.  Insert the key and Authenticate
    

[PreviousHow do I run StellarAIO with logs?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/status-codes-and-troubleshooting/how-do-i-run-stellaraio-with-logs)

# How do I add proxies? | Stellar

1.  Locate the **Proxies** tab
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FDh6ASiilfDNAPAuqLYxM%252Fproxiestab.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8cb76f2b-2150-4e64-b90f-5e9b350e8c10&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2827bd01&sv=2)
    
2.  Click on the **Green + Sign**
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FGWMEvR1Gmz9VA6QPGQcr%252Fproxygroupplus.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Defcb67dc-6df6-42c2-a609-ef75d4ccb9c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a0c67328&sv=2)
    
3.  Name your new proxy group and click "**Add**"
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FjXBGfNlNQOIdJaqUjhzy%252Fnewproxygroup.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc892b719-eaff-4f51-a55e-d40999039a52&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f9ca659&sv=2)
    
4.  Click on "Manage Proxies"
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F1h8YPFK5VAyqid4NoutS%252Fmanageproxiesbutton.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbfd327e1-6c1d-47c1-a194-c11d8f732dae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91fd9a71&sv=2)
    
5.  Copy and paste your proxy list and press "**Save**"
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F4HI6ufC2sdIjh15JEVpC%252Fmanageproxies.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd8f5285-913e-4f14-b0d4-f45519632b96&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b4bc6c7&sv=2)
    
6.  You have now added proxies to your proxy group which can now use.
    
    ![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FOjbbDjhpLLxkXbdTOBnK%252Fproxygroupnew.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69773d49-d5ce-454f-b490-9bdc9020f158&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59eb3a1c&sv=2)
    

[PreviousWhat is a proxy?chevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab/what-is-a-proxy)
[NextShould I use DC, Residential, or ISP Proxies?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab/should-i-use-dc-residential-or-isp-proxies)

# Scheels | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FJb2xQG8HslEA3LtVdO2N%252FMountains_SCHEELS_decal_Revised-removebg-preview.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2b28cab-ec95-4c82-b36e-e2aa7963b3fd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32a089ce&sv=2)

Our **Scheels module** supports both monitoring and automated checkout using a true **first come, first serve (FCFS)** flow. Because restocks can sell out quickly, success on Scheels depends on fast monitoring, stable proxies, and proper monitor-to-checkout pairing.

Stellar supports **watch task workflows** and **multi-variant checkout** for size-based products, allowing users to efficiently target multiple sizes without creating extra checkout tasks. This module is best suited for **sports cards, footwear, apparel, and limited-release items** that restock without warning.

With the right setup, Scheels can be a consistent and reliable site for securing high-demand products.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#quick-start-recommended-setup)

Quick Start (Recommended Setup)

_(For members who want a fast setup without reading everything)_

1.  Create and save your **Profile** with correct billing, shipping, and payment information.
    
2.  Add **ISP proxies** for monitoring and **Residential proxies** for checkout under the Proxies tab.
    
3.  Create **Monitor Mode tasks** using the **base SKU** for each product you want to run.
    
4.  Create **Normal Mode (Checkout) tasks** for the same products and enable **Watch Task**.
    
5.  If the product has **size variants**, enter multiple variants **comma-separated** in the Checkout task.
    
    *   Use base SKU only for cards or non-sized items.
        
    
6.  Set delays between **4000–6000** and Reset Delay around **5000**.
    
7.  Start Monitor tasks first, then start Checkout tasks and confirm they show **“Waiting for Monitor”**.
    
8.  Before major restocks or releases, run a **test task on an in-stock item** to verify profiles, proxies, and delays.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Scheels, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#task-overview)

Task Overview

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#monitor-mode)

Monitor mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FhFULjvwHyVn46Bp75IlM%252Fsmonitor.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def49fa2d-5ea4-4436-bca3-7ff55d1b24a9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66407ec2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#normal-mode)

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FRWuax9kcAEbE6QdzVgEE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D246455d0-c074-4d7a-986c-2d53cc1c372a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=141aba41&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#what-mode-should-i-use)

What Mode Should I Use?

**Monitor Mode**

*   Monitor Mode only checks for product availability.
    
*   When an item restocks, your Monitor Mode tasks will **ping your running Watch Tasks (Normal Mode)** to add to cart and checkout.
    

**Normal Mode**

*   Normal Mode is your **checkout task**.
    
*   These tasks handle add to cart and checkout once triggered by a Monitor task (if Watch Task is enabled) or can monitor and checkout on their own if Watch Task is disabled.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#profile-selection)

Profile Selection

Select the **Profile** you want to use.

*   The billing, shipping, and payment information from this profile will be used during checkout.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#proxy-recommendations)

Proxy Recommendations

Both **ISP and Residential proxies** work well on Scheels.

*   ISPs are ideal for monitoring
    
*   Residentials are recommended for checkout
    

If you need reliable proxies, check out [**Stella Proxies**](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
 for high quality ISP and Residential options.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#finding-the-sku-important)

Finding the SKU (Important)

Scheels SKUs are found in the **Image URL**, not the Product URL.

Steps to find the SKU:

1.  Go to the product page
    
2.  Select the color (if applicable)
    
3.  Ensure the item is **one size only** (no size dropdown)
    
4.  Right-click the product image
    
5.  Click **Open image in new tab**
    
6.  Copy the SKU from the Image URL
    

Example:

*   Image URL: `https://scheels.scene7.com/is/image/Scheels/04160439437?wid=1000&hei=1000`
    
*   SKU: `04160439437`
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#multi-variant-support-checkout-tasks-only)

Multi-Variant Support (Checkout Tasks Only)

Scheels now supports **Multi-Variant input for Checkout Tasks** on products that have **size variants**.

How this works:

*   **Monitor Tasks**
    
    *   Always use the **base SKU**
        
    
*   **Checkout (Normal Mode) Tasks**
    
    *   You may input **multiple size variants**, separated by commas
        
    *   No need to create separate checkout tasks for each size
        
    

Important notes:

*   This is **only for size variants**
    
*   Variants must belong to **one product only**
    
*   You cannot mix variants from different products
    

Examples:

*   Shoes
    
    *   Monitor Task → Base SKU
        
    *   Checkout Task → Multiple size variants (comma-separated)
        
    
*   Cards / Non-Sized Items
    
    *   Monitor Task → Base SKU
        
    *   Checkout Task → Base SKU
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#max-price)

Max Price

**Monitor Mode**

*   Enter the **max price per single item**
    
*   Example:
    
    *   Item retails at $29 → Enter `35`
        
    

**Normal Mode**

*   Enter the **max total order price**, including quantity
    
*   Example:
    
    *   Monitor price: `35`
        
    *   Quantity: `10`
        
    *   Normal Mode Max Price: `350`
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#quantity-qty)

Quantity (QTY)

*   A safe default is **1**
    
*   Your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
     should provide you with exact QTY recommendations based on product
    
*   Increase quantity only if the site allows multiple units per order
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#delay-recommendations)

Delay Recommendations

*   Recommended delay range: **4000 – 6000**
    
*   Adjust based on proxy quality and site behavior
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#reset-delay)

Reset Delay

Reset Delay controls how long (in milliseconds) a Monitor task waits before restarting after detecting a restock.

*   Recommended value: **~5000**
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#watch-task-option)

Watch Task Option

**Watch Tasks**

*   Do not monitor the site themselves
    
*   Wait for Monitor Mode tasks to detect a restock
    
*   Once pinged, they immediately add to cart and checkout
    

**Non-Watch Tasks**

*   Monitor the site directly
    
*   Use proxies continuously
    
*   Add to cart and checkout on their own
    

Best practice:

*   Use **Monitor Mode + Normal Mode (Watch Task enabled)** for better performance and fewer proxy bans.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#cashback-options)

Cashback Options

**Use Rakuten**

*   Enable this box after completing the [Rakuten setup guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-rakuten-cashback)
     to earn cashback.
    

**Use TopCashBack**

*   Enable this box after completing the [TopCashBack setup guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
     to earn cashback.
    

[PreviousScan UKchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scan-uk)
[NextScotty Cameronchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scotty-cameron)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Quick Start (Recommended Setup)](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#quick-start-recommended-setup)
    
*   [Preliminary Checklist](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#preliminary-checklist)
    
*   [Task Overview](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#task-overview)
    
*   [Monitor mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#monitor-mode)
    
*   [Normal mode](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/scheels#normal-mode)

# Topps US & EU | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2F2%2F29%2FTopps_Logo.svg%2F432px-Topps_Logo.svg.png%3F20110712004616&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c77689f5&sv=2)

circle-info

This is for Topps US & EU which is Shopify. All information below is for Shopify module > Topps Site

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Topps US, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu#h_ebe5f62d74)

**Captcha Harvesters**

If the website you're trying to bot has Captchas, you'll need to have Captcha Harvesters setup. You can follow the Captcha Harvesters guide [herearrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
.

Make sure you're using a Gmail with a One Click status and has a good gmail score inside the Captcha Harvester. Once you've logged into your Gmail and saved the information, the Solvers will open automatically when necessary while running your tasks. You can also open the Captcha Harvester before starting any Shopify tasks.

Be prepared you'll have to solve at least one captcha per task as some Shopify sites may have multiple checkpoint captchas and sometimes checkout captchas.

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FgohvnWvjQJKI7QHqu2GJ%252Fwaiting%2520for%2520captcha.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4709aca-86d1-41b5-817f-412ab2749a78&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=733f722e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu#adding-accounts)

**Adding Accounts**

Add your Topps accounts to Stellar by following the steps below

1.  Go to **Identities** tab
    
2.  Go to **Accounts** folder
    
3.  Select **Shopify**
    
4.  Click the **Add Account** button
    
5.  Name is your preference
    
6.  Shopify Store is Topps US
    
7.  Enter your Topps account email and password
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FEuE6KmDqidXVqjMlIgdG%252Ftoppsusaccounts.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D130ce05a-aaac-41f4-b7a8-dadc4c661364&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aed56712&sv=2)

circle-info

For login, you need to manually input code from your email. A small window will automatically open inside the bot when you need to input the code you were emailed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu#task-strategy-and-timing)

Task Strategy & Timing

**How Many Monitor Tasks Should I Create?**

*   Run **1 Monitor task per SKU**.
    
*   You can run multiple Monitor tasks if you want redundancy, but it’s **not required** and usually unnecessary.
    
*   Monitor tasks are lightweight and can run 24/7.
    

**Recommended:** 1 Monitor task per SKU is sufficient for most users.

* * *

**How Many Checkout Tasks Per Account?**

*   **Strictly 1 checkout task per Topps account.**
    
*   Running more than one checkout task on the same account can cause:
    
    *   Account locks
        
    *   Checkout failures
        
    *   Login/session instability
        
    

**Rule:** 1 account = 1 checkout task (no exceptions).

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu#task-overview)

**Task Overview**

Normal mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F1yaz9IT8nkOZu1b9zt7a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48ad7a99-c64c-455b-acce-da241bb4d172&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2b105ce&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Normal mode** relies on you inputting the product URL and/or keywords. This mode is recommended for Topps
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   DCs and ISPs are the best for Shopify due to speed. Residentials also work but may have high usage
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is **Input**?
    
    *   You can enter the **Product URL,** **Keywords** or **Variants**
        
        *   **Product URL** is the entire URL you see at the top of the product page. For example [**https://www.topps.com/pages/topps-finest-x-men-97**arrow-up-right](https://www.topps.com/pages/topps-finest-x-men-97)
            
        *   **Keywords** are a way for the bot to pick up, checkout the item you would like an d are often provided from your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
            . Find the name of the product and make keywords off of that. The keyword format is +Positive,-Negative. For example **+Jordan,+High,+Retro,-Shirt,-Pants,-Socks,-Hat**
            
        *   **Variants** are another way to identify a product and are often provided from your [cookgrouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
            
        
    *   Multicart feature allows you to purchase multiple products from one site in the same order. This allows you to save on shipping costs. You can use this feature by clicking on the + sign to add a new product line or click the trash can icon to delete a product line
        
    
*   What are **keywords** and how do I enter them?
    
    *   **Use + and - keywords** to find product and use commas to separate words. No spaces
        
    *   Example is **+topps,+complete,+set,+baseball,-nhl**
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   Be careful with your delays, websites with any proxy protection will ban your proxies fast. Use a wide variety of delays between 4000-8000
        
        *   To edit delays without stopping the task you can use the mass edit button
            
        
    
*   What is **Size**?
    
    *   Select the **Size** of the product you're trying to checkout
        
        *   You can use a custom size by typing in what you want to use instead of selecting a drop-down option and press enter
            
            *   If there isn't a size for the product you can select `Random`
                
            
        
    
*   What is **Site**?
    
    *   Select the **Site** you're trying to bot from the dropdown options
        
        *   This should automatically fill in once you enter a Product URL in the Input field
            
        
    
*   What is **Product Quantity**?
    
    *   The amount of the product you are wanting to be in the cart at checkout
        
    
*   What is Captcha Provider?
    
    *   We recommend to solve captchas manually via [Bot](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu#h_ebe5f62d74)
        
    
*   What is **Account**?
    
    *   If you would like to checkout on an [account](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu#adding-accounts)
         you can select which account here. Leave this option blank for guest checkout
        
    
*   What is **Password**?
    
    *   Some Shopify sites enable a password page which requires a password to enter the site. If you are using StellarAIO on one of these sites, make sure to click this checkbox and enter the password
        
        *   This is not recommended for Topps US
            
        
    
*   What is **Discount Code**?
    
    *   If you would like to use a discount code during checkout, click this checkbox and input the discount code
        
    
*   What is **Wait for Checkpoint**? box?
    
    *   Only check this if you want your task to wait for a checkpoint when starting. This is not recommended for Topps US
        
    
*   What is **Price Check?** box?
    
    *   Only check this box if you want to add a price check prior to your purchase to filter down more on the product you intend to purchase. This will prevent purchasing products over a specific price
        
        *   After you check this box, a new field will appear, type in the field what the safe max price is for your product. If the product you want to purchase is $29.99 then you can enter `30` into this field
            
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/topps-us-and-eu#error-messages-and-fixes)

Error Messages and Fixes

Error: Getting Block Page Fix: This is proxy related, try different proxies

[PreviousTargetGOchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/targetgo)
[NextToys R Us CAchevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/toys-r-us-ca)

# Pokemon Center | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FsPXkIoYV3bfMVqldzhIo%252Fimages__1_-removebg-preview.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a1b5db9-869a-427e-a930-dee0d9164ba0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f36cdcf&sv=2)

Our Pokemon Center module supports **guest checkout** only, making it one of the simpler and more consistent modules in Stellar. It’s primarily used for Pokémon cards that often return to stock without notice.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#video-guide)

**Video Guide**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#preliminary-checklist)

**Preliminary Checklist**

Before setting up tasks on Pokemon Center, make sure you have everything below prepared:

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.
> 
> If your profiles are not properly set up, you may encounter payment decline errors. In most cases, these should be considered **profile declines**, not true card issues. Pokémon Center can reject a profile for several reasons, including mismatched billing information, address inconsistencies or previously flagged details. Ensuring your profile information is accurate and consistent greatly reduces the chance of these declines.

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Run on Local PC**
    

> It's recommended to be on your local PC for Pokemon Center instead of running on your server.

*   **Create Captcha Harvesters**
    

> Create at least two [captcha harvesters](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
>  in the Captchas tab, you don't need to sign into YouTube (Gmail) for Pokemon Center. It's not recommended to use a proxy in the captcha harvesters proxy field unless you're on a server.

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#supported-modes)

Supported Modes

**Guest Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FO24amxsEL9m02muI0BWY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75ce04b3-5e43-4b8d-9f95-11b3bf7f3c8c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab9dd61&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#when-to-use-each-mode)

When to Use Each Mode

*   **Guest Mode** → These tasks will wait in queue then ATC and checkout the product(s) you have inputted into your tasks
    
    *   It's recommended to create at least 5 - 20 tasks per profile
        
    *   There's usually a total task limit of 400-500 tasks running at the same time
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#profile-selection)

Profile Selection

Select the profile you want to use under the **Profiles** dropdown. Your billing and shipping info from that profile will be used automatically during checkout.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#proxy-setup)

Proxy Setup

For the best performance:

*   Use **ISP proxies** for some of your tasks.
    
*   Use **Residential proxies** for majority of your tasks.
    

If you need reliable proxies, check out [Stella Proxies](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/proxies)
 for high quality ISP and Residential options.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#region)

Region

Select the correct region If you choose the wrong region, you will not be able to checkout items.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#products-url-or-pid)

Products (URL or PID)

You can live edit this field while tasks are running but needs to be done before your task enters the ATC process

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#url)

URL

Find the specific product page. Example: [https://www.pokemoncenter.com/product/701-03742/dratini-sitting-cuties-plush-4-inarrow-up-right](https://www.pokemoncenter.com/product/701-03742/dratini-sitting-cuties-plush-4-in)

Multiple URLs should be separated by commas: `url1,url2,url3`

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#pid)

PID

The Product Identifier is inside the URL.

Example PID: **701-03742** (Including the dash is required.)

Multiple PIDs can be entered like this: `PID1,PID2,PID3`

circle-exclamation

You must enter random numbers (ex. 127817190) in this field so your tasks can enter queue. You then want to edit all of your tasks to the correct Product URL or PID thats restocking. Your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups#whats-a-cookgroup)
 should be providing you with this product information.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#coupon)

Coupon

Enter any promo or coupon code normally.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#delay)

Delay

You can live edit this field while tasks are running but needs to be done before your task enters the ATC process

Recommended delay: **10000** Stable for queue movement and cart attempts during heavy traffic.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#module-unlock-delay)

Module Unlock Delay

If you don't want your tasks to start immediately after our Pokemon Center module is unlocked, you can enter a delay here.

This is to help reduce your tasks of passing queue too fast/early.

If you want to use this option, it's recommended to enter anywhere between `30000` - `60000` (Ex. `40000`)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#quantity-qty)

Quantity (QTY)

You can live edit this field while tasks are running but needs to be done before your task enters the ATC process

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#recommended-qty)

Recommended QTY

You can use **99** on restocks but some items may reject high quantities or can lead to errors like incapsula block; **1–2** qty is much safer. It's always best to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
 for the products max qty to maximize your checkouts.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#minimum-cart-quantity)

Minimum Cart Quantity

You can live edit this field while tasks are running but needs to be done before your task enters the ATC process

Enter the minimum number of items you want to purchase. If your cart does not reach this number, the task will not submit checkout.

Minimum Cart Quantity ensures that Stellar will **only proceed to checkout if your cart reaches the number of items you specify**, regardless of which SKUs were added. If the minimum isn’t met, the task will not check out.

**Example 1:** Minimum Cart is set to **3**. The bot carts **2 ETBs**. Because the total is **below 3**, the bot **will NOT checkout**.

**Example 2:** Minimum Cart is set to **1**. The bot carts **3 tins and 1 ETB**. Because the cart contains **at least 1 item**, the bot **WILL checkout**.

**Example 3:** You run **3 different SKUs**, each limited to quantity 1 at **$9.99**. SKU 1 adds, SKU 2 adds, SKU 3 is out of stock. Your cart total is **2 items**. With Minimum Cart set to **3**, the bot **will not checkout**, helping you avoid paying shipping on a small $19.98 order.

**Important:** Stellar will always attempt to **add all SKUs first** before checking whether the Minimum Cart requirement is met and proceeding to checkout.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#catchall)

Catchall

Enable this if you want Stellar to use your [Catchall](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/catchall-email-guide)
 email from the Settings tab.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#endless-mode)

Endless Mode

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#endless-mode-1)

Endless Mode

Enabled: After each successful checkout, task restarts automatically. Disabled: Task stops after one successful order.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#endless-limit)

Endless Limit

Enter how many successful orders you want before the task stops.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#skip-3ds)

Skip 3DS

**If you're in US or Canada, leave this option disabled**

Enabled: Bot attempts to bypass 3DS for faster checkout. This may increase payment declines depending on your bank. Disabled: Normal checkout flow. You may need to approve authentication manually if required.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#rotate-profiles-on-decline)

Rotate Profiles on Decline

It's recommended to use this feature as it will allow you to rotate your profile to another profile in your profile group in the case that Pokemon Center declines your payment / profile.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#captcha-provider)

Captcha Provider

Captchas appear in queue and at checkout. You can either use [Bot](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
 or [2captcha](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-2captcha)

Recommended setup:

*   **Only use** [**Bot**](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
    **, you have to solve captchas manually inside the captcha harvesters you created.** The captcha harvester windows will automatically open when it's time for you solve captchas
    
    *   It's recommended to enable the "Auto Click" option inside each captcha harvester
        
    
*   You could use [2captcha](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-2captcha)
     for some of your tasks but it's not reliable and could fail solving captchas
    

You do not need Youtube (Gmail) login but signing in can improve stability.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#auto-solve-captcha-feature)

**Auto-Solve Captcha Feature**

Stellar supports **auto-solving Captcha on Pokémon Center (PKC)** directly through our in-house solver.

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#auto-solve-options)

**Auto-Solve Options**

*   We recommend running a **mix of both (with and without Auto-Solve)** for best overall performance.
    
*   **Auto-click can safely be enabled on all harvesters.**
    

All auto-solved captchas are handled **serverside** meaning no additional setup or local resources are required.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#proxy-recommendations-for-pkc-captchas)

**Proxy Recommendations for PKC Captchas**

Through internal testing:

*   **Clean ISP proxies** performed best overall
    
*   **Residential proxies** also worked well in some cases
    
*   Pokémon Center has increased **proxy protection** especially against one-click captchas
    

Using clean, unburned proxies is critical for consistent captcha success.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#error-messages-and-fixes)

Error Messages & Fixes

*   **Module Disabled**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Normal behavior
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_
        
        *   Module is locked when no Pokémon Center queue is live
            
        *   Either the module isn’t unlocked yet **or** restart your task/bot
            
        
    
*   **Incapsula Block**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Usually a proxy issue
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_
        
        *   Try different proxies
            
        *   Use premium sticky residential proxies (Stella Premium Resis recommended)
            
        
    
*   **Captcha Pool Not Found**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ No captcha solver key saved
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_
        
        *   Enter a captcha solver key in **Stellar → Settings → Captchas**
            
        
    
*   **Full Data Dome Ban**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Proxies are banned
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_
        
        *   Try different proxies
            
        *   Use premium sticky residential proxies (Stella Premium Resis recommended)
            
        
    
*   **Payment Decline**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ Pokémon Center website / payment processing issue (usually profile-related)
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_
        
        *   Treat as a **profile decline**, not a card issue
            
        *   Ensure billing info matches exactly
            
        *   Check address consistency
            
        *   Avoid using previously flagged profile details
            
        *   Keep profile information accurate and consistent to reduce declines
            
        
    
*   **Getting Homepage**
    
    *   _Possible cause:_ If looping or stuck, it’s site-related
        
    *   _Suggested fix:_
        
        *   Let tasks run **or**
            
        *   Restart affected tasks
            
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/pokemon-center#summary)

Summary

Pokemon Center is one of the most stable and consistent retail modules in Stellar. With the right setup, solid proxies, good captcha solving and smart delays, users can consistently secure Pokémon cards.

# Walmart CA | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.corporate.walmart.com%2Fdims4%2FWMT%2F15870a4%2F2147483647%2Fstrip%2Ftrue%2Fcrop%2F1224x792%2B0%2B0%2Fresize%2F870x563%21%2Fquality%2F90%2F%3Furl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fcdn.corporate.walmart.com%252F0e%252F78%252F1c0917c94ce29c76e21e59934d25%252Flogo-walamrtspark-blue-transparent-background.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ee12f2d&sv=2)

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fw7qKsCBpVAEkGQD7wmx8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D779e9c2d-dc42-4bdd-a9f6-4f98f9f0fa82&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b57d57f&sv=2)

*   **CA Resis** are recommended for Walmart.ca, you do not need Canadian ISP proxies for Walmart.ca. Residential proxies may also be used (if absolutely needed) but watch the amount of data usage. Typically drops are known ahead of time to prevent proxy burns
    
*   **Checkout Proxies** will require **CA ISP** or **CA Residential** Proxies. Most users will use residential proxies as CA ISP's are harder to come by and a lot do not work on Walmart.ca.
    
*   The _Checkout Flow_ for Walmart.ca works differently than Walmart.com so the setup will be slightly different.
    
*   You have four tasks that can be created, a **Monitor Task** (monitor the SKU of interest), **Guest Task** (checkout task but accounts are required for hype drops), **Account task** and finally **Account Gen Task**.
    

You will be presented with only 1 mode to choose from when creating Walmart.ca tasks. This task will monitor and attempt to check out the item of interest if detected that it is in stock. The following will take you through how to setup the tasks.

*   **Profiles**
    

> Create and save your checkout [profiles](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-add-a-profile)
>  under the **Profiles tab** in Stellar. These contain your billing, shipping and payment info.

*   **Walmart Accounts**
    

> Accounts are required

*   **Proxies**
    

> *   **ISP proxies** – Recommended for some of your tasks
>     
> *   **Residential proxies** – Recommended for majority of your tasks
>     
>     *   Save both proxy groups under the **Proxies tab** in Stellar.
>         
>         *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
>              for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
>             
>         
>     

*   **Cook Group Access**
    

> Optional but recommended. Your [cook grouparrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
>  can help you find product URLs, SKUs and early restock alerts.

*   **Test Task**
    

> Before big drops, run a **test task** on a random in stock product to confirm your account, proxies and delays are functioning correctly.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/walmart-ca#monitor-mode)

Monitor Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FOO4jP0gLyc1hQb47dIJA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4951554e-89ed-40cb-9928-5628d818b435&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58e6cbf8&sv=2)

Use Bulk CSV List – This feature allows you to input multiple skus at once to monitor. Monitor Type – Different ways the bot can monitor. Run both API & ATC during drop time. Use App – If you want to use the Walmart CA App to monitor.

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/walmart-ca#guest-mode)

Guest Mode

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F6tD4cq2LLuWKT8CfNZcs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d06e3ce-1dd1-4b74-8f0b-91c0ac239205&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=de351486&sv=2)

This is used to checkout products using guest checkout. Note: All hype drops require a Walmart account so you'll need to use Account mode

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/walmart-ca#account-mode)

**Account Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fu8FRynOMHVDD4Rbr8xpo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ea7d48a-fa3f-4775-9a90-6a45b8a148d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eac28c8d&sv=2)

This is used to checkout products using your Walmart account

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/walmart-ca#account-gen-mode)

**Account Gen Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FcFcmngMWWFLBmYlkuNZI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1e28630-61d5-46a4-9e58-ab1925b57d8d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7554760&sv=2)

This is used to create Walmart CA accounts using the email in your profile

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/walmart-ca#set-defaults-mode)

**Set Defaults Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F9xma3ZoVFTOHfnCjiVDO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0167f31-0ab3-4c60-ac02-ff2386481a5a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdaa2d0c&sv=2)

This is used to set default information in your Walmart account from your profile you select

**Mode**: Account _**(YOUR CHECKOUT TASK!)**_

*   This Checkout "mode" available for Walmart CA called "Account"; It will use your Account to check the item out on Walmart.ca. **!!** _**Payment methods saved to the account is not used, instead it uses the profiles you have created within Stellar.**_ **!!**
    
*   You also want to use **Monitor mode** to check for product availability. Your monitor task(s) will trigger your running Account mode watch tasks to ATC and checkout. It's recommended to use monitor mode + account mode tasks with watch task enabled
    
*   _**Profile**_
    
    *   Select a profile that you have created in Stellar. This is where you use your hard cards (main credit card brands), or your virtual credit cards or VCC's, with your shipping and billing information.
        
    
*   _**Checkout Proxy**_
    
    *   If you have CA ISP's that work with Walmart, you can use them here. Otherwise, generate Canadian Residential (Resi) proxies. The quality of the canadian residential proxies **DO** matter, you may not be able to get passed the PX if your proxies are not good.
        
    
*   _**Input List**_
    
    *   You can input SKU or [Tag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-tags-tab/tags)
        
    
*   _**Delay**_
    
    *   Any delay between 3000 and 5000 is good, lower if you have a large pool of proxies. During drops this can be lowered. Drop times will be provided by your CG.
        
    
*   _**QTY**_
    
    *   The best QTY to use is 1, but if the item you're running for allows for more QTY per cart, feel free to increase the QTY.
        
    
*   _**Session**_
    
    *   Bot automatically matches profile email to account email - you can leave session blank
        
    
*   _**Fulfillment Type**_
    
    *   Select Shipping or Pickup
        
    
*   _**Postal Code**_
    
    *   Center of radius
        
    
*   _**Pickup Radius**_
    
    *   Distance in KM of pickup radius from postal code, for shipping to input 0
        
    
*   _**Buy Now ATC**_
    
    *   Need to be run on 50% of tasks
        
    
*   _**Use App**_
    
    *   Need to be run on 50% of tasks
        
    
*   _**Endless Mode**_
    
    *   Repeats checkout attempts after success
        
    
*   _**Endless Limit**_
    
    *   Max number of checkouts per task
        
    
*   _**Watch Task (Highly Reccomended)**_
    
    *   Checkout task waits for Monitor task to ping
        
    *   Easier on proxies
        
    *   Faster response time
        
    *   Lower risk of Target throttling
        
    
*   _**Use TopCashBack**_
    
    *   Follow the [TCB guide](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-do-i-set-up-topcashback)
         if you choose to use this option
        
    

[PreviousVery UKchevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/very-uk)
[NextWalmart GO (US)chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/walmart-go-us)
