# How Do I J1g My Profiles? | Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles#whats-j1gging)

What's j1gging?

J1gging allows you to create many profiles from an actual default profile. Shipping information, billing information, and payment information are all included in a profile. A typical person has one or two profiles, but with j1gging, you can create hundreds. Having extra profiles enables you to scale up your setup, create more accounts on websites, increase your chances of hitting, and increase the product quantity

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles#what-youll-need-before-you-get-started-j1gging)

What you'll need before you get started j1gging

1.  Decide on how many profiles you want to create. Ex. 100
    
2.  "X" number of email addresses ready to be pasted into spreadsheet cells. You can buy, generate or hand make these email accounts, I personally recommend to buy bulk gmails or outlooks with email access
    
3.  Credit cards for the "x" number of profiles you want to make. If you want to make 100 profiles, you'll need 100 unique credit cards. You can use Virtual Credit Cards like Privacy, Slash, Revolut etc. to link a checking account with these VCC providers. You can also look into Credit Card VCCs like Amex, Capital One and Citi
    
4.  Patience. This process takes some time, I don't recommend doing this if you're in a rush
    

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles#step-by-step-instructions-to-j1g-using-spreadsheet)

Step By Step Instructions to J1g Using Spreadsheet

This spreadsheet is formatted to work with Stellars required format. This will not work for other bots

1.  Open this [Google Spreadsheetarrow-up-right](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1MdgQaixdZhkgaxlxaXbyNCeVf7OTS-8j92R2l7Hb5Js/copy)
     and Make a Copy
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FmQYauQZIZn5UftSGpcYv%252Fcopygooglespreadsheet.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d023d28-bd8e-4844-9956-d4bf0f787818&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a871717b&sv=2)

1.  **Please read the first tab "Instructions"**
    
2.  Move onto the second tab "New Profiles" and replace line B2 with your real actual information, this will be your default profile and the spreadsheet will j1g some of this info into the rows below
    
3.  Paste your list of emails into B3 through the rest of B column
    
4.  For cells C3 and below, these phone numbers will automatically be updated using the area code from the phone number in C2.
    
    *   Once you're satisfied with your phone number list, copy cells C3 and below and CTRL + SHFT + V to paste the values without the formula so the formula doesn't keep randomizing the phone numbers every time you make a spreadsheet change
        
    
5.  For D column, copy `=index('Random Names'!$A$2:$A,RANDBETWEEN(1,counta('Random Names'!$A$2:$A)))` and paste into D3 and drag sequence down
    
6.  For E Column is much more personal preference but I like to leave my last name the same so if any delivery partners give me issues I can show them last name matches
    
7.  For G Column, copy `=J1gs!A2 & " " & $G$2` and paste into G3 and drag sequence down. This will use the 3 letter j1g in front of your address
    
    *   To use 3 letter j1g in the middle of your address, copy `=left($G$2, Find(" ", $G$2)) & " " & J1gs!A12 & " " & MID($G$2, FIND(" ", $G$2) + 1, LEN($G$2))` and paste anywhere into G3 and drag sequence down
        
    
8.  For Columns I to T, most cells should auto populate from the formulas in the spreadsheet
    
9.  Very last step and the most tedious step is to enter in your payment information in Columns U to Z
    
    *   You can use Virtual Credit Cards like Privacy, Slash, Revolut etc. to link a checking account with these VCC providers. You can also look into Credit Card VCCs like Amex, Capital One and Citi. Keep in mind some VCC providers merchant lock the card if its first use, for example if you use a privacy vcc to purchase something from Target you cant use that same vcc for Adidas
        
    
10.  Once you're satisfied with your new profiles it's time to **download "New Profiles" tab as CSV file**
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FGubxQRFY8HyXeQ1nFs8R%252Fnewdownloadascsvguide.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39fb0f6a-1f1c-45d7-b55a-6407b553fe85&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9bf0334&sv=2)

12\. Now that you have a CSV file with your new profiles, move to the next section below to begin importing your new profiles to Stellar

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles#download-csv-template-from-stellar)

Download CSV Template from Stellar

This is the second part of the process, once you're completed with the first spreadsheet its time to move the profiles you just made to this new CSV template to import them into Stellar

1.  In Stellar, go to Profiles tab > Open a new Profile Group > Click on Download CSV Template button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FXNjQIuDZqcikq1r1vO9x%252Fcsvtemplate.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd23ee5e5-36bb-425d-a2c7-431c03508124&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=448bdf6f&sv=2)

1.  This will download a file with the correct format of CSV to import the profiles to Stellar
    
2.  Open Google Sheets > Open new sheet > File > Import > Upload
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252Fkl2IJkSvnDA98yLXp4oF%252Fimportcsvtogooglesheets1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91ff5e41-84b6-4167-92bf-36496b49f22b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=836f0013&sv=2)

1.  Copy and Paste your profiles from spreadsheet #1 (j1g creator spreadsheet) to spreadsheet #2 (profile template)
    
2.  Save spreadsheet #2 (profile template)
    
3.  Open Stellar > Profiles tab > Create new Profile group > Import button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FUeMHpPa3CXtpQMhlskHp%252Fprofiletemplate.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd959eff8-229a-4ffd-9562-8f636065f535&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc21aaaa&sv=2)

1.  You can now view your new profiles in bot
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252F056C2MWrvIiGRq12rrnO%252Fnewprofilessavedinbot.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da058e3df-5dee-4ffb-88d4-580420da50fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cea2e806&sv=2)

With these new profiles you can now use Stellars account generator to create accounts using these profiles, use these profiles for guest checkout purchases and much more

[PreviousHow do I Mass Import & Export Profileschevron-left](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-mass-import-and-export-profiles)
[NextWhat is the Proxies tab?chevron-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-proxies-tab)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [What's j1gging?](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles#whats-j1gging)
    
*   [What you'll need before you get started j1gging](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles#what-youll-need-before-you-get-started-j1gging)
    
*   [Step By Step Instructions to J1g Using Spreadsheet](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles#step-by-step-instructions-to-j1g-using-spreadsheet)
    
*   [Download CSV Template from Stellar](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-profiles-tab/how-do-i-j1g-my-profiles#download-csv-template-from-stellar)

# Popmart | Stellar

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2F2%2F29%2FPop_Mart_logo.svg%2F2560px-Pop_Mart_logo.svg.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aee905ad&sv=2)

**What You'll Need First**

1.  **Proxies** Reliable ISP proxies to monitor products and residential proxies to checkout products are essential to avoid bans. Use proxies when creating tasks.
    
    1.  If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
         for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
        
    
2.  **Accounts (Optional)** Popmart supports account-based and guest checkout. For Account mode tasks, pre-created accounts or Stellar’s **account-gen mode** are needed.
    
3.  **IMAP (Optional)** Only required for account generation if you’re creating new accounts using Stellar.
    
4.  **PayPal (Optional)** Popmart supports PayPal checkout, this is solely optional. Select PayPal as your Payment Method in task creation setup and you'll be able to checkout via PayPal manually
    
5.  **SKUs** Obtain the product SKU(s) for the items you're targeting.
    
    1.  You can obtain SKUs and other product information from your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#accounts)

**Accounts**

If you're using Account mode tasks, you need to either pre-create accounts or generate them with Stellar's **Account-gen mode**

**Add Pre-Created Accounts to Stellar**

1.  Navigate to the **Identities** tab
    
2.  **Sessions** folder
    
3.  Select **Popmart**
    
4.  Click on **Add Session** button
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FGoog76kAPkdL7BpBsxU3%252Fpopmartsessions.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8db06043-88be-4e07-9242-b826c39c6b57&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34f61733&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#account-generation-steps)

**Account Generation Steps**

1.  **Mode**: Select `Account-gen` in Stellar’s task creation window.
    
2.  **IMAP Session**: (Optional) Link your email session using [IMAP credentials](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#imap-configuration)
    .
    
3.  **Proxies**: Use reliable proxies for account creation.
    
4.  **Delay**: Recommended setting is around `3500` to avoid rate limiting.
    
5.  **Start Time**: Optionally schedule the start time for generating accounts.
    

Refer to the **Account-gen mode** section below for a detailed overview.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#imap-configuration)

**IMAP Configuration**

IMAP access allows Stellar to handle email verification for account creation.

[IMAP Guide Overviewarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-identities-tab/imap-overview)

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#paypal-payment)

PayPal Payment

If you select PayPal as your payment method, you need to create a [Discord webhook](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-to-set-up-discord-notifications)
 then you'll receive a notification message with a PayPal purchase link. Click the link in the webhook and proceed to PayPal checkout manually

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#task-overview)

**Task Overview**

circle-exclamation

Reliable ISP proxies to monitor products and residential proxies to checkout products are essential to avoid bans. Use proxies when creating tasks.

1.  If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://help.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
     for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
    

####

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FbKW38Z9tCMDxpkWNddvI%252Fpopmart%2520account%2520gen.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D879be7d7-58ac-4e56-9e01-0efcb3bb6c56&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35dab1d9&sv=2)

**Monitor Popnow Mode**

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FecRIo2SH7SgzbBRb1GQi%252Fmonitor%2520popnow%2520mode.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22ef83cb-9389-4606-93b2-4bb7f85c9664&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9e3a6a2&sv=2)

*   What **Mode** do I use?
    
    *   **Monitor mode** continuously checks for product restocks and will ping your running checkout tasks in Waiting for Monitor status to attempt to ATC and checkout
        
        *   Using Monitor Mode tasks are recommended because they significantly improve speed and efficiency
            
        
    *   **Monitor Popnow mode** continuously checks for product restocks and will ping your running checkout tasks in Waiting for Monitor status to attempt to ATC and checkout
        
        *   Specifically designed to monitor Popnow exclusive drops, ensuring faster detection and better performance on high demand releases
            
        
    *   **Guest mode** is one of our checkout task options that will purchase products without requiring an account. Ideal for quick and simple purchases that don't require accounts
        
    *   **Account mode** is one of our checkout task options that will purchase products with requiring an account
        
    *   **Popnow mode** is one of our checkout task options that's specifically designed to purchase Popnow exclusive products
        
    *   **Account gen mode** creates new Popmart accounts to use for purchases. Useful for running multiple tasks while avoiding detection or purchase limits
        
    
*   What does **Profile** mean?
    
    *   Select a **Profile** you want to use and that profile information will be used when checking out items
        
    
*   What type of **Proxies** should I use?
    
    *   ISPs for monitoring and residentials for checkout tasks
        
        *   If you're looking for proxies, check out [Stella Proxiesarrow-up-right](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/stella-proxies)
             for high quality ISP and Residential proxies
            
        
    
*   What is the **SKU** and how do I get them?
    
    *   Enter the product's unique SKU
        
        *   You can retrieve SKUs from the retailers website or from your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
            
        
    
*   What is **Product Quantity**?
    
    *   Enter the how many units you'd like to purchase in one order (For Popmart Instore you need to run qty of `6` for Whole set so you just select Single and qty of `6`, for regular checkout tasks nothing changes.)
        
        *   We recommend to check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
             for quantity recommendations as different products have different max quantity limits
            
            *   Stellar does not automatically adjust the quantity if you set a number higher than what's allowed
                
            
        
    
*   What is **Store ID**?
    
    *   Enter the Store ID you'd like to pick up your orders from. See Store ID List below
        
        *   South Coast Plaza: `POSUS01` American Dream: `POSUS06` Westfield Valley Fair: `POSUS07` Century City: `POSUS08` Glendale Galleria: `POSUS10` Fashion Show: `POSUS11` Bellevue Square: `POSUS12` Westfield UTC: `POSUS15` Stonestown Galleria: `POSUS16` Stonebriar Centre POP UP: `POSUS17` Victoria Gardens POP UP: `POSUS18` First Colony Mall: `POSUS19` The Woodlands Mall: `POSUS20` Michigan Avenue POP UP: `POSUS22` Seattle Premium Outlets POP UP: `POSUS23` Willowbrook Mall: `POSUS24` Fashion Outlets Chicago: `POSUS25` Tangram POP UP: `POSUS26` Staten Island Mall: `POSUS27` Kenwood Towne Centre: `POSUS28` Southcenter: `POSUS29` Oakbrook Center: `POSUS30` SONO Collection: `POSUS31` Galleria Dallas: `POSUS32` World Trade Center: `POSUS33` Westfield Galleria at Roseville: `POSUS34` Westfield Culver City: `POSUS35` Northridge Fashion Center: `POSUS36` The Mall in Columbia POP UP: `POSUS37` Christiana Wein pop up: `POSUS38` Westfield Fashion Square: `POSUS39` Clackamas Town Center: `POSUS40` Fashion Place: `POSUS41` Towson Town Center: `POSUS42` Woodfield Mall: `POSUS43` Baybrook Mall: `POSUS44` Providence Place: `POSUS45` Miracle Mills Shops: `POSUS46` Downtown Summerlin: `POSUS47` Orland Square: `POSUS48` Stoneridge Shopping Center: `POSUS49` Alderwood Mall: `POSUS50`
            
        
    
*   What is **Size**?
    
    *   Select the size you'd like to purchase
        
        *   If unsure about the priduct size please check with your [cookgroup](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/getting-started-with-stellaraio/cook-groups)
            
        
    
*   What **Delays** should I use?
    
    *   **Monitoring Delay**: We recommend to use delays of 3000-6000 depending on the quality of your proxies
        
    *   **Reset Delay**: 5000 or less
        
    *   **Delay for checkout tasks**: 2000 or less
        
    
*   What is **Payment Method**?
    
    *   Select Credit Card or [PayPal](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#paypal-payment)
        
    
*   What is **TD Solver**?
    
    *   Select API or Browser
        
        *   API allows you to run more tasks compared to browser
            
        
    
*   What is **Session**?
    
    *   Select your [Session](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#accounts)
        
        *   You can leave this field empty and Stellar will auto match the profile to your account from the Identities tab. Make sure your email from your profile is exactly the same as the email from a session in the Identities tab
            
        
    
*   What is **IMAP Session**? (Only for Account Gen)
    
    *   Select your [IMAP Session](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#imap-configuration)
        
        *   You can leave this field empty and you'll need to manually enter in the account verification codes you'll receive via email. A window will open when its time for you to input the account verification codes, make sure you have at least one [captcha harvester](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-captchas-tab/how-do-i-set-up-the-captcha-harvester)
             set up
            
        
    
*   What is the **Watch Task?** checkbox?
    
    *   The **Watch Task** option allows your checkout task (e.g., Guest mode) to work together with a **Monitor mode task**. Here's how it works:
        
        *   If you check this box, your **checkout task** will not monitor for restocks directly. Instead, it will wait for a **Monitor mode task** (with the same SKU) to detect a restock
            
            *   Once the Monitor task detects the restock, it will "ping" the checkout (with the same SKU) task to run. The checkout task will then add the item to your cart and proceed to checkout
                
            
        
        When using the **Watch Task** option:
        
        1.  Start your checkout task. It will display the message: **"Waiting for Monitor Ping."** This means it's ready and set up correctly
            
        2.  When the Monitor task detects a restock, it will automatically trigger the checkout task (with the same SKU) to run
            
        
        If you leave the **Watch Task** checkbox **unchecked**, the checkout task will act independently. It will monitor the SKU itself, add the item to your cart, and checkout directly
        
    

circle-exclamation

Using Watch Task is highly recommended for restocks because it allows the Monitor task to do the heavy lifting. This improves performance and helps avoid overloading the site. We don't recommend to use Watch Task for rumored or confirmed releases.

*   What is **Override Address?** checkbox?
    
    *   Check this box if you want to override the address in your Popmart account
        
    
*   What is **Use App?** checkbox?
    
    *   Check this box if you want to use Popmart App for this task
        
    
*   What is **Send Cart Webhook?** checkbox?
    
    *   Sends you a [Discord webhook](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/navigating-stellaraio/what-is-the-settings-tab/how-to-set-up-discord-notifications)
         message when your task carts so you can try to manually checkout. This may spam your webhook channel and might be unstable. Keep in mind the 5 minute cart hold
        
    
*   What is **Stop Task After Carting?** checkbox?
    
    *   Stops the task once it carted, this lets you pay manually. This is sometimes more effective on certain accounts. Keep in mind the 5 minute cart hold
        
    

![](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1122101074-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-MQL0BOlyqRRf7zyNKSf%252Fuploads%252FUBmc7dfG9Ui5O8dnryvp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbabda18d-49bc-40f8-9edf-a6260f1bd694&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0cb2e46&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://guides.stellaraio.com/stellar/retailers/popmart#tips-for-success)

**Tips for Success**

*   **Proxies**: Always test proxies to ensure they're functional and not banned.
    
*   **Emails**: Use unique emails for account generation to prevent duplicate registrations.
    
*   **Delays**: Adjust delays depending on site traffic, lower delays for fast drops, higher for stability.
